9|34|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙisjore az olimonu oʙidon amvoli mardumro ʙa nohaq mexurand va digaronro az rohi Xudo ʙozmedorand. Va kasonero, ki zaru sim cam' mekunand va dar rohi Xudo xarcas namekunand, ʙa azoʙe dardovar xaʙar deh
9|35|ruze, ki dar otasi cahannam gudoxta savand va pesonivu pahlu va pustasonro ʙo on doƣ kunand. In ast on cize, ki ʙaroi xud cam' karda ʙuded. Holo ta'mi zaxirai xesro ʙicased
9|36|Sumori mohho dar nazdi Xudo, dar kitoʙi Xudo az on ruz, ki osmonhovu zaminro ʙijofarida, duvozdah ast. Cahor moh mohhoi haromand. In ast dini durust. Dar on mohho ʙar xestan sitam makuned. Va hamcunon, ki musrikon hamagi ʙa cangi sumo ʙarxostand, hamagi ʙa cangi onho ʙarxezed. Va ʙidoned, ki Xudo ʙo parhezgoron ast
9|37|Ba der partoftani mohhoi harom afzuni dar kufr ast va saʙaʙi gumrohii kofiron. Onho jak sol on mohro halol mesumurdand va jak sol harom, to ʙo on sumor, ki Xudo harom kardaast, muvofiq joʙand. Pas on ciro, ki Xudo harom karda, halol mesumorand. Kirdori nopisandason dar nazarason orosta gardida va Xudo kofironro hidojat namekunad
9|38|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙaroi ci cun ʙa sumo gujand, ki ʙaroi cang dar rohi Xudo cam' saved, gujo ʙa zamin mecasped? Ojo ʙa coi zindagii uxravi ʙa zindagii dunjo rozi sudaed? Mato'i in dunjo dar ʙaroʙari mato'i oxirat ƣajri andake hec nest
9|39|Agar ʙa cang cam' nasaved. Xudo sumoro ʙa sikancae dardnok azoʙ mekunad va qavmi digarero ʙa coi sumo intixoʙ kunad va ʙa Xudo niz zijone namerasoned, ki Xudo ʙar har kore tavonost
9|40|Agar sumo jorias nakuned, on goh, ki kofiron ʙerunas kardand, Xudo jorias kard. Jake az on du ʙa hangome, ki dar ƣor ʙudand, ʙa rafiqas meguft: «Anduhgin maʙos, Xudo ʙo most!» Xudo ʙa dilas oromis ʙaxsid va ʙo laskarhoe, ki sumo onro namedided, quvvatas dod. Va kalomi kofironro past gardonid, zero kalomi Xudo ʙolost va Xudo piruzmandu hakim ast
9|41|Ba cang ʙiraved, xoh ʙar sumo oson ʙosad, xoh dusvor va ʙo molu coni xes dar rohi Xudo cihod kuned. Agar ʙidoned, xajri sumo dar in ast
9|42|Agar mato'e dast joftani ʙuvad jo safare ʙuvad na candon daroz, az pai tu meomadand, vale aknun, ki roh daroz sudaast, pajmudanasro dusvor mehisoʙand. Va ʙa Xudo qasam mexurand, ki agar metavonistem, hamrohi sumo ʙerun meomadem. Inho tan ʙa halokat mesuporand. Xudo medonad, ki duruƣ megujand
9|43|Xudojat afv kunad, Caro ʙa onon ruxsati mondan dodi? Meʙoist onho, ki rost meguftand, oskor savand va tu duruƣgujonro ham ʙisnosi
9|44|Onon, ki ʙa Xudo va ruzi qijomat imon dorand, hargiz ʙaron cihod kardan ʙo molu conason az tu ruxsat namexohand va Xudo parhezgoronro mesinosad
9|45|Kasone, ki ʙa Xudo va ruzi qijomat imon nadorand va dilhojasonro sak faro giriftaast va in sak onhoro ʙa hajroni afkanda as, t, az tu ruxsat mexohand
9|46|Agar mexostand, ki ʙa cang ʙerun savand, ʙaroi xud asʙoʙi safar omoda karda ʙudand, vale Xudo safarʙar sudani ononro noxus dost va az cangason ʙozdost va ʙa onho gufta sud, ki hamrohi kasone, ki ʙojad dar xona ʙinisinand, dar xona ʙinisined
9|47|Agar ʙo sumo ʙa cang ʙerun omada ʙudand, cize cuz iztiroʙ ʙa sumo nameafzudand va to fitnaangezi kunand va ʙaroi dusmanon ʙa cosusi pardozand, dar mijoni sumo raxna mekardand va Xudo ʙa sitamkoron ogoh ast
9|48|Pes az in ham fitnagari mekardand va korhoro ʙaroi tu voƶguna cilva medodand to on goh, ki haq ƣoliʙ omad va farmoni Xudovand oskor sud, dar hole, ki az on nopisandi dostand
9|49|Ba'ze az onon megujand: «Maro ruxsat deh va ʙa gunoh majandoz». Ogoh ʙos, ki inho xud dar gunoh aftodaand va cahannam ʙar kofiron ihota dorad
9|50|Agar xajre ʙa tu rasad, anduhginason sozad va agar ʙa tu musiʙate rasad, megujand: «Mo corai kori xud pes az in andesidaem». On goh sodmon ʙozmegardand
9|51|Bigu: «Musiʙate cuz on ci Xudo ʙaroi mo muqarrar kardaast, ʙa mo naxohad rasid. U mavloi most va mu'minon ʙar Xudo tavakkal kunand»
9|52|Bigu: «Ojo cuz jake az on du neki intizori cizi digarero ʙaroi mo dored? Vale mo muntazirem, ki azoʙi Xudo jo az coniʙi U jo ʙa dasti mo ʙa sumo ʙirasad. Pas sumo muntazir ʙosed, mo niz ʙo sumo muntazir memonem»
9|53|Bigu: «Xudo az sumo namepazirad, ci az rui rizo xarc kuned, ci az rui norizoi, zero mardume nofarmon hasted»
9|54|Hec ciz mone'i qaʙuli xarchojason nasuda, ƣairi on ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon najovarand va ʙo ʙemajli ʙa namoz hozir mesavand va ʙa norizoi nafaqa mekunand
9|55|Doroivu farzandonason turo ʙa hajrat naandozad. Baroi onand, ki Xudo mexohad ʙa onho dar in dunjo azoʙason kunad va dar hole, ki hanuz kofirand, conason ʙarojad
9|56|Ba Xudo savgand mexurand, ki az sumojand va hol on ki az sumo nestand, inho az sumo ʙimnokand
9|57|Agar panohgoh jo ƣor jo nihongohe mejoftand, sitoʙon ʙa on co ruj meovardand
9|58|Ba'ze az onho turo dar taqsimi sadaqot ʙa zulm muttaham mekunand, agar ʙa onho ato kunand, xusnud mesavand va agar ato nakunand, xasm megirand
9|59|Ci mesavad, agar ʙa on ci Xudovu pajomʙaras ʙa onon ato mekunad, xusnud ʙosand va ʙigujand: «Xudo moro ʙas ast va Xudovu pajomʙaras moro az fazli xud ʙenasiʙ naxohand guzost va mo ʙa Xudo raƣʙat mekunem?»
9|60|Sadaqot ʙaroi faqiron astu miskinon va korguzoroni cam'ovarii on. Va niz ʙaroi ʙa dast ovardani dili muxolifon va ozod kardani ʙandagonu qarzdoron va xarc dar rohi Xudo va musofironi muhtoc va on farizaest az coniʙi Xudo. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
9|61|Ba'ze az onho pajomʙarro meozorandu megujand, ki u ʙa suxani har kas gus medihad. Bigu: «U ʙaroi sumo sunavandai suxani xajr ast. Ba Xudo imon dorad va mu'minonro ʙovar dorad va rahmatest ʙaroi onhoe, ki imon ovardaand. Va onon, ki rasuli Xudoro ʙijozorand, ʙa sikancae dardovar giriftor xohand sud
9|62|Dar ʙaroʙari sumo ʙa Xudo savgand mexurand, to xusnudaton sozand va hol on ki agar imon ovardaand, soistatar ast, ki Xudovu rasulasro xusnud sozand
9|63|Ojo namedonand, ki har kas, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras ziddijat mekunad, covidona dar otasi cahannam xohad ʙud va in rasvoii ʙuzurgest
9|64|Munofiqon metarsand, ki maʙod az osmon dar ʙorai onho surae nozil savad va az on ci dar dil pinhon kardaand ʙoxaʙarason sozad. Bigu: «Masxara kuned, ki Xudo on ciro, ki az on metarsed, oskor xohad soxt»
9|65|Agar az onho ʙipursi, ki ci mekarded? Megujand: «Mo ʙo ham xarf mezadem va ʙozi mekardem». Bigu: «Ojo Xudo va ojoti U va pajomʙarasro masxara mekarded?»
9|66|Uzr najovared. Pas az imon kofir sudaed. Agar az gunohi guruhe az sumo ʙiguzarem, guruhi digarro, ki gunahkor sudaand, azoʙ xohem kard
9|67|Mardoni munofiq va zanoni munofiq hama hamonandi jakdigarand. Ba korhoi zist farmon medihand va az korhoi nek man' mekunand va musti xudro az xarci dar roxi Xudo meʙandand. Xudoro faromus kardaand. Xudo niz esonro faromus kardaast, zero munofiqon nofarmononand
9|68|Xudo ʙa mardoni munofiqu zanoni munofiq va kofiron va'dai otasi cahannam dodaast. Dar on covidonaand. Hamin ʙarojason ʙas ast. La'nati Xudo ʙar onho ʙod va ʙa azoʙe pojdor giriftor xohand sud
9|69|Hamonandi kasone, ki pes az sumo ʙudand, ʙo nerui ʙestar va doroivu farzandonn ʙestar, Onho az nasiʙi xes ʙahramand sudand. Sumo niz az nasiʙi xes ʙahramand sudaed, hamcunon, ki kasone, ki pes az sumo ʙudaand, az nasiʙi xes ʙahramand suda ʙudand. Sumo suxanoni ʙotil gufted, hamcunon, ki onho suxani ʙotil meguftand. A'moli onon dar dunjovu oxirat nociz gardid va zijonmand sudand
9|70|Ojo xaʙari kasone, ki pes az onho ʙudaand, cun qavmi Nuh va Odu Samud va qavmi Iʙrohimu ashoʙi Madjanu Mu'tafikaro nasunidaand, ki pajomʙaronason ʙo nisonahoi oskor ʙar onho firistoda sudand? Xudo ʙa onho sitam namekard, onon xud ʙar xud sitam mekardand
9|71|Mardoni mu'min va zanoni mu'min dustoni jakdigarand. Ba neki farmon medihand va az nosoist ʙozmedorand va namoz meguzorand va zakot medihand va az Xudovu pajomʙaras farmonʙardori mekunand. Xudo inhoro rahmat xohad kard, Xudo piruzmandu hakim ast
9|72|Xudo ʙa mardoni mu'min va zanoni mu'min ʙihisthoero va'da dodaast, ki cujho dar on corist va ʙihistijon hamesa dar on cojand va niz xonahoe neku dar ʙihisti covid. Vale xusnudii Xudo az hama ʙuzurgtar ast, ki piruzii ʙuzurg xusnudii Xudovand ast
9|73|Ej pajomʙar, ʙo kofironu munofiqon ʙicang va ʙo onon ʙa siddat raftor kun, cojgohason cahannam ast, ki ʙad sarancomest
9|74|Ba Xudo savgand mexurand, ki naguftaand, vale kalimai kufrro ʙar zaʙon rondaand. Va pas az on ki islom ovarda ʙudand, kofir sudaand. Va qasdkori kardand, ammo ʙa on noil nasudand. Ajʙcuiason az on rust, ki Xudovu pajomʙaras az ƣanimatho ʙosarvatason kardand. Pas, agar tavʙa kunand, xajrason dar on ast va agar rujgardon savand. Xudo ʙa azoʙi dardnoke dar dunjovu oxirat azoʙason xohad kard va onhoro dar rui zamin na dustdore xohad ʙud va na madadkore
9|75|Ba'ze az onho ʙo Xudo pajmon ʙastand, ki agar az fazli xud mole nasiʙamon kunad, zakot medihem va dar zumrai solehon medaroem
9|76|Cun Xudo az fazli xud mole nasiʙason kard, ʙaxili kardand va ʙa rujgardoni ʙozgastand
9|77|Va az on pas to ruze, ki ʙo u muloqot kunand, ʙo on va'daxilofi ʙo Xudo va on duruƣho, ki meguftand, dilhojasonro coi nifoq soxt
9|78|Ojo namedonand, ki Xudo rozi dili onhoro medonad va az pic-pic kardanason ogoh ast? Zero Ust, ki donoi nihonhost
9|79|Xudovand ʙa masxara megirad kasonero, ki ʙar mu'minone, ki ʙa raƣʙat sadaqa medihand va ʙes az tavonoii xes cize namejoʙand, ajʙ megirand va masxaraason mekunand. Va onhoro azoʙe dardovar ast
9|80|Mexohi ʙarojason ʙaxsis ʙixoh mexohi ʙaxsis naxoh. Agar haftod ʙor ham ʙarojason ʙaxsis ʙixohi. Xudojason naxohad ʙaxsid, zero ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon nadorand va Xudo mardumi nofarmonro hidojat namekunad
9|81|Onon, ki dar xona nisastaand va az hamrohi ʙo rasuli Xudo aqiʙnisini kardand, xusholand. Cihod ʙo molu coni xesro dar rohi Xudo noxus sumurdandu guftand: «Dar havoi garm ʙa cang naraved!» Agar mefahmand, ʙigu: «Garmii otasi cahannam ʙestar ast!»
9|82|Ba cazoi a'mole, ki ancom dodaand, ʙojad, ki andak ʙixandand va farovon ʙigirjand
9|83|Agar Xudo turo az cang ʙozgardonid va ʙo guruhe az onho didor kardi va az tu xostand, ki ʙaroi cangi digar ʙerun ojand, ʙigu: «Sumo hargiz ʙo man ʙa cang ʙerun naxohed sud va hamrohi man ʙo hec dusmane naʙard naxohed kard, zero sumo az naxust ʙa nisastan dar xona xusnud ʙudaed. Pas aknun ham ʙo onon, ki az farmon xilofkori kardaand, dar xona ʙimoned!»
9|84|Cun ʙimirand, ʙar hec jak az onon namoz makun va ʙar qaʙrason maist. Inho ʙa Xudo va rasulas kofir sudaand va nofarmon murdaand
9|85|Amvolu avlodason ʙa hajr'atat najafkanad. Xudo mexohad ʙa saʙaʙi onho dar dunjo azoʙason kunad va dar ajni kufr con ʙisuporand
9|86|Cun surae nozil sud, ki ʙa Xudo imon ʙijovared va ʙo pajomʙaras ʙa cang ʙiraved, tavongaronason az tu ruxsat xostandu guftand: «Moro ʙigzor to ʙo onhoe, ki ʙojad dar xona nisinand, dar xona ʙinisinem!»
9|87|Ba on rozi sudaand, ki hamrohi xonanisinon ʙosand, ʙar dilhojason muhr nihoda suda va namefahmand
9|88|Vale pajomʙar va kasone, ki ʙo u imon ovardaand, ʙo molu coni xud dar rohi Xudo cihod kardand. Nekiho az oni onhost va onhojand, nacotjoftagon
9|89|Xudo ʙarojason ʙihisthoe, ki cujho dar on ravon ast va dar on co covidonand, omoda kardaast. In ast nacoti ʙuzurg
9|90|Guruhe az araʙhoi ʙodijanisin omadand va uzr ovardand, to onhoro ruxsat dihand, ki ʙa cang naravand va onhoe, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras duruƣ gufta ʙudand, dar xona nisastand. Ba zudi ʙa kofironason azoʙe dardovar xohad rasid
9|91|Bar notavononu ʙemoron va onon, ki mavodi cangii xes namejoʙand, har goh dar amal ʙaroi Xudovu pajomʙaras ixlos kunand, gunohe nest, agar ʙa cang najojand, ki ʙar nekukoron hec guna itoʙe nest va Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
9|92|Va niz ʙar onon, ki nazdi tu omadand, to markaʙ ʙaroi naʙardason dihi va tu gufti, ki markaʙe nadoram va onho ʙaroi xarc kardan hec najoftand va askrezonu ƣamgin ʙozgastand, gunohe nest
9|93|Xasmu azoʙi Xudo ʙar kasonest, ki dar ajni tavongari az tu ruxsat mexohand va ʙa on xusnudand, ki ʙo xonanisinon dar xona ʙimonand. Xudo dilhojasonro muhr ʙarnihoda ast, ki namedonand
9|94|Cun sumo ʙa nazdason ʙozgarded, meojandu uzr meovarand. Bigu: «Uzr majovared, guftoratonro ʙovar nadorem, ki Xudo moro az axʙori sumo ogoh kardaast. Ba zudi Xudovu pajomʙaras ʙa a'moli sumo xohand rasid. On goh sumoro nazdi on Xudovande, ki donoi nihonu oskor ast, meʙarand, to az naticai a'molaton ogohaton sozad!»
9|95|Cun ʙa nazdason ʙozgarded, ʙarojaton savgand Mexurand, to az xatojason darguzarsd. Az onho ruj gardoned, ki mardume palidand va ʙa xotiri a'molason coj dar cahannam dorand
9|96|Barojaton savgand mexurand, to az onon xusnud saved. Agar sumo ham xusnud saved, Xudo az in mardumi nofarmon xusnud naxohad sud
9|97|Araʙhoi ʙodijanisin kofirtaru munofiqtar az digaronand va ʙa ʙexaʙari az hukmhoe, ki Xudo ʙar pajomʙaras nozil kardaast, sazovortarand. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
9|98|Ba'ze az araʙhoi ʙodijanisin on ciro, ki xarc mekunand, cun zijone mepindorand va muntazirand, to ʙa sumo musiʙate ʙirasad. Musiʙati ʙad ʙar xudason ʙod va Xudo sunavovu donost
9|99|Va ʙa'ze az araʙhoi ʙodijanisin ʙa Xudovu ruzi qijomat imon dorand va on ciro, ki xarc mekunand, ʙaroi nazdik sudan ʙa Xudo va ʙa xotiri du'oi pajomʙar xarc mekukand. Bidoned, ki hamin saʙaʙi nazdikijason ʙa Xudo xohad sud va Xudo ʙa rahmati xes doxilason xohad kard, zero omurzandavu mehruʙon ast
9|100|Az on guruhi naxustin az muhociron va ahli Madina, ki peskadam sudand va onon, ki ʙa neki az pajason raftand, Xudo xusnud ast va onho niz az Xudo xusnudand. Barojason ʙihisthoe, ki dar onho naxrho corist va hamesa dar on co xohand ʙud, omoda kardaast. In ast komjoʙii ʙuzurg
9|101|Guruhe az araʙhoi ʙodijanisin, ki girdi sumoro giriftaand, munofiqand va guruhe az mardumi Madina niz dar nifoq isror mevarzand. Tu onhoro namesinosi, mo mesinosemason va du ʙor azoʙason xohem kard va ʙa azoʙi ʙuzurg giriftor mesavand
9|102|Va guruhe digar ʙa gunohi xud e'tirof kardand, ki a'moli nekuro ʙo korhoi zist omextaand. Sojad Xudo tavʙaasonro ʙipazirad, zero Xudo omurzandavu mehruʙon ast
9|103|Az doroihojason sadaqa ʙisiton, to ononro poku munazzah sozi va ʙarojason du'o kun, zero du'oi tu mojai oromisi onhost va Xudo sunavovu donost
9|104|Ojo hanuz nadonistaand, ki Xudost, ki tavʙai ʙandagonasro mepazirad va sadaqotro mesitonad va Xudost, ki tavʙapaziru mehruʙon ast
9|105|Bigu: «Amal kuned, Xudovu pajomʙaras az mu'minon a'moli sumoro xohand did va sumo ʙa nazdi donoi nihonu oskoro ʙozgardonida mesaved va U az amalhojaton ogohaton xohad kard»
9|106|Va guruhe digar ʙa masijjati (xosti) Xudovand voguzosta sudaand, ki jo azoʙason mekunad jo tavʙaasonro mepazirad. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
9|107|Xudo sohidi medihad: «Onhoe, ki mascide mesozand, to ʙa mu'minon zijon rasonand va mijonason kufru cudoi andozand va to ʙaroi kasone, ki mexohand ʙo Xudovu pajomʙaras cang kunand, kamingohe ʙosad, on goh savgand mexurand, ki moro qasde cuz nekukori naʙuda ast, duruƣ megujand»
9|108|Hargiz dar on mascid namoz maguzor. Mascide, ki az ruzi naxust ʙar parhezgori ʙunjod suda, soistatar ast, ki dar on co namoz kuni. Dar on co mardone hastand, ki dust dorand pokiza ʙosand, zero Xudo pokizagonro dust dorad
9|109|Ojo kase, ki ʙinoi mascidro ʙar tars az Xudo va xusnudii U nihoda, ʙehtar ast jo on kase, ki ʙinoi mascidro ʙar kanorai selgohe, ki oʙ zeri onro susta ʙosad, nihodaast, to ʙo u dar otasi cahannam sarnagun gardad? Va Xudo mardumi sitamgarro hidojat namekunad
9|110|On ʙino, ki ʙarovardaand, hamesa mojai tasvis dar dilason xohad ʙud, to on hangom, ki dilason pora-pora gardad. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
9|111|Xudo az mu'minon conhovu molhojasonro xarid, to ʙihist az onon ʙosad. Dar rohi Xudo cang mekunand, ci ʙikusand jo kusta savand, va'dae, ki Xudo dar Tavrotu Incil va Qur'on doda ast, ʙa haq ʙar uhdai Ust. Va ci kase ʙehtar az Xudo ʙa ahdi xud vafo xohad kard? Ba in xaridu furuxt, ki kardaed, sod ʙosed, ki komjoʙii ʙuzurgest
9|112|Tavʙakunandagonand, parastandagonand, sukrguzoronand, ruzadoronand, ruqu'kunandagonand, sacdakunandagonand, amrkunandagon ʙa ma'ruf va man'kunandagon az munkarand, va hofizoni hududi Xudojand! Va mu'minonro xusxaʙar deh
9|113|Naʙojad pajomʙar va kasone, ki imon ovardaand, ʙaroi musrikon, harcand az xesovandon ʙosand, pas az on ki donistand, ki ʙa cahannam meravand, talaʙi ʙaxsois kunand
9|114|Baxsois xostani Iʙrohim ʙaroi padaras naʙud, ƣajri xotiri va'dae, ki ʙa u doda ʙud. Va cun ʙaroi u oskor sud, ki padaras dusmani Xudost, az u ʙezori cust. Zero Iʙrohim ʙisjor xudojtarsu ʙurdʙor ʙud
9|115|Xudo qavmero, ki hidojat kardaast, gumroh namekunad, to ʙarojason ravsan kunad, ki az ci ciz ʙojad ʙiparhezand, ki Xudo ʙar har cize donost
9|116|Farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin az oni Xudost! Zinda mekunadu memironad va sumoro cuz Xudo dustdoru jovare nest
9|117|Xudo tavʙai pajomʙaru muhocirin va ansorro, ki dar on soati usrat hamrohi U ʙudand, az on pas, ki nazdik ʙud, ki guruhero dil az cang ʙigardad, paziruft. Tavʙaason paziruft, zero ʙa onho raufu (musfiqu) mehruʙon ast
9|118|Va niz Xudo paziruft tavʙai on se tanro, ki az cang xonanisini karda ʙudand, to on goh, ki zamin ʙo hamai kusodagijas ʙar onho tang sud va con dar tanason nameƣuncid va xud donistand, ki cuz Xudovand hec panohgohe, ki ʙa on ruj ovarand, nadorand. Pas Xudovand tavʙai onon paziruft, to ʙa U ʙozojand, ki tavʙapaziru mehruʙon ast
9|119|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙo rostgujon ʙosed
9|120|Ahli Madina va araʙhoi ʙodijanisini atrofi onro narasad, ki az hamrohi ʙo pajomʙari Xudo kafokasi namojand va naʙojad, ki az U ʙa xud (ja'ne az U guzasta ʙa hifzi coni xud ʙosand) pardozand. Zero dar rohi Xudo hec tasnagi ʙa onho cira nasavad jo ʙa ranc naaftand, jo ʙa gurusnagi ducor nagardand jo qadame, ki kofironro xasmgin sozad, ʙarnadorand, jo ʙa dusman dastʙurde nazanand, magar on ki amali solehe ʙarojason navista savad, ki Xudo podosi nekukoronro noʙud namesozad
9|121|Va hec mole — ci andaku ci ʙisjor — xarc nakunand va az hec vodie nagzarand, magar on ki ʙa hisoʙason navista savad, to Xudo podosason dihad, cun podosi nekutarin kore, ki mekardaand
9|122|Va natavonand mu'minon, ki hamagi ʙa safar ravand. Caro az har guruhe dastae ʙa safar naravand, to donisi dini xesro ʙijomuzand va cun ʙozgastand, mardumi xudro xusdor dihand, ʙosad, ki az zistkori hazar kunand
9|123|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙo kofirone, ki nazdiki sumojand, cang kuned, to dar sumo siddatu durusti joʙand va ʙidoned, ki Xudo ʙo parhezgoron ast
9|124|Va cun surae nozil savad, ʙa'ze mepursand: «In sura ʙa imoni kadom jak az sumo darafzud?» Onon, ki imon ovardaand, ʙa imonason afzuda savad va xud sodmoni mekunand
9|125|Ammo onon, ki dar dilhojason marazest, cuz inkore ʙar inkorason najafzud va hamcunon kofir ʙimurdand
9|126|Ojo nameʙinand, ki dar har sol jak jo du ʙor mavridi ozmois voqe' mesavand? Vale na tavʙa mekunand va na pand megirand
9|127|Va cun surae nozil savad, ʙa'ze ʙa ʙa'ze digar nigoh mekunand: «Ojo kase sumoro meʙinad?» Va ʙozmegardand. Xudo dilhojasonro az imon munsarif soxta (ʙargardonda), zero mardume nofahmand
9|128|Alʙatta pajomʙare az xudi sumo ʙar sumo firistoda sud, har on ci sumoro ranc medihad, ʙar u garon meojad. Saxt ʙa sumo dilʙasta ast va ʙo mu'minon musfiqu mehruʙon ast
9|129|Agar ʙozgardand, ʙigu: «Xudo ʙaroi man kofist, xudoe cuz U nest, ʙar U tavakkal kardam va Ust Parvardigori arsi ʙuzurg
10|1|Alif, lom, ro. In ast ojathoikitoʙi ʙo hikmat
10|2|Ojo mardum dar taaccuʙand, az in ki ʙar marde az xudason vahj kardem, ki mardumro ʙitarson va mu'minonro xusxaʙar deh, ki dar nazdi Parvardigorason pojgohe ʙaland dorand? Kofiron guftand, ki in mard oskoro codugarest
10|3|Parvardigori sumo Olloh ast, ki osmonhovu zaminro dar sas ruz ʙijofarid; sipas ʙa ars pardoxt: korhoro tadʙir kard. Cuz ʙa ruxsati U safo'atkunandae naʙosad. In ast Olloh — Parvardigori sumo. Uro ʙiparasted! Caro pand namegired
10|4|Bozgasti hamai sumo ʙa Ust. In ʙarhaq va'dai Xudost. U maxluqotro ʙijofarinad. On goh ononro ʙa sui xud ʙozgardonad, to kasonero, ki imon ovarda va kori soista kardaand, az rui adl mukofot dihad. Va kofironro ʙa cazoi kufrason saroʙest az oʙi cusonu azoʙest dardovar
10|5|Ust on, ki xursedro ravsani ʙaxsidu mohro munavvar soxt va ʙarojas manozile mu'ajjan kard, to az sumori solho va hisoʙ ogoh saved. Xudo hamai inhoro cuz ʙa haq najofarid va ojotro ʙaroi mardume, ki medonand, ʙatafsil ʙajon mekunad
10|6|Dar omadusudi saʙu ruz va on ci Xudo dar osmonhovu zamin ofaridaast, ʙaroi parhezgoron iʙrathost
10|7|Kasone, ki ʙa didori Mo umed nadorand va ʙa zindagii dunjavi xusnud suda va ʙa on oromis joftaand va onon, ki az ojoti Mo ʙexaʙarand
10|8|ʙa cazoi korhoe, ki mekardaand, cojgohason cahannam ast
10|9|Ononro, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, Parvardigorason ʙa saʙaʙi imonason ʙa ʙihisthoe purne'mat, ki nahrhoi oʙ dar zeri pojason corist, hidojat mekunad
10|10|Dar on co du'ojason in ast: «Bor Xudoe, Tu poKi». Va ʙa hangomi durud salom megujand. Va pojoni du'ojason in ast: «Sukr Xudoro, on Parvardigori cahonijon»
10|11|Agar ʙo hamon sitoʙ, ki mardum ʙaroi xud xajr metalaʙand, Xudo ʙarojason sarr metalaʙid, margason faro rasida ʙud. Pas ononro, ki ʙa didori Mo umed nadorand, vomeguzorem, to dar gumrohii xud sargardon ʙimonand
10|12|Cun ʙa odami zarare rasad, ci ʙar pahlu xufta ʙosad va ci nisasta jo istoda, Moro ʙa du'o mexonad. Va cun on zararro az u dur sozem, cunon meguzarad, ki gui Moro ʙaroi daf'i on zarare, ki ʙa u rasida ʙud, hargiz naxondaast. Amalhoi isrofkoron incunin dar nazarason orosta sudaast
10|13|Va Mo mardumero, ki pes az sumo ʙudand, cun sitam kardand va ʙa pajomʙaronason, ki ʙo daloili ravsan sui onho omada ʙudand, imon nameovardand, halok kardem. Mardumi gunahkorro incunin cazo medihem
10|14|On goh sumoro dar rui zamin conisini onho gardonidem, to ʙingarem, ki ci guna amal mekuned
10|15|Cun ojoti ravsani mo ʙar onon tilovat sud, onho, ki ʙa didori Mo umed nadorand, guftand: «Qur'one ƣajri in Qur'on ʙijovar jo digargunas kun!» Bigu: «Maro narasad, ki onro az sui xud digargun kunam. Har ci ʙa man vahj mesavad, pajravi hamon hastam. Metarsam, ki agar ʙa Parvardigoram nofarmon savam, ʙa azoʙi on ruzi ʙuzurg giriftor ojam»
10|16|Bigu: «agar Xudo mexost, man onro ʙar sumo tilovat namekardam va sumoro az on ogoh namesoxtam. Va pes az in dar mijoni sumo umre zistaam. Caro ʙa aql darnamejoʙed?»
10|17|Kist sitamkortar az on, ki ʙar Xudo duruƣ meʙandad, jo ojoti Uro duruƣ meʙarorad? Alʙatta kofiron nacot namejoʙand
10|18|Ƣajri Xudo cizhoero meparastand, ki na sudason merasonad na zijon. Va megujand: «Inho safe'oni mo dar nazdi Xudojand». Bigu: «Ojo ʙa Xudo az cize xaʙar medihed, ki dar zaminu osmon az on xaʙare nadorad? Xudo pok ast va az on ci ʙo U sarik mesozed, ʙolotar ast!»
10|19|Mardum cuz jak ummat naʙudand, mijonason ixtilof aftod. Va agar na on suxane ʙud, ki pes az in az Parvardigorat sodir gasta ʙud, dar on ci ixtilof mekunand, hukm suda ʙud
10|20|Va megujand: «Caro az coniʙi Parvardigoras mu'cizae ʙar u nozil namesavad?» Bigu: «Ilmi ƣajʙ az oni Xudost. Intizor ʙikased! Man niz ʙo sumo muntazir memonam!»
10|21|Har goh pas az zarare, ki ʙa mardum rasidaast, rahmate ʙa onho ʙicasonem, ʙini, ki dar ojoti Mo ʙadandesi mekunand, ʙigu: «Makri Xudo zudtar ast». Rasuloni Mo niz ʙadandesihoi sumoro menavisand
10|22|Ust, ki sumoro dar xuski va dar darjo sajr medihad. To on goh, ki dar kistiho hastand va ʙodi muvofiq ʙa harakatason meovarad, sodmonand. Cun tufon faro rasad va mavc az har su ʙar onho rezad, cunon kn pindorand, ki dar muhosirai mavc qaror giriftaand, Xudoro az rui ixlosi aqida ʙixonand, ki agar moro az in xatar ʙirahoni, az sukrguzoron xohem ʙud
10|23|Cun Xudo onhoro ʙirahonad, ʙini, ki dar zamin ʙa nohaq sarkasi kunand. Ej mardum, in sarkasi ʙa zijoni xudaton ast. Manfiatest dar in zindagii dunjavi. On goh hama ʙa nazdi Mo ʙozmegarded to az korhoe, ki mekardaed, ogohaton sozem
10|24|Misoli in zindagii dunjo cun ʙoronest, ki az osmon nozil kunem, to ʙa on har guna rastaniho az zamin ʙirujad, ci onho, ki odamijon mexurand va ci onho, ki corpojon mecarand. Cun zamin zinati xud ʙargirift va orosta sud va mardumas pindostand, ki xud qodir ʙar on hama ʙudaand, farmoni Mo saʙhangom jo ʙa ruz darrasad va cunon az ʙexas ʙarkanem, ki gui diruz dar on makon hec ciz naʙudaast, Ojotro ʙaroi mardume, ki meandesand, incunin tafsil medihem
10|25|Xudovand ʙa saroi salomat da'vat mekunad va har kiro ʙixohad ʙa rohi rost hidojat mekunad
10|26|Muzdi onon, ki neki mekunand, nekist va cize afzun ʙar on. Na sijaxruj savandu na xor. Inho ahli ʙihistand va dar on covidonand
10|27|Va ʙaroi onon, ki murtakiʙi ʙadiho savand, muzdi har ʙadi monandi on ast va xori ʙar onho ƣoliʙ mesavad. Kase onhoro az xasmi Xudo nigah namedorad, cunon savand, ki gujo suratason dar porae az saʙi torik pusida suda ast. Inho ahli cahanamand va covidona dar on hastand
10|28|Va ruze hamai onhoro dar mahsar gird ovarem. Sipas musrikonro guem: «Sumo va ʙuthojaton dar makoni xud qaror gired!» Sipas onhoro az jakdigar cudo mekunem va ʙuthojason megujand: «Sumo hargiz moro nameparastidaed»
10|29|Xudo ʙa guvohi mijoni movu sumo kofist, ki mo az parastisi sumo hargiz ogoh naʙudaem
10|30|Dar on co har kas harci kardaast, cazoasro xohad did va hamaro ʙa sui Xudo — mavloi haqiqiason ʙozmegardonand va hamai on ʙuton, ki ʙa ʙotil meparastidand, noʙud mesavand
10|31|Bigu: «Ci kase az osmonu zamin ʙa sumo ruzi medihad? Kist, ki sunavoivu ʙinoi meʙaxsad? Zindaro az murda padid meorad va murdaro az zinda va korxoro ʙa somon meovarad?» Xohand guft: «Olloh». Bigu: «Ojo namotarsed?»
10|32|On Olloh — Parvardigori xaqiqii sumost, ʙa'd az haqiqat cuz gumrohi cist? Pas ʙa kuco ruj meovared
10|33|Pas suxani Parvardigori tu dar ʙorai isjongaron, ki guft: «Inho imon nameovarand», ʙa haqiqat pajvast
10|34|Bigu: «Ojo az in ʙutoni sumo kase hast, ki cizero ʙijofarinad va ʙoz zinda kunad?» Bigu: «Xudoi jakto maxluqotro meofarinad va ʙoz zinda mekunad. Pas ci guna az haq ʙerohaton mekunand?»
10|35|Bigu: «Ojo az in ʙutoni sumo kase hast, ki ʙa haq roh namojad?» Bigu: «Xudo ʙa haq roh menamojad. Ojo on, ki ʙa haq roh menamojad ʙa pajravi sazovortar ast a on ki ʙa haq roh namenamojad va xud niz muhtoci hidojat ast? Sumoro ci mesavad? Ci guna hukm mekuned?»
10|36|Bestarason faqat pajravi gumonand va gumon nametavonad coi haqro ʙigirad. Alʙatta Xudo ʙa kore, ki mekunand, ogoh ast
10|37|Nasojad, ki in Qur'onro cuz ʙa Xudo nisʙat kunand ʙalki tasdiqi cizest, ki pes az on omadaast va ʙajoni on kitoʙ ast. Sakke nest, ki az coniʙi Parvardigori cahonijon ast
10|38|Megujand, ki onro ʙa duruƣ ʙa Xudo nisʙat mekunad. Bigu: «Agar rost megued, cuz Xudo har kiro, ki metavoned, ʙa jori ʙixoned va surae monandi on ʙijovared»
10|39|Cizero duruƣ sumurdand, ki ʙa ilmi on ihota najofta ʙudand va hanuz azoʙas ʙa onho naomadaast. Kasone, ki pes az onon ʙudand, niz pajomʙaronro cunin ʙa duruƣ ʙarovardaand. Pas ʙingar, ki oqiʙati kori sitamkoron ci guna ʙudaast
10|40|Ba'ze az onho ʙa on imon meovarand va ʙa'ze imon nameovarand. Va IIarvardigori tu ʙa fasodkoron ogohtar ast
10|41|Agar turo ʙa duruƣ nisʙat kardan, ʙigu: «Amali man az oni man ast va amali sumo az oni sumo. Sumo az kori man ʙezored va man az kori sumo ʙezoram»
10|42|Ba'ze az onho ʙa tu gus medihand. Ojo agar darnajoʙand, tu metavoni karonro sunavo sozi
10|43|Ba'ze az onho ʙa tu menigarand. Ojo agar naʙinand, tu metavoni kuroni noʙinoro roh ʙinamoi
10|44|Xudovand ʙa mardum hec sitam namekunad, vale mardum xud ʙa xud sitam mekunand
10|45|Va ruze, ki Xudovand ononro dar mahsar gird ovarad, cunon pindori, ki tanho soate az ruz dar dunjo istodaand, jakdigarro ʙisinosand. Onho, ki didor ʙo Xudoro duruƣ, mehisoʙidand, zjajondidaand va hidojatnajoftaand
10|46|Jo ʙa'ze az cizhoero, ki ʙa onho va'da dodaem, ʙa tu menamojonem jo turo memironem. Bozgasti hamaason ʙa nazdi most va Xudo ʙa har kore, ki mekunand, sohid ast
10|47|Har ummatero pajomʙare ʙud va cun pajomʙarason ʙijomad, korho mijonason ʙa adolat hal sudand va mavridi sitam voqe' nasudand
10|48|Megujand: «Agar rost megued, pas in va'da ci vaqt xohad ʙud?»
10|49|Bigu: «Man dar ʙorai xud, cuz on ci Xudo ʙixohad, moliki hec sudu zijone nestam. Margi har ummatero zamone muajjan ast. Cun zamonason faro rasad, na jak soat der kunand va na jak soat pes ravand»
10|50|Bigu: «Ci mekuned, agar azoʙi u ʙa nogoh saʙhangom jo ʙa ruz faro rasad? Gunohkoron ci cizro incunin ʙa sitoʙ metalaʙand
10|51|Ojo cun azoʙ ʙa vuqu' pajvandad, ʙa on imon meovared? Aknun in hamon cizest, ki faro rasidanasro ʙa sitoʙ mexosted
10|52|On goh ʙa sitamkoron gujand: «Azoʙi covidro ʙicased! Ojo na cunin ast, ki dar ʙaroʙari amalhojaton cazo meʙined?»
10|53|Az tu xaʙar mepursand, ki ojo haq ast? Bigu: «Ore, savgand ʙa Parvardigoram, ki haq ast va sumoro quvvai firor az on nest!»
10|54|Agar har gunahkore sohiʙi hamai rui zamin ʙosad, xohad, ki xudro ʙa on azoʙ ʙozxarad va cun azoʙro ʙingarand, pusajmonii xud dar dil nihon dorand. Mijonason ʙa adolat hukm savad va mavridi sitam voqe' nagardand
10|55|Bidoned, ki har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast, az oni Xudost! Va ogoh ʙosed, ki va'dai Xudo haq ast, vale ʙestarason namedonand
10|56|Ust, ki zinda mekunadu memironad va hama ʙa sui U ʙozmegardand
10|57|Ej mardum, ʙaroi sumo az coniʙi Parvardigoraton pande omad va sifoe ʙaroi on ʙemorie, ki dar dil dored va rohnamoivu rahmate ʙaroi mu'minon
10|58|Bigu: «Ba fazli Xudovu rahmati U». Sodmon savand, zero in du az har ci cam' mekunand, ʙehtar ast
10|59|Bigu: «Ojo ʙa rizqe, ki Xudo ʙarojaton nozil kardaast, nigaristaed? Ba'zero harom sumurded va ʙa'zero halol». Bigu: «Xudo ʙa sumo icoza dodaast jo ʙa U duruƣ meʙanded?»
10|60|Onon, ki ʙa Xudo duruƣ meʙandand, dar ʙorai ruzi qijomat ci gumon kardaand? Xudo fazli xudro ʙa mardumon arzoni medorad, vale ʙestarinason sukr namegujand
10|61|Dar har kore, ki ʙosi va har ci az Qur'on ʙixoni va dast ʙa har amale, ki ʙizaned, hangome ki ʙa on mepardozed, mo nozir ʙar sumo hastem. Bar Parvardigori tu hatto ʙa miqdori zarrae dar zaminu osmonho pusida nest. Va har ci xurdtar az on jo ʙuzurgtar az on ʙosad, dar kitoʙi muʙin navista sudaast
10|62|Ogoh ʙosed, ki ʙar dustoni Xudo ʙime nest va ƣamgin namesavand
10|63|Kasonero, ki imon ovardand va parhezgori mekardand
10|64|xusxaʙar ast onhoro dar dunjovu oxirat. Suxani Xudo digargun namesavad. In ast komjoʙii ʙuzurg
10|65|Suxani onon turo ƣamgin nasozad. Izzat ʙa tamomi az oni Xudovand ast. Ust, ki sunavovu donost
10|66|Ogoh ʙosed, ki az oni Xudost har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast va onon, ki ƣajri Xudoro sarikon mexonand, az gumoni xud pajravi mekunand va duruƣ megujand
10|67|Ust, ki saʙro ʙarojaton padid ovard, to dar on ʙijoromed va ruzro padid ovard, to dar on ʙuʙined. Dar inho ʙaroi mardume, ki mesunavand, iʙrathost
10|68|Guftand: «Xudo farzande intixoʙidast». Pok ast! Benijoz ast! Az oni Ust har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast! Sumoro ʙar on suxan dalele nest. Caro dar ʙorai Xudo cizhoe megued, ki ʙa on ogoh nested
10|69|Bigu: «Onho, ki ʙa Xudo duruƣ meʙandand, nacot namejoʙand!»
10|70|Barxurdori az dunjo, on goh ʙozgastason ʙa sui Mo. Sipas ʙa cazoi kufr varzidanason azoʙe saxtason mecasonem
10|71|Barojason dostoni Nuhro ʙixon, on goh, ki ʙa qavmi xud guft: «Ej qavmi man, agar istodani man dar mijoni sumo va jodovarii ojoti Xudo ʙar sumo garon meojad, man ʙar Xudo tavakkal mekunam, koruʙori xud va ʙutonatonro gird ovared, cunon ki hec ciz az kore, ki mekuned, ʙar sumo pusida naʙosad va ʙa dusmanii man qadam ʙa pes nihed va maro muhlat nadihed
10|72|Va agar pust karded, man az sumo hec muzde naxostaam, ki muzdi man ʙo Xudost va man amr sudaam, ki az taslimsudagon ʙosam!»
10|73|Duruƣas ʙarovardand va Mo uvu hamrohonasro dar kisti ʙirahonidem va ononro conisini pesinijon soxtem va kasonero, ki ojoti Moro duruƣ mesumurdand, ƣarq kardem. Pas ʙingar, ki oqiʙati ʙimdodasudagon ci guna ʙud
10|74|On goh pas az u pajomʙarone ʙar qavmason firistodem va onon dalelhoe ravsan ovardand, vale mardum ʙa on ci pes az on duruƣ ʙarovarda ʙudand, imon ovaranda naʙudand. Bar dilhoi tacovuzkoron incunin muhr menihem
10|75|Va pas az onho Musovu Horunro hamrohi ojotamon ʙar Fir'avnu ʙuzurgoni qavmas firistodem. Va onon sarkasi kardand va mardume taʙahkor ʙudand
10|76|Va cun haq az nazdi Mo ʙa sui onho omad, guftand, ki in codue oskor ast
10|77|Muso guft: «Ojo suxani haqro, ki inak ʙar sumo nozil sudaast, codu mexoned va hol on ki codugaron nacot namejoʙand!»
10|78|Guftand: «Ojo omadai, to moro az on din, ki padaronamonro ʙar on joftaem, dur sozi, to dar zamin sarvari joʙed? Vale mo ʙa sumo imon nameovarem!»
10|79|Fir'avn guft: «Hamai codugaroni donoro nazdi man ʙijovared!»
10|80|Cun codugaron omadand, Muso guft: «Bijafkaned, har ciro, ki ʙojad ʙijafkaned!»
10|81|Cun ʙijafkandand, Muso guft: «On ci sumo ovardaed, codust va Xudo onro ʙotil xohad soxt, zero Xudo kori fasodkoronro ʙa saloh nameovarad
10|82|Va Xudovand ʙo suxanoni xud haqro ʙa isʙot merasonad, agarci gunahgoronro noxus ojad»
10|83|Az ʙimi ozori Fir'avn va ʙuzurgoni qavmi u, cuz guruhe az onho ʙa Muso imon najovardand. Va Fir'avn dar zamin ʙartari mecust va u az tacovuzkoron ʙud
10|84|Muso guft: «Ej qavmi man, agar ʙa Xudo imon ovardaed va taslimi farmon hasted, ʙa U tavakkal kuned!»
10|85|Guftand; Bar Xudo tavakkal kardem, ej Parvardigori mo, moro maƣluʙi in mardumi sitamkor makun
10|86|va ʙa rahmati xud moro az in kofiron rahoi ʙaxs!»
10|87|Ba Muso va ʙarodaras vahj kardem, ki ʙaroi qavmi xud dar Misr xonahoe muhajjo kuned va xonahoi xudro iʙodatgoh sozed va namoz guzored va mu'minonro xusxaʙar deh
10|88|Muso guft: «Ej Parvardigori mo, ʙa Fir'avnu ʙuzurgoni qavmas dar in cahon zinatu amvol dodai, ej Parvardigori mo, to digaronro az tariqi Tu gumroh kunand. Ej Parvardigori mo, molhojasonro noʙud soz va dilasonro saxt kun! Imon nameovarand, to on goh, ki azoʙi dardovarro ʙingarand»
10|89|Guft: «Xosti sumo icoʙat sud, soʙitqadam ʙosed va ʙa tariqai nodonon pajravi makuned»
10|90|Mo ʙani—Isroilro az darjo guzaronidem. Fir'avnu laskarijonas ʙa qasdi sitamu tacovuz ʙa ta'qiʙason pardoxtand. Cun Fir'avn ƣark mesud, guft: «Imon ovardam, ki hec xudovande cuz on ki ʙani—Isroil ʙa on imon ovardaavd, nest va man az taslimsudagonam»
10|91|Ojo aknun? Va tu pes az in isjon mekardi va az fasodkoron ʙudi
10|92|Imruz cismi turo ʙa xuski mepartoem, to ʙaron onon, ki pas az tu memonand, iʙrate ʙosi va hol on ki ʙisjore az mardum az ojoti Mo ƣofiland
10|93|Alʙatta ʙani-Isroilro dar makone neku coj dodem va az pokiho ruzijason dodem va to on hangom, ki sohiʙi donis nasuda ʙudand, ziddijate nadostand. Parvardigori tu dar ruzi qijomat dar on ci ziddijat mekardand, mijonason hukm xohad kard
10|94|Agar dar on ci ʙar tu nozil kardaem, dar suʙha hasti, az onhoe, ki kitoʙi osmonii pes az turo mexonand, ʙipurs. Alʙatta haq ast on ci az coniʙi Parvardigorat ʙar tu nozil sudaast. Pas naʙojad dar sumori suʙhakukandagon ʙosi
10|95|Va az onon, ki ojoti Xudoro duruƣ meʙarorand, maʙos, ki dar zumrai zijonkunandagon ʙosi
10|96|Kasone, ki suxani Parvardigori tu dar ʙorai onon vociʙ sudaast, imon nameovarand
10|97|harcand har guna mu'cizae ʙar onon oskor savad, to on goh, ki azoʙi dardovarro ʙingarand
10|98|Caro mardumi hec dehae, ʙa hangome ki imonasom naf'ason msdod, imon najovardand. magar qavmi Junus, ki cun imon ovardand, azoʙi xori dar dunjoro az onon ʙardostem va to hangome ki acalason faro rasid, az zindagi ʙarxurdorason kardem
10|99|Agar Parvardigori tu ʙixohad, hamai kasone, ki dar rui zaminand, imon meovarand. Ojo tu mardumro macʙur mekuni, ki imon ʙijovarand
10|100|Be xosti Xudo hec kasro narasad, ki imon ʙijovarad. Va palidiro ʙar kasone, ki xiradi xud ʙa kor nameʙarand, muqarrar mekunad
10|101|Bigu: «Bingared, ki ci cizhoe dar osmonhovu zamin ast!» Va in ojotu husdorho qavmero, ki imon nameovarand, naf' namekunad
10|102|Intizori ruzero mekasand monandi ruzhoe, ki pesinijonason muntaziras ʙudand? Bigu; «Intizor ʙikased, ki man niz ʙo sumo muntaziram!»
10|103|On goh pajomʙaronamon va kasonero, ki imon ovardaand, merahonem. Zero ʙar Mo fariza ast, ki mu'minonro ʙirahonem
10|104|Bigu: «Ej mardum, agar sumo dar dini man sak dored, man cizhoero, ki ʙa coi Olloh meparasted, nameparastam. Man Ollohro meparastam, ki sumoro memironad va amr sudaam, ki az mu'minon ʙosam!»
10|105|Va ʙa dini pok ruj ovar va az musrikon maʙos
10|106|Ba coi Olloh xudojonero, ki na ʙa tu sud merasonand va na zijon, maxon. Agar cunin kuni, az sitamkoron xohi ʙud
10|107|Va agar Xudo ʙa tu zijone ʙirasonad, cuz U kase daf'i on natavonad kard Va agar ʙaroi tu xajre ʙixohad, hec kas fazli Uro ʙoznatavonad dost. Fazli xudro ʙa har kas az ʙandagonas, ki ʙixohad, merasonad va U omurzandavu mehruʙon ast
10|108|Bigu: «Ej mardum, pajomi rostin az coniʙi Parvardigoraton ʙarojaton, faro rasid. Pas har kas, ki ʙa rohi rost hidojat joʙad, hidojat ʙa sudi ust. Va har ki gumroh gardad, ʙa zijoni xud ʙa gumrohi aftodaast. Va man uhdadori sumo nestam»
10|109|Cizero, ki ʙa tu vahj mesavad, pajravi kun va saʙr kun to Xudo dovari kunad, ki U ʙehtarini dovaron ast
11|1|Alif, lom, ro. Kitoʙest ʙo ojote ustuvoru ravsan az coniʙi hakime ogoh
11|2|ki ƣajri Xudoi jaktoro naparasted, man az coniʙi U tarsonandai sumo va niz muƶdadihandae ʙaroi sumo hastam
11|3|Va niz az Parvardigoraton ʙaxsois ʙixohed va ʙa dargohas tavʙa kuned, to sumoro az rizqe neku, to on goh, ki muqarrar ast, ʙarxurdori dihad. Va har soistai ne'matro ne'mat dihad. Va agar rujgardon saved, ʙar sumo az azoʙi ruzi ʙuzurg ʙimnokam
11|4|Bozgastaton ʙa Xudost va U ʙa har kore tavonost
11|5|Ogoh ʙos, ki inho surat ʙarmegardonand, to rozi dili xud pinhon dorand, hol on ki ʙa on hangom, ki comahoi xud dar sar mekasand. Xudo oskoru nihonasonro medonad, zero U ʙa rozi dilho ogoh ast
11|6|Har cunʙandae dar rui zamin mavcud ast, ruzii u ʙar uhdai Xudost va coi zistu margasro medonad zero hama dar kitoʙi muʙin omadaast
11|7|Ust, ki osmonhovu zaminro dar sas ruz ofarid va arsi U ʙar rui oʙ ʙud. To ʙijozmojad kadom jak az sumo ʙa amal nekutar ast. Va agar ʙigui, ki ʙa'd az marg zinda mesaved, kofiron gujand, ki in cuz coduii oskor nest
11|8|Va agar cand gohe azoʙasonro ʙa der ʙijafkanem, mepursand: «Ci ciz mone'i on sudaast?» Ogoh ʙosed, cun azoʙason faro rasad, onro ʙoznagardonand va on ci masxaraas mekardand, ononro dar ʙar xohad girift
11|9|Agar ʙa inson rahmate ʙicasonem, on goh az u ʙozas girem, noumed mesavad va nosukri mekunad
11|10|Va agar pas az saxtivu ranc ne'matu osoise ʙa u ʙicasonem, megujad: «Noguvoriho az man dur sudaast». Va dar in hol sodmon ast va faxr mekunad
11|11|ƣajri kasone, ki saʙr varzidand va korhoi neku kardand, ki omurzis va muzdi ʙuzurg az oni onhost
11|12|Sojad, ki ʙa'ze az cizhoero, ki ʙar tu vahj kardaem, tark kuni va ʙa on diltang ʙosi, ki megujand: «Caro gance ʙar u afkanda namesavad? Va caro faristae hamrohi u nameojad?» Cuz in nest, ki tu ʙimdihandae ʙes nesti va Xudost, ki korsozi har cizest
11|13|Jo on ki megujand, ki az xud ʙarmeʙofad va ʙa duruƣ ʙa Xudo nisʙatas mekunad. Bigu: «Agar rost megued, cuz Xudo har kiro, ki tavoned, ʙa jori ʙitalaʙed va dah sura monandi on ʙa ham ʙarʙofta, ʙijovared
11|14|Pas agar sumoro icoʙat nakardand, ʙidoned, ki Qur'on ʙa ilmi Xudo nozil suda va niz hec xudoe cuz U nest. Ojo taslim mesaved?»
11|15|Onon, ki zindagivu zinati in dunjoro ʙixohand, pas hamai muzdi kirdorasonro dar in cahon medihem va dar on nuqsone nameʙinand
11|16|Inho kasone hastand, ki dar oxirat cuz otas nasiʙe nadorand va har ci kardaand, nociz savad va har ci ʙa coj ovarand, ʙotil ast
11|17|Ojo on kas, ki az coniʙi Parvardigori xud dalele ravsan dorad va zaʙonas ʙa on gujost va pes az in kitoʙi Muso, ki xud pesvovu rahmate ʙudaast, ʙa on guvohi doda, ʙo on kas, ki dalele nadorad, ʙaroʙar ast? Onho ʙa on kitoʙi ravsan imon meovarand. Va har guruhi digare, ki ʙa U kofir savad, cojgohas dar otas ast. Dar on sak makun, ki haq ast va az coniʙi Parvardigorat omadaast. Vale ʙestari mardum imon nameovarand
11|18|Ci kas sitamkortar az on kasest, ki ʙa Xudo duruƣ meʙandad? Inhoro ʙa Parvardigorason arza xohand dost va sohidon guvohi xohand dod, ki inhoand, ki ʙar Parvardigorason duruƣ meʙastaand. La'nati Xudo ʙar sitamkoron ʙod
11|19|onon, ki mardumro az rohi Xudo ʙozmedorand va rohi Xudoro kaciasro mexohand va ʙa oxirat imon nadorand
11|20|Inho nametavonand dar rui zamin az Xudo ʙigurezand va ƣajri U hec jovare nadorand, azoʙason muzo'af (ducandon) mesavad. Na tavoni sunidan dostaand va na tavoni didan
11|21|Inho ʙa xestan zijon rasonidand va on ciro, ki ʙa duruƣ Xudo mexondand, az dast dodaand
11|22|Ba nocor dar oxirat zijonkortarand
11|23|Kasone, ki imon ovardand va korhoi soista kardaand va dar ʙaroʙari Parvardigorason sar xam namudaand, ahli ʙihistand va dar on covidonand
11|24|Misoli in du guruh misli kuru kar va ʙinovu sunavost. Ojo in du ʙa misol ʙo ham ʙaroʙarand? Caro pand namegired
11|25|Va Nuhro ʙar mardumas ʙa pajomʙari firistodem. Guft: «Man ʙaroi sumo ʙimdihandae oskoram
11|26|ki cuz Xudoi jaktoro naparasted! Zero az azoʙi ruzi saxti qijomat ʙar sumo ʙimnokam!»
11|27|Buzurgoni qavmas, ki kofir ʙudand, guftand: -Mo turo cuz insone monandi xud nameʙinem. Va nameʙinem, ki cuz odamoni past ʙa tu pajravi kunand. Va nameʙinem, ki sumoro ʙar mo ʙehtarie ʙosad, ʙalki pindorem, ki duruƣ megued»
11|28|Guft: «Ej qavmi man, ci megued, agar az Parvardigoram huccate ʙa hamroh dosta ʙosam va U maro rahmati xes arzoni karda ʙosad va sumo az didani on notavon ʙosed, ojo dar hole, ki xud namexohed, sumoro ʙa zuri ʙa qaʙuli U vodorem
11|29|Ej qavmi man, dar ʙaroʙari taʙliƣi risolati xud mole az sumo nametalaʙam, Muzdi man tanho ʙo Xudost. Onhoero, ki imon ovardaand, az xud nameronam, onon ʙo Parvardigori xud didor xohand kard. Vale meʙinam, ki sumo mardume nodon hasted
11|30|Ej qavmi man, agar onhoro az xud ʙironam, ci kase dar muqoʙili Xudo maro jori xohad kard? Ojo haqiqatro darnamejoʙed
11|31|Ba sumo namegujam, ki xazoini Xudo dar nazdi man ast, Va ilmi ƣajʙ ham namedonam. Va namegujam, ki farista hastam. Va namegujam, ki Xudo ʙa onon, ki sumo ʙa haqorat dar onho menigared, xajri xudro ato nakunad. Xudo ʙa on ci dar dilhoi onhost, ogohtar ast. Agar cunin kunam, az sitamkoron xoham ʙud»
11|32|Guftand: «Ej Nuh ʙo mo cidol kardi va ʙisjor ham cidol kardi. Agar rost megui, har va'dae, ki ʙa mo dodai, ʙijovar!»
11|33|Guft: «Xudost, ki agar ʙixohad, on va'daro oskor mekunad va sumo az on natavoned gurext
11|34|Va agar Xudo xosta ʙosad, ki gumrohaton sozad, agar man ʙixoham sumoro pand diham, pandam sud naxohad kard. Ust Parvardigori sumo va hama ʙa nazdi U ʙozmegarded»
11|35|Jo megujand, ki onro ʙa Xudo duruƣ ʙastaast. Bigu: «Agar onro ʙa Xudo duruƣ ʙasta ʙosam, gunohas ʙar man ast va man az gunohe, ki mokuned, muʙarro (pok) hastam
11|36|Va ʙa Nuh vahj rasid, ki az qavmi tu cuz on guruh, ki imon ovardaand, digar imon naxohand ovard. Az kirdori onon anduhgin maʙos
11|37|Kistiro zeri nazar va ilhomi Mo ʙisoz va dar ʙorai in sitamkoron ʙo Man suxan maguj, ki hama ƣarq savand
11|38|Nuh kisti mesoxt va har ʙor, ki ʙuzurgoni qavmas ʙar u meguzastand, masxaraas mekardand. Meguft: «Agar sumo moro masxara mekuned, ʙa zudi mo ham monandi sumo masxaraaton xohem kard
11|39|Ba zudi xohed donist, ki azoʙ ʙar ki rasad va xoras sozad va azoʙi covid ʙar ki farojad!»
11|40|Cui farmoni Mo faro omad va tanur cusid, guftem: «Az har naru moda duto va niz xonadoni xudro dar kisti ʙinson, — ƣajri on kase, ki hukm dar ʙoraas az pes sodir suda ʙosad — va niz onhoero, ki ʙa tu imon ovardaand. Va cuz andake ʙa u imon najovarda ʙudand»
11|41|Guft: «Bar on savor saved, ki ʙa nomi Xudo ʙa rox aftad va ʙa nomi Xudo ʙiistad. Zero Parvardigori man ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
11|42|Kisti ononro dar mijoni mavchoe cun kuh meʙurd. Nuh pisarasro, ki dar gusae istoda ʙud, nido dod: «Ej pisar, ʙo mo savor sav va ʙo kofiron maʙos!»
11|43|Guft: «Man ʙar sari kuhe, ki maro az oʙ nigah dorad, co xoham girift». Guft: «Imruz hec nigahdorandae az farmoni Xudo nest, ƣajri kasero, ki ʙar u rahm ovarad». Nogahon mavc mijoni on du parda gast va u az ƣarq sudagon ʙud
11|44|Va gufta sud: «Ej zamin, oʙi xud furu ʙar va ej osmon, ʙozist». Oʙ furu sud va kor ʙa pojon omad va kisti ʙar kuhi Cudi qaror girift va nido omad, ki la'nat ʙod ʙar mardumi sitamkora
11|45|Nuh Parvardigorasro nido dod: «Ej Parvardigori man, pisaram az xonadoni man ʙud va va'dai Tu haq ast va nerumandtarini hukmkunandagon Tu Hasti!»
11|46|Guft: «Ej Nuh, u az xonadoni tu nest, u amalest nosoleh. Az sari noogohi az Man cize maxoh. Barhazar medoram turo, ki az mardumi nodon ʙosi»
11|47|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, panoh meʙaram ʙa Tu, agar az sari noogohi cize ʙixoham va agar maro naʙaxsoi va ʙa man rahmat najovari, az zijonkardagon xoham ʙud»
11|48|Gufta sud: «Ej Nuh ʙa salomat va ʙarakote, ki ʙar tuvu onho, ki hamrohi tuand, arzoni dostaem, furud oj. Va ummathoe hastand, ki onhoro ʙarxurdor mesozem, on goh dastxusi azoʙi dardovari Mo mesavand»
11|49|Inho az xaʙarhoi ƣajʙ ast, ki ʙar tu vahj mekunem. Pes az in na tu onhoro medonisti va na qavmi tu. Pas saʙr kun, zero oqiʙati nek az oni parhezgoron ast
11|50|Va ʙar qavmi Od ʙarodarason Hudro firistodem. Guft: «Ej qavmi man, Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparasted, sumoro hec xudoe cuz U nest va sumo duruƣsozone ʙes nested
11|51|Ej qavmi man, dar ʙaroʙari pajomi xud az sumo muzde nametalaʙam. Muzdi man tanxo ʙo on kasest, ki maro ofaridaast. Caro az rui xirad nameandesed
11|52|Va ej qavmi man, az Parvardigoraton ʙaxsois ʙixohed, on goh ʙar ostoni U tavʙa kuned to ʙoronro paj dar paj ʙar sumo furu rezad va ʙar nerujaton ʙijafzojad! Va cun gunahkoron ruj ʙarmatoʙed!»
11|53|Guftand: «Ej xud, tu ʙaroi mo daleli ravsane najovardai va mo ʙa guftori tu xudojoni xudro tark namekunem va ʙa tu imon nameovarem
11|54|Ƣajri in naguem, ki ʙa'ze az xudojoni mo ʙa tu ozore rasondaand». Guft: «Xudoro guvoh megiram va sumo niz guvoh ʙosed, ki man az on ci ƣajri Xudoi jakto ʙa sirk meparasted, ʙezoram
11|55|Hamagi ʙa hilagari ʙar ziddi man ʙarxezed va maro muhlat nadihed
11|56|Man ʙar Xudoi jakto, ki Parvardigori man va Parvardigori sumost, tavakkal kardam. Hec cunʙandae, nest magar on ki zimomi ixtijorasro U giriftaast. Alʙatta Parvardigori man ʙar siroti mustaqim ast
11|57|Agar, ham rujgardon saved, man risolati xudro ʙa sumo rasonidam va Parvardigori man mardumi digarero conisini sumo xohad soxt va hec ʙa u zijone namerasoned. Zero Parzardigori man nigahʙoni hamai cizhost!»
11|58|Cun farmoni Mo darrasid, ʙa ʙaxsoisi xes Hud va kasonero, ki ʙa u imon ovarda ʙudand, nacot dodem va onhoro az azoʙi saxt rahonidem
11|59|Inho qavmi Od ʙudand, ki ojoti Parvardigorasonro inkor kardand va pajomʙaronasro nofarmoni kardand va ʙa farmoni har caʙʙori sarkas gardan nihodand
11|60|Va dar in dunjovu ruzi qijomat giriftori la'nat sudand. Ogoh ʙosed, ki qavmi Od ʙa Parvardigorason kofir sudand, ki la'nat ʙod ʙar Od, qavmi Hud
11|61|Va ʙar qavmi Samud ʙarodarason Solehro firistodem. Guft: «Ej qavmi man. Xudoj jaktoro ʙiparasted! Sumoro cuz U xudoe nest. Ust, ki sumoro az zamin padid ovardaast va xost, ki oʙodonas dored. Pas ʙaxsois xohed va ʙa dargohas tavʙa kuned. Alʙatta Parvardigori man nazdik ast va du'ohoro icoʙat mekunad!»
11|62|Guftand: «Ej Soleh pes az in ʙa tu umed medostem. Ojo moro az parastisi on ci padaronamon meparastidand, ʙozmedori? Mo az on ci moro ʙa on da'vat mekuni, dar sakkem»
11|63|Guft: «Ej qavmi man, ci gued agar az Parvardigoram huccate ʙa hamroh dosta ʙosam va U maro rahmati xud arzoni karda ʙosad, ci kase maro jori mekunad, agar az farmonas sarpeci kunam? Agar az sumo farmon ʙaram, cuz ʙa zijoni man naxohed afzud
11|64|Ej qavmi man, in modasuturi Xudovand ast va nisonaest ʙaroi sumo. Bigzoredas to dar zamini Xudo ʙicarad va ʙa ʙadi majozoredas, ki ʙa zudi azoʙ sumoro furu girad»
11|65|Pas modasuturro qatl kardand. Guft: «Se ruz dar xonahoi xud az zindagi nasiʙador saved va in va'daest xoli az duruƣ»
11|66|Cun amri Mo faro rasid Solehro ʙo kasone, ki ʙa u imon ovarda ʙudand, ʙa rahmati xud az xorii on ruz nacot ʙaxsidem. Zero Parvardigori tu tavonovu piruzmand ast
11|67|Va sitamkoronro sajhae (na'rae) furu girift va dar xonahoi xud ʙar coj murdand
11|68|Cunon ki gujo hargiz dar on dijor naʙudaand. Ogoh ʙosed, ki qavmi Samud ʙa Parvardigorason kofir sudand, hamono, ʙar qavmi Samud la'nat ʙod
11|69|Ba tahqiq rasuloni Mo ʙaroi Iʙrohim muƶda ozardand. Guftand: «Salom!» Guft: «Salom!» Va lahzae ʙa'd gusolae ʙirjon xozir ovard
11|70|Va cun did, ki ʙa on dast daroz namekunand, ononro noxus dost va dar dil az onho ʙimnok sud, guftand: «Matars, mo ʙar qavmi Lut firistoda sudaem»
11|71|Zanas, ki istoda ʙud, xandid. Uro ʙa Ishoq xusxaʙar dodem va pas az Ishoq ʙa Ja'quʙ
11|72|Zan guft: «Voj ʙar man, ojo dar in pironsoli mezojam va in savhari man niz pir ast? In cizi aciʙest!»
11|73|Guftand: «Ojo az farmoni Xudo ta'accuʙ mekuni? Rahmatu ʙarakati Xudo ʙar sumo — ahli in xona arzoni ʙod. U sutudani va ʙuzurgvor ast
11|74|Cun vahdat az Iʙrohim ʙiraft va uro xusxaʙar omad, ʙo Mo dar ʙorai qavmi Lut ʙa mucodala ʙarxost
11|75|Iʙrohim ʙurdʙor ast va rahmdil ast va farmonʙardor ast
11|76|Ej Iʙrohim, az in suxan ruj gardon! Farmoni Parvardigorat omadaast va ʙar onho azoʙe, ki hec ʙargaste nadorad, furud xohad omad
11|77|Cun rasuloni Mo nazdi Lut omadand, Lut anduhginu diltang sud va guft: «Imruz ruzi saxtest»
11|78|Va qavmas sitoʙon nazdi u omadand va onon pes az in murtakiʙi korhoi zist mesudand. Lut guft: «Ej qavmi man, inho duxtaroni man hastand. Baroi Sumo pokizatarand. Az Xudo ʙitarsed va moro dar ʙaroʙari mehmononam hicil makuned. Ojo mardi xiradmande dar mijoni sumo nest?»
11|79|Guftaʹ: d: «Tu xud medoni, ki moro ʙa duxtaroni tu nijoze nest va niz medoni, ki ci mexohem»
11|80|Lut guft: «Kos dar ʙaroʙari sumo qudrate medostam va metavonistam ʙa takjagohe ustuvor panoh ʙiʙaram!»
11|81|Guftand: «Ej Lut, mo rasuloni Parvardigori tu hastem! Inho hargiz ʙa tu dast naxohand joft. Cun pose az saʙ ʙigzarad, xonadoni xudro ʙerun ʙiʙar. Va hec jak az sumo ruj ʙarnagardonad, cuz zanat, ki ʙa u niz on ci ʙa onho rasad, xohad rasid. Va'dai onho suʙhgoh ast. Ojo suʙh nazdik nest?»
11|82|Cun farmoni Mo faro rasid, on coro zeru zaʙar kardem va ʙar on sahr ʙorone az sanghoe az siccil" paj dar paj ʙoronidem
11|83|ki ʙar onho nisoni Parvardigorat ʙud va cunin azoʙe az sitamkoron dur nest
11|84|Va ʙar Madjan ʙarodarason Su'ajʙro firistodem. Guft: «Ej qavmi man, Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparasted, sumoro hec xudoe cuz U nest! Va dar pajmonavu tarozu nuqson makuned! Inak sumoro dar ne'mat meʙinam. Va az ruze, ki azoʙas sumoro furu girad, ʙimnokam
11|85|Ej qavmi man, pajmonavu tarozuro az rui adl komil ado kuned va ʙa mardum cizhojasonro kam madihed va cun taʙahkoron dar zamni fasod nakuned
11|86|Agar imon ovardaed, on ci Xudo ʙoki meguzorad, ʙarojaton ʙehtar ast. Va man nigahʙoni sumo nestam»
11|87|Guftand: «Ej Su'ajʙ, ojo namozat ʙa tu farmon medihad, ki mo on ciro padaronamon meparastidand, tark guem jo dar molhoi xud oncunon, ki xud mexohem, istifoda nakunem? Ba rosti tu marde ʙurdʙoru xiradmand hasti»
11|88|Guft: «Ej qavmi man, ci megued, agar ʙo man az coniʙi Parvardigoram huccate ʙosad va U maro rizqe neku ato karda ʙosad? Agar sumoro man' mekunam, ʙaroi on nest, ki xud sude ʙiʙaram. To on co, ki ʙitavonam, qasde cuz ʙa saloh ovardanaton nadoram. Tavfiqi man tanho ʙo Xudost. Ba U tavakkal kardaam va ʙa dargohi U ruj meovaram»
11|89|Ej qavmi man, ziddijat ʙo man sumoro ʙa kore vonadorad to on ci ʙar qavmi Nuh jo qavmi Hud jo qavmi Soleh jo dar hamin nazdiki ʙa qavmi Lut rasid, ʙa sumo niz ʙirasad
11|90|Az Parvardigoraton omurzis ʙixohed. Ba dargohas tavʙa kuned, ki Parvardigori man mehruʙonu dustdoranda ast!»
11|91|Guftand: «Ej Su'ajʙ, ʙisjore az cizhoero, ki megui, namefahmem, turo dar mijoni xud notavon meʙinem, agar ʙa xotiri qaʙilaat naʙud, sangsorat mekardem va tu ʙar mo piruzi najoʙi»
11|92|Guft: «Ej qavmi man, ojo qaʙilai man dar nazdi sumo az Xudo piruzmandtar ast? Ojo Xudoro pasi pusti xud afkapded? Va hol on ki Parvardigori man ʙar har kore, ki mekuned, ogoh ast
11|93|Ej qavmi man, sumo hamcunon, ki hasted, ʙa kori xud masƣul ʙosed va man ham ʙa kori xud masƣul mesavam. Ba zudi xohed donist, ki on azoʙi xorkunanda ʙar ci kase furud meojad va ci kase duruƣgust. Muntazir ʙimoned, man niz ʙo sumo muntazir memonam!»
11|94|Cun amri Mo faro rasid, Su'ajʙ va kasonero, ki ʙa u imon ovarda ʙudand, ʙa rahmati xud rahonidem. Va sitamkoronro farjodi saxte furu girift va dar xonahoi xes ʙar coj murdand
11|95|cunon ki gujo hargiz dar on dijor naʙudaand. Ogoh ʙos, la'nat ʙar mardumi Madjan ʙod, hamcunon ki la'nat ʙar qavmi Samud
11|96|Va Mo Musoro hamroh ʙo ojotu huccati oskori xud firistodem
11|97|ʙa nazdi Fir'avn va ʙuzurgoni qavmas. Ammo onon pajravi farmoni Fir'avn sudand. Va farmoni Fir'avn ʙa rohi savoʙ roh namenamud
11|98|Dar ruzi qijomat pesopesi qavmi xud ʙijojad va hamaro ʙa otas darovarad, ki doxilsudagonro ʙad cojgohest
11|99|La'nati incahoni va la'nati ruzi qijomatro az paj dorand va ci ʙad atoe ʙa onon doda sudast
11|100|Inho axʙori dehahoest, ki ʙaroi tu hikojat mekunem; dehahoe, ki ʙa'ze hanuz ʙarpojand va ʙa'ze vajron
11|101|Mo ʙa onho sitam nakardem, ʙalki xud ʙa xud sitam mekardand. Va cun amri Parvardigori tu faro rasid, xudojone, ki ʙa coi Xudoi jakto meparastidand, hec darkorason najomadand va cuz zijonkori cize ʙar onon najafzudand
11|102|Incunin ʙud ʙa azoʙ giriftani Parvardigori tu, vaqte ki ʙixohad dehae sitamkorro ʙa azoʙ kasad. Ba azoʙ giriftani U azoʙe saxt dardovar ast
11|103|Dar inho ʙaroi kasone, ki az azoʙi oxirat ʙimnokand, iʙratest, dar on ruz, ki mardum gird ovarda savand va on ruz, ki mardumro dar on hozir ovarand
11|104|Va cuz to andak muddate ʙa deras nameguzorem
11|105|Ruze, ki cun ʙijojad, hec kas cuz ʙa farmoni U suxan nagujad va mardumon ʙa'ze ʙadʙaxt ʙosand va ʙa'ze nekʙaxt
11|106|Ammo ʙadʙaxton dar otasand va mardumonro dar on co nolae zoru farjode saxt ʙuvad
11|107|Va to osmonhovu zamin ʙoqi hastand, dar on co covidona ʙimonand, magar on ci Parvardigorat ʙixohad, zero Parvardigori tu har ci xohad, hamon kunad
11|108|Ammo nekʙaxton to osmonhovu zamin ʙoqi hastand, dar ʙihist covidon ʙimonand; ƣajri on ci Parvardigorat ʙixohad. Atoi U hec qat' namesavad
11|109|Az on ci inho meparastand, ʙa sakku suʙha maʙos. Cuz ʙa on guna, ki padaronason pes az in meparastidand, nameparastand. Mo nasiʙi ononro ʙe hec kamukost ado xohem kard
11|110|Ba Muso kitoʙ dodem. Dar on kitoʙ ixtilof sud. Agar na hukme ʙud, ki pes az coniʙi Parvardigorat sodir suda ʙud, mijonason dovari suda ʙud, ki onho dar on kitoʙ saxt dar suʙhaand
11|111|Va Parvardigori tu cazoi a'moli hamaro ʙa tamomi xohad dod va Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekunand, ogoh ast
11|112|Hamroh ʙo onon, ki ʙo tu ru ʙa Xudo kardaand, hamcunon, ki amr sudai, soʙitqadam ʙos. Va az had naguzared, ki U ʙa har kore, ki mekuned, ʙinost
11|113|Ba sitamkoron majl nakuned, ki otas ʙisuzonadaton. Sumoro ƣajri Xudo hec duste nest va kase joriaton nakunad
11|114|Namoz ʙiguzor dar oƣozu ancomi ruz va so'ate az saʙ. Zero nekiho ʙadihoro az mijon meʙarand. In pandest ʙaroi pandgirandagon
11|115|Saʙr kun, zero Xudovand muzdi nekukoronro taʙoh namesozad
11|116|Caro dar mijoni mardumone, ki pes az sumo ʙudand, ƣajri andake, ki az on mijon nacotason dodem, xiradmandone naʙudand, to mardumonro az fasod kardan dar zamin ʙozdorand? Zolimon az pai osudagivu lazzati dunjo raftand va gunahkor ʙudand
11|117|Parvardigori tu hec dehaero, ki mardumas nekukor ʙosand, ʙa sitam halok naxohad soxt
11|118|Va agar Parpardigori tu xosta ʙud, hamai mardumro jak ummat karda ʙud, vale xamesa gunogun xohand ʙud
11|119|magar onhoe, ki Parvardigorat ʙar onho rahmat ovarda va onhoro ʙaroi hamin ʙijofaridaast. Va suxani Parvardigori tu ʙar in muqarrar suda, ki cahannamro az hamai cinnu ins pur mekunam
11|120|Har xaʙare az axʙori pajomʙaronro ʙarojat hikojat mekunem, to turo qavidil gardonem. Va dar in kitoʙ ʙar tu suxani haq va ʙaroi mu'minon pandu nasihat nozil sudaast
11|121|Ba kasone, ki imon nameovarand, ʙigu: «Sumo ʙa ci tarz, ki xohed, amal kuned, mo niz amal mekunem
11|122|Sumo intizor ʙikased, mo niz muntazir memonem!»
11|123|Va az oni Xudost nihoni osmonhovu zamin va ʙa U ʙozgardonda mesavad hamai korho. Uro ʙiparast va ʙar U tavakkal kun, ki Parvardirorat az on ci ʙa coj meovared, ƣofil nest
12|1|Alif, lom, ro. Inhost ojoti kitoʙi ravsangar
12|2|Mo Qur'one araʙi nozilas kardaem, ʙosad, ki sumo darjoʙed
12|3|Bo in Qur'on, ki ʙa tu vahj kardaem, ʙehtarin dostonro ʙarojat hikojat mekunem, ki tu az in pes az ʙexaʙaron ʙudai
12|4|On goh, ki Jusuf ʙa padari xud guft: «Ej padar, man dar xoʙ jozdah sitora va xursed va moh didam, didam, ki sacdaam mekunand»
12|5|Guft: «Ej pisari xurdakam, xoʙatro ʙaroi ʙarodaronat hikojat makun, ki turo hilae meandesand, Zero sajton odamijonro dusmane oskor ast
12|6|Va incunin Parvardigorat turo ʙarmeguzinad va ta'ʙiri xoʙ meomuzad va hamcunon, ki ne'mati xudro pes az in ʙar padaroni tu Iʙrohimu Ishoq komil karda ʙud, ʙar tuvu xonadoni Ja'quʙ ham komil mekunad, ki Parvardigorat donovu hakim ast!»
12|7|Dar dostoni Jusuf va ʙarodaronas ʙaroi onon, ki az on pursidaand, iʙrathost
12|8|On goh, ki guftand: «Jusuf va ʙarodaras nazdi padaramon mahʙuʙtar az mo hastand, hol on ki mo xud guruhe nerumandem. Padaramon dar gumrohii oskorest»
12|9|«Jusufro ʙikused jo dar sarzamine digaras ʙiandozed, to padar xosi sumo gardad va az on pas mardume soista garded»
12|10|Jake az onho guft: «Agar mexohed kore kuned, Jusufro nakused; dar qa'ri toriki cohas ʙipartoed, to korvone uro ʙigirad»
12|11|Guftand: Ej padar, ci sud, ki moro ʙar Jusuf ʙovari namekuni, hol on ki mo xajrxohi u hastem
12|12|Fardo uro ʙo mo ʙifirist, to ʙigardadu ʙozi kunad va mo nigahdoras hastem»
12|13|Guft: «Agar uro ʙiʙared, ƣamgin mesavam va metarsam, ki az u ƣofil saved va gurg uro ʙixurad»
12|14|Guftand: «Bo in guruhi nerumand, ki mo hastem, agar gurg uro ʙixurad, az zijonkoron xohem ʙud»
12|15|Cun uro ʙurdand va qasd kardand, ki dar qa'ri toriki cohas ʙijafkanand, ʙa u vahj kardem, ki onhoro az in korason ogoh xohi soxt va xud nadonand
12|16|Saʙhangom girjon nazdi padarason ʙoz omadand
12|17|Guftand: «Ej padar, mo ʙa asp toxtan rafta ʙudem va Jusufro nazdi mato'i xud guzosta ʙudem, gurg uro xurd. Va harcand ham, ki rost ʙiguem, tu suxani moro ʙovar nadori»
12|18|Comaasro, ki ʙa xuni duruƣin oƣusta ʙud, ovardand, guft: «Nafsi sumo korero dar nazaraton ʙijorosta ast. Aknun ʙaroi man saʙri camil ʙehtar ast va Xudost, ki dar in ʙora az u jori ʙojad xost»
12|19|Korvone omad. Oʙovarasonro firistodand. Satil furu kard. Guft: «Muƶdagoni, in pisarest». Uro cun mato'e pinhon soxtand va Xudo ʙa kore, ki mekardand, ogoh ʙud
12|20|Uro ʙa ʙahoi andak, ʙa cand dirham furuxtand, ki hec raƣʙate ʙa u nadostand
12|21|Kase az mardumi Misr, ki uro xarida ʙud, ʙa zanas guft: «To dar in cost, giromijas ʙidor, sojad ʙa mo sude ʙirasonad, jo uro ʙa farzandi ʙipazirem». Va incunin Jusufro dar zamin coj dodem, to ʙa u ta'ʙiri xoʙ omuzem. Va Xudo ʙar kori xes ƣoliʙ ast. Vale ʙestari mardum namedokand
12|22|Va cun ʙoliƣ sud, hikmatu donisas dodem va nekukoronro incunin mukofot medihem
12|23|Va on zan, ki Jusuf dar xonaas ʙud, dar pai komcui az Jusuf meʙud. Va darhoro ʙastu guft: «Bisitoʙ». Guft: «Panoh meʙaram ʙa Xudo, U parvaronandai man ast va maro oʙrui neku doda va sitamkoron nacotjofta namesavand»
12|24|On zan majli u kard. Va agar ʙurhoni Parvardigorasro nadida ʙud, u niz majli on zan mekard. Cunin kardem, to ʙadivu zistkoriro az vaj ʙozgardonem. Zero u az ʙakdagoni pokdili Mo ʙud
12|25|Har du ʙa coniʙi dar davidand va zan comai uro az pas ʙidarid. Va sui on zanro nazdiki dar didand. Zan guft: «Cazoi kase, ki ʙo zani tu qasdi ʙade dosta ʙosad, cist, cuz in ki ʙa zindon aftad jo ʙa azoʙe dardovar giriftor ojad?»
12|26|Jusuf guft: «U dar pai komcui az man ʙud va maro ʙa xud xond». Va jake az kasoni zan guvohi dod, ki agar comaas az pes daridaast, zan rost megujad va u duruƣgust
12|27|Va agar comaas az pas daridaast, zan duruƣ megujad va u rostgust
12|28|Cun did comaas az pas daridaast, guft: «In az makri sumo zanon ast, ki makri sumo zanon makre ʙuzurg ast
12|29|Ej Jusuf, zaʙoni xud nigoh dor va ej zan, az gunohi xud ʙaxsois ʙixoh, ki tu az xatokoroni»
12|30|Zakoni sahr guftand: «Zani Aziz dar pai komcui az ƣulomi xud sudaast va seftai u gasta ast. Mo vajro dar gumrohii oskoro meʙipem»
12|31|Cun afsunasonro sunid, nazdason kas firistod va maclise tartiʙ dod va ʙa har jak korde dod va guft: «Berun oj, to turo ʙingarand». Cun uro didand, ʙuzurgas sumurdand va dasti xes ʙiʙuridand va guftand: «Ma'ozalloh in odami nest, in faristae ʙuzurgvor ast!»
12|32|Guft: «In hamon ast, ki maro dar ʙoʙi u malomat mekarded. Man dar pai komcui az u ʙudam va u xudro nigoh dost. Agar on ci farmonas mediham, nakunad, ʙa zindon xohad aftod va xor xohad sud»
12|33|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, ʙaroi man zindon dust dostanitar ast az on ci maro ʙa on mexonand va agar makri in zanonro az man nagardoni, ʙa onho majl mekunam va dar sumori nodonon darmeojam»
12|34|Parvardigoras du'ojasro icoʙat kard va makri zanon az u dur kard. Zero Xudo sunavovu donost
12|35|Pas ʙo on nisonaho, ki dida ʙudand, tasmim kardand, ki cande ʙa zindonas ʙijafkanand
12|36|Du cavon niz ʙo u ʙa zindon aftodand. Jake az on du guft: «Dar xoʙ xudro didam, ki angur mefisoram». Digare guft: «Xudro didam, ki non ʙar sar nihoda meʙaram va parrandagon az on mexurand. Moro az ta'ʙiri on ogoh kun, ki az nekukoronat meʙinem»
12|37|Guft: «Ta'omi ruzonai sumo hanuz naomada ʙosad, ki pes az on sumoro az ta'ʙiri on xoʙho, cunon ki Parvardigoram ʙa man omuxtaast, xaʙar mediham. Man dini mardumero, ki ʙa Xudoi jakto imon nadorand va ʙa ruzi qijomat kofirand, tark kardaam
12|38|Man pajravi dini padaronam Iʙrohimu Ishoqu Ja'quʙ hastam va moro nasojad, ki hec cizro sariki Xudo qaror dihem. In fazilatest, ki Xudo ʙar movu ʙar mardumi digar arzoni dostaast, vale ʙestari mardum nosukrand
12|39|Ej du zindoni, ojo xudojoni parokanda ʙehtar ast jo Olloh — on Xudovandi jaktoi ƣoliʙ ʙar hamagon
12|40|Nameparasted ƣajri Xudoi jakto magar ʙutonero, ki xud va padaronaton onhoro ʙa nomhoe xondaed va Xudo huccate ʙar isʙoti onho nozil nakardaast. Hukm cuz hukmi Xudo nest. Farmon dodaast, ki cuz uro naparasted. In ast dini rostu ustuvor, vale ʙestari mardum namedonand
12|41|Ej du zindoni, ammo jake az sumo ʙaroi xocai xud saroʙ rezad, ammo digarero ʙar dor kunand va parrandagon sari u ʙixurand. Kore, ki dar ʙorai on nazar mexosted, ʙa pojon omadaast»
12|42|Ba jake az on du, ki medonnst, raho mesavad, guft: «Maro nazdi xocai xud jod kun!» Ammo sajton az xotiras dur kard, ki pesi mavlojas az u jod kunad va cand sol dar zindon ʙimond
12|43|Podsoh guft: «Dar xoʙ haft govi farʙehro didam, ki onhoro haft govi loƣar mexurand va haft xusai saʙz didam va haft xusai xusk. Ej xosagoni man, xoʙi maro ta'ʙir kuned, agar ta'ʙiri xoʙ medoned»
12|44|Guftand: «Inho xoʙhoi osuftaast va moro ʙa ta'ʙiri in xoʙho ogohi nest»
12|45|Jake az on du, ki raho suda ʙud va pas az muddate ʙa jodas omada ʙud, guft: «Man sumoro az ta'ʙiri on ogoh mekunam. Maro nazdi u ʙifiristed»
12|46|«Ej Jusuf, ej mardi rostguj, ʙaroi mo ta'ʙir kun, ki haft govi farʙehro haft govi loƣar mexurand va haft xusai saʙzu haft xusai xusk. Bosad, ki man nazdi mardum ʙozgardam va onon ogoh gardand»
12|47|Guft: «Haft sol paj dar paj ʙikored va har ci medaraved, cuz andake, ki mexured, ʙo xusa anʙor kuned
12|48|Az on pas haft sol kaxti meojad va dar on haft sol on ci ʙarojason cam' kardaand, ʙixurand ƣajri andake, ki nigoh medored
12|49|Pas az on sole ojad, ki mardumonro ʙoron dihand va dar on sol afsurdanihoro mefusurand»
12|50|Podsoh guft: «Nazdi manas ʙijovared». Cun firistoda nazdi u omad, Jusuf guft: «Nazdi xocaat ʙozgard va ʙipurs: Hikojati on zanon, ki dasthoi xudro ʙuridand, ci ʙud? Ki Parvardigori man ʙa makrason ogoh ast!»
12|51|Guft: «Ej zanon, on goh ki xostori tani Jusuf meʙuded, hikojati sumo ci ʙud?» Guftand: «Panoh ʙar Xudo! Uro hec gunahkor namedonem». Zani Aziz guft: «Aknun haq oskor sud. Man dar pai komcui az u meʙudam va u dar zumrai rostgujon ast!»
12|52|«Cunin sud to ʙidonad, ki man dar ƣajʙatas ʙa u xijonat nakardaam va Xudo hilai xoinonro ʙa maqsad namerasozdad
12|53|Man xudamro ʙegunoh namedonam, zero nafs odamiro ʙa ʙadi farmon medihad. Magar Parvardigori man ʙiʙaxsojad, zero Parvardigori man omurzandavu mehruʙon ast!»
12|54|Podsoh guft: «Uro nazdi man ʙijovared to hamnisini xosi xud gar donam». Va cun ʙo u suxan guft, guft; «Tu az imruz nazdi mo sohiʙmartaʙa va ʙovarinok hasti»
12|55|Guft: «Maro ʙar xazinahoi in sarzamin muqarrar kun, ki man nigahʙone donojam»
12|56|Incunin Jusufro dar on sarzamin oʙru dodem. Har co, ki mexost, coj megirift. Rahmati xudro ʙa har kas, ki ʙixohem, arzoni medorem va muzdi nekukoronro ʙarʙod namekunem
12|57|Va alʙatta muzdi oncahoni ʙaroi kasone, ki imop ovardaand va parhezgori mekunand, ʙehtar ast
12|58|Barodaroni Jusuf omadand va ʙar u doxil sudand, onhoro sinoxt va onho nasinoxtandas
12|59|Cun ʙorhojasonro muhajjo soxt, guft: «Barodari padarijatonro niz nazdi man ʙijovared, ojo nameʙined, ki pajmonaro komil ado mekunam va ʙehtarin mizʙonam
12|60|Agar uro nazdi man najovared, pajmonae nazdi man naxohed dost va ʙa man nazdik masaved»
12|61|Guftand: «Mo uro ʙa isror az padar xohem xost va in korro xohem kard»
12|62|Va ʙa mardoni xud guft: «Sarmojaasonro dar ʙorhojason ʙinihed, ʙosad, ki cun nazdi kasonason ʙozgardand va onro ʙijoʙand, ʙoz ojand»
12|63|Cun nazdi padar ʙozgastand, guftand: «Ej padar, pajmona az mo man' namudand. Barodaramonro ʙo mo ʙifirist, to pajmona ʙozgirem. Mo nigahdori u hastem»
12|64|Guft: «Ojo uro ʙa sumo ʙisuporam, hamcunon ki ʙarodarasro pes az in ʙa sumo supurdam?» Xudo ʙehtarin nigahdor ast va Ust mehruʙontarini mehruʙonon
12|65|Cun ʙori xudro kusudand, didand, ki sarmojaasonro pas dodaand. Guftand: «Ej padar, dar talaʙi ci hastem? In sarmojai most, ki ʙa mo pas dodaand. Baroi kasoni xud ƣalla ʙijovarem va ʙarodaramonro hifz kunem va ʙori suture afzun girem, ki on ci dorem, andak ast»
12|66|Guft: «Hargiz uro ʙo sumo namefiristam, to ʙo man ʙa nomi Xudo pajmone ʙiʙanded, ki nazdi manas ʙozmeovared. Magar on ki hama giriftor saved». Cun ʙo u ahd kardand, guft: «Xudo ʙar on ci meguem, guvoh ast!»
12|67|Guft: «Ej pisaroni man, az jak darvoza doxil nasaved; az darvozahoi gunogun doxil saved. Va man qazoi Xudoro az sari sumo daf' natavonam kard va hec farmone ƣajri farmoni Xudo nest. Bar U tavakkal kardam va tavakkalkunandagon ʙar U tavakkul kunand»
12|68|Cun az coe, ki padar farmon doda ʙud, doxil sudand, in kor dar ʙaroʙari irodai Xudo sudason naʙaxsid. Tanho hocate dar zamiri Ja'quʙ ʙud, ki onro oskor soxt, zero uro ilme ʙud, ki Xud ʙa u omuxta ʙudem, vale ʙestari mardum namedonand
12|69|Cun ʙar Jusuf doxil sudand, ʙarodarasro nazdi xud coj dod. Guft: «Man ʙarodari tu hastam. Az kore, ki inho kardaand, anduhgin maʙos»
12|70|Cun ʙorhojasonro muhajjo kard, comro dar ʙori ʙarodar nihod. On goh munodi (sadodihanda) sado dod: «Ej korvonijon, sumo duzdoned»
12|71|Korvonijon nazdi onho ʙozgastand va guftand: «Ci gum kardaed?»
12|72|Guftand: «Comi podsohro. Va har ki ʙijovaradas, uro ʙori suturest va man kafili mekunam»
12|73|Guftand: «Xudoro, sumo xud medoned, ki mo fasod kardan ʙa in sarzamin najomadaem va duzd naʙudaem»
12|74|Guftand: «Agar duruƣ gufta ʙosed, cazoi duzd cist?»
12|75|Guftand: «Cazojas hamon kasest, ki dar ʙori u jofta savad. Pas u xud cazoi amali xud ast va mo gunahkoronro cunin cazo dihem»
12|76|Pes az ʙori ʙarodar ʙar ʙori onho koftanro sar kard, on goh az ʙori ʙarodaras ʙerun ovard. Hilae incunin ʙa Jusuf omuxtem. Dar dini on podsoh giriftani ʙarodar xaqqi u naʙud, cize ʙud, ki Xudo mexost. Har kasro, ki ʙixohem, ʙa daracote ʙolo meʙarem va ʙoloi har donoe donotarest
12|77|Guftand: «Agar u duzdi karda, ʙarodaras niz pes az in duzdi karda ʙud». Jusuf cavoʙi on suxan dar dil pinhon dost va hec izxor nakard va guft: «Sumo dar vaz'e ʙadtar hasted va Xudo ʙa ʙuhtone, ki mezaned, ogohtar ast!»
12|78|Guftand: «Ej aziz, uro padarest solxurda. Jake az moro ʙa coi u ʙigir, ki az nekukoronat meʙinem»
12|79|Guft: «Xudo nakunad, ki cuz on kasro, ki ʙori xud nazdi u joftaem, ʙigirem. Agar cunin kunem, az sitamkoron xohem ʙud»
12|80|Cun az u noumed sudand, ʙaroi masvarat ʙa kanore raftand va ʙuzurgtarinason guft: «Ojo namedoned, ki padaraton az sumo ʙa nomi Xudo pajmon girifta va pes az in niz dar haqqi Jusuf kutohi kardaed? Man az in sarzamin ʙerun nameojam, to padar maro ruxsat dihad jo Xudo dar ʙorai man dovari kunad, ki U ʙehtarini dovaron ast
12|81|Nazdi padar ʙozgarded va ʙigued: «Ej padar, pisarat duzdi kard va mo cuz ʙa on ci medonistem, sahodat nadodem va az ƣajʙ niz ogoh nestem
12|82|Az sahre, ki dar on ʙudaem va az korvone, ki hamrohas omadaem ʙipurs, ki mo rost meguem»
12|83|Guft: «Na, nafsi sumo korero dar nazaraton ʙijorost va maro saʙri camil ʙehtar ast. Sojad Xudo hamaro ʙa man ʙozgardonad, ki U donovu hakim ast!»
12|84|Rui xud az onho ʙigardonidu guft: «Ej anduho ʙar Jusuf». Va casmonas az ƣam sapedi girift va hamcunon anduhi xud furu mexurd
12|85|Guftand: «Ba Xudo savgand pajvasta Jusufro jod mekuni, to ʙemor gardi jo ʙimiri»
12|86|Guft; «Cuz in nest, ki sarhi anduhi xud tanho ʙo Xudo megujam. Zero on ci man az Xudo medonam, sumo namedoned
12|87|Ej pisaroni man, ʙiravedu Jusuf va ʙarodarasro ʙicued va az rahmati Xudo noumed masaved. Zero tanho kofiron az rahmati Xudo ma'jus mesavand»
12|88|Cun ʙar Jusuf doxil sudand, guftand: «Ej aziz, movu kasonamon ʙa gurusnagi aftodaem va ʙo sarmojai andak omadaem, pajmonai moro tamom ado kun va ʙar mo sadaqa ʙideh zero Xudo sadaqadihandagonro dust dorad!»
12|89|Guft: «Medoned, ki az rui nodoni ʙo Jusuf va ʙarodaras ci karded?»
12|90|Guftand: «Ojo ʙa haqiqat tu Jusufi?» Guft: «Man Jusufam va in ʙarodari man ast va Xudo ʙa mo ne'mat dod. Zero har kas, ki parhezgori kunad va saʙr namojad, Xudo muzdasro noʙud namesozad»
12|91|Guftand: «Ba Xudo savgand, ki xudo turo ʙar mo fazilat dod va mo xatokor ʙudem»
12|92|Guft: «Imruz sumoro sarzanis naʙojad kard; Xudo sumoro meʙaxsojad, ki U mehruʙontarini mehruʙonon ast
12|93|In comai maro ʙiʙared va ʙar rui padaram andozed to ʙino gardad. Va hamai kasoni xudro nazdi man ʙijovared»
12|94|Cun korvon ʙa roh aftod, padarason guft: «Agar maro devona naxoned, ʙui Jusuf his mekunam»
12|95|Guftand: «Ba Xudo savgand, ki tu dar hamon gumrohii derinan xud hasti!»
12|96|Cun muƶdadihanda omad va coma ʙar rui u andoxt, ʙino gast. Guft: «Ojo naguftamaton, ki on ci man az Xudo medonam, sumo namedoned?»
12|97|Guftand: «Ej padar, ʙaroi gunohoni mo omurzis ʙixoh, ki mo xatokor ʙudaem»
12|98|Guft; «Az Parvardigoram ʙaroi sumo ʙaxsois xoham xost, U ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast!»
12|99|Cun ʙar Jusuf doxil sudand, padaru modarro ʙa oƣus kasidu guft: «Ba Misr daroed, ki agar Xudo ʙixohad, dar amon xohed ʙud!»
12|100|Padaru modarro ʙar taxt ʙarovard va hama dar ʙaroʙari u ʙa sacda daromadand. Guft: «Ej padar, in ast ta'ʙiri on xoʙi man, ki inak Parvardigoram onro rost ʙarovard. Va ci qadar ʙa man neki kardaast, on goh, ki maro az zindon ʙirahonid va pas az on, ki sajton mijoni manu ʙarodaronam fasod karda ʙud, sumoro az ʙodija ʙa in co ovard. Parvardigori man ʙa har ci iroda kunad, daqiq ast, ki U donovu hakim ast
12|101|Ej Parvardigori man, maro farmonravoi dodi va maro ilmi ta'ʙiri xoʙ omuxti. Ej ofarinandai osmonhovu zamin, tu dar dunjovu oxirat korsozi mani. Maro musalmon ʙimiron va qarini soistagon soz!»
12|102|Inho xaʙarhoi ƣajʙ ast, ki ʙa tu vahj mekunem. Va on hangom, ki ʙo jakdigar gird omada ʙudand va masvarat mekardand va xila mesoxtand, tu nazdi onho naʙudi
12|103|Harcand tu ʙa imonason haris ʙosi, ʙestari mardum imon nameovarand
12|104|Va tu dar muqoʙili pajomʙarijat az onho muzde nametalaʙi va in kitoʙ cuz pande ʙaroi mardumi cahon nest
12|105|Ci ʙisjor nisonahoe dar osmonhovu zamin ast, ki ʙar on meguzarand va az on ruj ʙarmetoʙand
12|106|Va ʙestarason ʙa Xudo imon najovarand, ʙalki hamcunon musrikand
12|107|Ojo pindorand, ki emini joftaand az in, ki uquʙate umumi az azoʙi Xudo onhoro furu girad jo qijomat ʙa nogoh faro rasad, ʙe on ki xaʙardor savand
12|108|Bigu: «In rohi man ast. Manu pajravonam hamagonro ʙo dalelu huccat ʙa sui Xudo mexonem. Pok ast Xudo va man az musrikon nestam!»
12|109|Va Mo pes az tu ʙa pajƣamʙari nafiristodem magar mardonero az mardumi dehaho, ki ʙa onhovahj mekardem. Ojo dar rui zamin namegardand, to ʙingarand, ki pojoni kori pesinijonason ci ʙudaast? Va olami oxirat parhezgoronro ʙehtar ast, caro nameandesed
12|110|Cun pajomʙaron navmed sudand va cunon donistand, ki onhoro duruƣ meʙarorand, joriason kardem va har kiro, ki xostem, nacot dodem va azoʙi Mo az mardumi gunahkor ʙozgardonida nasavad
12|111|Dar dostonhojason xiradmandonro iʙratest. In dostone soxta nest, ʙalki tasdiqi suxani pesinnjon va tafsili har cizest ʙaroi onho, ki imon ovardaand, hidojat astu rahmat
13|1|Alif, lom, mim, ro. Inho ojoti in kitoʙ ast va on ci az Parvardigorat ʙar tu nozil sudaast, haq ast, vale ʙestari mardum imon nameovarand
13|2|Olloh — hamon Xudovandest, ki osmonhoro ʙe hec sutune, ki onro ʙuʙined, ʙarafrost. Sipas ʙa ars pardoxt va oftoʙu mohro, ki har jak to zamone muajjan dar sajrand, rom kard. Korhoro megardonad va ojotro ʙajon mekunad, ʙosad, ki ʙa didori Parvardigoraton jaqin kuned
13|3|Ust, ki zaminro ʙigusturd va dar on kuhxovu rudho qaror dod va az har meva cuft-cuft padid ovard va saʙro dar ruz mepusonad. Dar inho iʙrathost ʙaroi mardume, ki meandesand
13|4|Va ʙar rui zamin qit'ahoest dar kanori jakdigar va ʙoƣhoi anguru knstzorho va naxlhoe, ki dutana az jak resa rusta ast jo jaktana az jak resa va hama ʙa jak oʙ seroʙ mesavand va dar samara ʙa'zero dar ʙa'ze digar ʙartari nihodaem. Alʙatta dar inho ʙaroi xiradmandon iʙrathost
13|5|Agar tu dar hajrat meoi, taaccuʙ dar suxani onho ast, ki ojo on hangom, ki xok savem, az nav moro ʙijofarinad? Inho ʙa Parvardigorason imon nadorand, ʙar gardanhoson tavqho ʙosad va ahli cahannamand va dar on covidonaand
13|6|Ba sitoʙ az tu pes az xajru ʙaxsois azoʙ metalaʙand. Pes az onho azoʙhoe ʙudaast va Parvardigori tu mardumro, ʙo on ki sitam kardaand, meʙaxsad va niz Parvardigori tu ʙa saxti uquʙat mekunad
13|7|Kofiron megujand: «Caro az coniʙi Parvardigoras mu'cizae ʙar u nozil namesavad?» Cuz in nest, ki tu ʙimdihandae hasti va har qavmero rohnamoest
13|8|Xudo medonad, ki har zane ci dar rahm dorad va on ci rahmho kohad va on ci rahmho afzojad. Va har cizro dar nazdi U miqdore mu'ajjan ast
13|9|Donoi nihonu oskor — on Xudom ʙuzurgi ʙalandmartaʙa
13|10|Baroi U jakson ast az sumo har ki suxan ʙa pinhon gujad jo ʙa oskoro. Va on ki dar pardai saʙ pinhon mesavad va on ki dar ruz ʙa oskoro meravad
13|11|Odamiro faristagonest, ki pajopaj ʙa amri Xudo az ruʙaruvu pusti saras meojand va nigahʙonijas mekunand. Xudo cizero, ki az oni mardumest, digargun nakunad, to on mardum xud digargun savand. Cun Xudo ʙaroi mardume ʙadi xohad, hec ciz mone'i U natavonad sud va onhoro ƣajri Xudo hec korsoze nest
13|12|Ust, ki ʙarqro goh ʙaroi tarsonidan va goh ʙaroi umed ʙaxsidan ʙa sumo menamojonad va aʙrhoi garonʙorro padid meovarad
13|13|Ra'd ʙa sitoisi U va faristagon az ʙimi U tasʙeh mekunand. Va otasakhoro mefiristad va har kiro ʙixohad, ʙa on oseʙ merasonad. Boz ham dar ʙorai Xudo ʙahsu cidol mekunand. Va U ʙa saxti uquʙat mekunad
13|14|Xosi Ust duovu ilticoi rostin. Onho, ki cuz Uro iltico mekunand, hec posuxason namegujand. Monandi kase, ki du dast ʙa sui oʙ ʙarad to oʙ ʙa dahon rasonad va natavonad, ki oʙ ʙa dahon rasonad. Va du'oi kofiron cuz ʙa gumrohi nest
13|15|Xohu noxoh ʙaroi Xudovand sacda mekunand hamai onho, ki dar osmonhovu zaminand va sojahojason niz ʙomdodonu somgohon ʙa sacda meojand. (Sacda)
13|16|Bigu: «Kist Parvardigori osmonhovu zamin?» Bigu: «Olloh». Bigu; «Ojo ƣajri U xudojone giriftaed, ki qodir ʙa sudu zijoni xud nestand? Bigu: «Ojo noʙinovu ʙino ʙaroʙarand? Jo torikivu ravsani jaksonand? Jo sarikone, ki ʙaroi Xudo qoil sudaand, cizhoe ofaridaand, monandi on ci Xudo ofaridaast va onon dar ʙorai ofarinis ʙa istiʙoh aftodaand?» Bigu: «Olloh ofarinandai har cizest va U jagonavu qahhor ast!»
13|17|Az osmon oʙ firistod va har jak cuje ʙa andozai xud cori sud va oʙi ravon kaf (k) ʙar sar ovard. Va az on ci ʙar otas megudozand, to zevaru mato'e sozand, niz kafke ʙar sar ojad. Xudo ʙaroi haqqu ʙotil cunin masal zanad, Ammo kafk ʙa kanore aftad va noʙud savad va on ci ʙaroi mardum sudmand ast, dar zamin pojdor ʙimonad. Xudo incunin misol meorad
13|18|Baroi onon, ki da'vati parvardigorasonro qaʙul kardand, mukofoti nekuest. Va kasone, ki da'vati Uro qaʙul nakardand, agar har on ciro, ki ʙar rui zamin ast va monandi onro dosta ʙosand, onro fido dihand, onon ʙa saxti ʙozxost xohand sud va makonason cahannam ast va ʙad cojgohest
13|19|Ojo kase, ki medonad on ci az coniʙi Parvardigorat ʙar tu nozil suda haq ast monandi kasset, ki noʙinost? Tanho xiradmandon pand megirand
13|20|kasone, ki ʙa ahdi Xudo vafo mekunand va xud pajmon namesikanand
13|21|onon, ki on ciro Xudo ʙa pajvastani on farmon doda, pajvand mekunand va az Parvardigorason metarsand va az saxtii hisoʙi Xudovand ʙimnokand
13|22|onon, ki ʙa talaʙi savoʙi Parvardigori xud saʙr pesa kardand va namoz guzoridand va dar nihonu oskor az on ci ʙa onho ruzi dodaem, xajr kardand va ʙadiro ʙo neki ʙarmegardonand. Oqiʙati neki oxirat az onhost
13|23|Bihisthoi covidon onho va har ki nekukor ʙudaast az padaronu hamsaron va farzandonason, ʙadon doxil savand va faristagon az har dar ʙa nazdason ojand
13|24|Salom ʙar sumo ʙa xotiri on hama saʙre, ki kardaed. Saroi oxirat ci saroe nekust
13|25|Va onho, ki pajmoni Xudoro pas az ʙastanas mesikanand va on ciro, ki Xudo ʙa pajvastani on farmon doda, qat' mekunand va dar zamin fasod mekunand, la'nat ʙar onhost va ʙadihoi on cahon nasiʙason
13|26|Xudo har kiro xohad, ruzii ʙisjor dihad jo ruzii andak. Va mardum ʙa zindagii dunjo xusnudand, hol on ki zindagii dunjo dar ʙaroʙari zindagii oxirat cuz andak mato'e nest
13|27|Kofiron megujand: «Caro az coniʙi Parvardigoras mu'cizae ʙar u nozil namesavad?» Bigu: «Xudo har kiro ʙixohad, gumroh mekunad. Va har kiro ʙa dargohi U ruj kunad, hidojat mekunad»
13|28|Onhoe, ki imon ovardaand va dilhojason ʙa jodi Xudo oromis mejoʙad, ogoh ʙosed, ki dilho ʙa jodi Xudo oromis mejoʙad
13|29|Zindagii xus va ʙozgastangohi neku az oni kasonest, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand
13|30|Hamcunin turo ʙa mijoni ummate, ki pes az onxo ummathoi digar ʙudaand, ʙa pajƣamʙari firistodaem, to on ciro, ki ʙar tu vahj kardaem, ʙarojason tilovat kuni va onho ʙa Rahmon kofir mesavand. Bigu: «U Parvardigori man ast. Xudoe cuz U nest. Bar U tavakkal kardaam va tavʙai man ʙa dargohi Ust!»
13|31|Agar Qur'one tavonist ʙud, ki kuhho ʙa on ʙa cunʙis ojand jo zamin pora-pora savad, jo murdagonro ʙa suxan orad, cuz in Qur'on nameʙud, ki hamai korho az oni Xudost. Ojo mu'minon hanuz nadonistaand, ki agar Xudo mexost, hamai mardumro hidojat mekard? Va kofironro pajvasta ʙa saʙaʙi amalhojason hodisae rasad jo on hodisa dar nazdikii xonahojason furud ojad, to on goh, ki va'dai Xudo ojad, zero Xudo xilofi va'da namekunad
13|32|Pajomʙarone ham, ki pes az tu ʙudand, ʙa masxara girifta sudand. Man ʙa kofiron muhlat dodam, on goh hamaro furu giriftam va on uquʙati man ci saxt ʙud
13|33|Ojo on ki ʙar hamai mardum va amalhojason nozir ast, monandi ʙuton ast? Baroi Xudo sarikone qoil sudand. Bigu: «Onhoro nom ʙiʙared. Sojad mexohed Uro az cize dar rui zamin ogoh kuned, ki namedonad, jo suxanoni ʙehuda megujand?» Dar nazari kofiron makrason orosta omad va az rohi rost ʙeroh sudand. Va har kiro Xudo gumroh kunad, hec rohnamoe nadorad
13|34|Dar in zindagii dunjo ʙa azoʙe giriftor ojand va azoʙi oxirat saxttar ast va onhoro hec nigahdorandae az azoʙi Xudo nest
13|35|Sifati ʙihiste, ki ʙa parhezgoron va'da suda: oʙ az zeri daraxtonas ravon ast va mevahovu sojaas hamesagist. In sarancomi kasonest, ki parhezgorand va sarancomi kofiron otas ast
13|36|Ahli kitoʙ az on ci ʙar tu nozil suda, sodmonand. Va az on camo'at kasone hastand, ki ʙa'ze az onro inkor mekunand. Bigu: «Man amr sudaam, ki Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparastam va ʙa U sirk najovaram. Ba sui U da'vat mekunam va ʙozgasti man ʙa sui Ust
13|37|Hamcunin Qur'onro ʙa zaʙoni araʙi nozil kardem. Agar pas az donise, ki ʙa tu rasida, az pai xohishoi onho ʙiravi, dar ʙaroʙari azoʙi Xudo korsozu nigahdorandae naxohi dost
13|38|Ba tahqiq pes az tu pajomʙarone firistodaem va ʙarojason hamsaronu farzandon qaror dodaem. Va hec pajomʙarero haqqi on naʙud, ki cuz ʙa farmoni Xudo ojate ʙijovarad va har amrero zamone navistasuda ast
13|39|Xudo har ciro ʙixohad, mahv jo isʙot mekunad va ummulkitoʙ nazdi Ust
