20|68|Guftem; «Matars, ki tu ʙolotar hasti
20|69|On ci dar dasti rost dori, ʙijafkan, to har ciro, ki soxtaand, furu ʙarad. Onon hilai coduvon soxtaand va codugar hec goh piruz namesavad»
20|70|Sohiron ʙa sacda vodor sudand. Guftand: «Ba Parvardigori Horunu Muso imon ovardem»
20|71|Fir'avn guft: «Ojo pes az on, ki sumoro ruxsat diham, ʙa U imon ovarded? U ʙuzurgi sumost, ki ʙa sumo codugari omuxtaast. Dasthovu pohotonro az capu rost meʙuram va ʙar tanai daraxti xurmo ʙa doraton meovezam to ʙidoned, ki azoʙi kadom jak az mo saxttaru pojandatar ast»
20|72|Guftand: «Savgand ʙa on ki moro ofaridaast, ki turo ʙar on nisonahoi ravsan, ki didaem, tarceh namedihem (ʙehtar namesumorem), ʙa har ci xohi, hukm kun, ki rivoci hukmi tu dar zindagii incahonist
20|73|Inak ʙa Parvardigori xud imon ovardem to az xatohoi mo va on codugari, ki moro ʙa on vodosti, darguzarad, ki Xudo ʙehtaru pojdortar ast»
20|74|Alʙatta har kas, ki gunahkor nazdi Parvardigoras ʙijojad, cahannam cojgohi ust, ki dar on co na memirad va na zindagi mekunad
20|75|Va onon, ki ʙo imon nazdi u ojand va korhoi soista kunand, sohiʙi daracote ʙaland ʙosand
20|76|Bihisthoi covidon, ki dar on nahrho ravon ast va aʙadi dar on co ʙosand. Va in ast muzdi pokon
20|77|Ba Muso vahj kardem, ki ʙandagoni Moro saʙhangom ʙerun ʙiʙar va ʙarojason (ʙo mu'ciza) dar darjo guzargohe xusk ʙicuj va matars, ki ʙar tu dast joʙand va ʙim ʙa dil roh madeh
20|78|Firʹavn, ʙo laskarhojas az pajason ravon sud. Va darjo cunon, ki ʙojad, ononro dar xud furu pusid
20|79|Fir'avn qavmasro gumrox kard, na rohnamoi
20|80|«Ej ʙani-Isroil, sumoro az dusmanaton rahonidem va ʙo sumo dar coniʙi rosti kuhi Tur va'da nihodem va ʙarojaton manna (sirini) va salvo (ʙedona) nozil kardem
20|81|Az cizhoi pokiza, ki sumoro ruzi dodaem, ʙixured va az had meguzaronedas, to maʙod xasmi Man ʙa sumo rasad, ki har kas, ki xasmi Man ʙa u ʙirasad, dar otas aftad
20|82|Har kas, ki tavʙa kunad va imon ovarad va kori soista kunad va ʙa rohi hidojat ʙijaftad, uro meʙaxsoem
20|83|Ej Muso, ci ciz turo vodost, to ʙar qavmat pesi giri?» (ja'ne az qavmat pestar ʙijoi)
20|84|Guft: «Onho hamonhojand, ki az pai man ravonand. Ej Parvardigori man, man ʙa sui Tu sitoftam, to xusnud gardi»
20|85|Guft: «Mo qavmi turo pas az tu ozmois kardem va Somiri gumrohason soxt»
20|86|Muso xasmgin va puranduh nazdi qavmas ʙozgastu guft: «Ej qavmi man, ojo Parvardigoraton sumoro va'dahoi neku nadoda ʙud? Ojo der kardani man daroz kasid jo xosted, ki xasmi Parvardigoraton ʙa sumo furud ojad, ki va'dai maro xilof karded?»
20|87|Guftand; «Mo ʙa ixtijori xud va'dai tu xilof nakardem. Az zaru zevari on qavm ʙardostem. Onhoro dar otas andoxtem. Va Somiri niz andoxt
20|88|Va ʙarojason tandisi (pajkarai) gusolae, ki na'rai govonro dost, ʙisoxt va guftand: «In xudoi sumo va xudoi Musost. Va Muso faromus karda ast»
20|89|Ojo namedonand, ki hec posuxe ʙa suxanason namedihad va hec naf'u zijone ʙarojason nadorad
20|90|Horun niz pes az in ʙa onho gufta ʙud: «Ej qavmi man, sumoro ʙa in gusola ozmudaand. Parvardigori sumo Xudoi rahmon ast. Az pai man ʙijoed va farmonʙardori man ʙosed!»
20|91|Guftand; «Mo hamesa ʙa parastisi u menisinem, to Muso ʙa nazdi mo ʙozgardad»
20|92|Guft: «Ej Horun, hangome ki didi gumroh mesavand
20|93|caro az pai man naomadi? Ojo tu niz az farmoni man sarpeci karda ʙudi?»
20|94|Guft: «Ej pisari modaram, cang ʙar risu sari man majandoz. Man tarsidam, ki ʙigui: «Tu mijoni ʙani-Isroil cudoi afkandi va guftori maro riojat nakardi»
20|95|Guft: «Va tu, ej Somiri, in ci kore ʙud, ki kardi?»
20|96|Guft: «Man cize didam, ki onho namedidand. Muste az xoke, ki naqsi poi on rasul (Ciʙriil) ʙar on ʙud, ʙargiriftam va dar on qolaʙ afkandam va nafsi man in korro dar casmi man ʙijorost»
20|97|Guft: «Birav, dar zindagii in dunjo cunon savi, ki pajvasta ʙiguj: «Ba man nazdik masav». Va niz turo va'daest, ki! az on raho nasavi va inak ʙa xudojat, ki pajvasta iʙodatas mekardi, ʙingar, ki mesuzonemas va ʙa darjoas meafsonem
20|98|Cuz in nest, ki xudoi sumo Olloh ast, ki hec xudoe ƣajri U nest va ilmas hama cizro dar ʙar giriftaast»
20|99|Incunin xaʙarhoi guzastaro ʙaroi tu hikojat mekunem. Va ʙa tu az coniʙi Xud Qur'onro ato kardem
20|100|Har kas, ki az on ruj gardonad, ruzi qijomat ʙori gunoh ʙar dus mekasad
20|101|Dar on kor xamesa ʙimonand. Va ʙori, ruzi qijomat ʙarojason ʙori ʙadest
20|102|Ruze, ki dar sur damida savad va gunahkoronro dar on ruz kaʙudcasm gird meovarem
20|103|Ohista ʙo ham suxan megujand, ki dah ruz ʙes dar dunjo naistodaed
20|104|Mo ʙar guftori onho ogohtarem, on goh ki nekuravistarini onho megujad: «Cuz jak ruz naistodaed»
20|105|Turo az kuhho mepursand. Bigu: «Parvardigori man hamaro parokanda mesozad
20|106|va onhoro ʙa zamine hamvor ʙadal mekunad
20|107|dar on hec kacivu pastivu ʙalandi nameʙini»
20|108|Dar on ruz az pai on do'i (Isrofil), ki hec kaciro dar u roh nest, ravon gardand. Va sadoho dar ʙaroʙari Xudoi rahmon past mesavand va az hec kas ƣajri sadoi poe naxohi sunid
20|109|Dar on ruz safo'at naf' nadihad, faqat onro, ki Xudoi rahmon icozat dihad va suxanasro ʙipisandad, naf' dihad
20|110|Har ciro dar pesi rui onhost va har ciro dar pusti sarason ast medonad va ilmi onon Uro dar ʙar nagirad
20|111|Va cehraho dar ʙaroʙari Xudoi zindai pojanda xoze' (mute') mesavad va har ki ʙori kufr ʙar dus mekasad, noumed megardad
20|112|Va har kas, ki korhoi soista kunad va mu'min ʙosad, naʙojad az hec sitame va sikaste ʙitarsad
20|113|Incunin onro Qur'one araʙi nozil kardem va dar on gunogun xusdor dodem, sojad ʙitarsand jo pande toza girand
20|114|Pas ʙartar ast Xudoi jakto- on podsohi rostin! Va pes az on ki vahj ʙa pojon rasad, dar xondani Qur'on sitoʙ makun. Va ʙigu: «Ej Parvardigori man, ʙa ilmi man ʙijafzoj»
20|115|Va mo pes az in ʙo Odam pajmon ʙastem, vale faromus kard va ʙosaʙras najoftem
20|116|Va on goh, ki ʙa faristagon guftem: «Odamro sacda kuned». Hama ƣajri Iʙlis, ki sarpeci kard, sacda kardand
20|117|Guftem: «Ej Odam, in dusmani tu va hamsari tust, sumoro az ʙihist ʙerun nakunad, ki ʙadʙaxt savi
20|118|ki tu dar ʙihist na gurusna mesavi va na ʙarahna memoni
20|119|va na tasna mesavi va na ducori toʙisi oftoʙ»
20|120|Sajton vasvasaas kardu guft: «Ej Odam, ojo turo ʙa daraxti covidoni va mulki durnasavanda roh ʙinamojam?»
20|121|Az on daraxt xurdand va sarmgohason dar nazarason padidor sud. Va hamcunon ʙargi daraxtoni ʙihist ʙar onho mecasponidand. Odam ʙa Parvardigori xud osi sud va roh gum kard

20|127|Incunin isrofkoron va kasonero, ki ʙa ojoti Parvardigorason imon nameovarand, cazo medihem. Alʙatta azoʙi oxirat saxttaru pojdortar ast
20|128|Ojo on hama mardume, ki pes az in dar masokini inho roh meraftand va Mo hamaro halok kardem, saʙaʙi hidojati inho nasudaand? Inho nisonahoest ʙaroi xiradmandon
20|129|Agar na suxane ʙud, ki Parvardigorat pes az in gufta va zamonro mu'ajjan karda ʙud, azoʙason dar in cahon hatmi meʙud

20|131|Agar zanonu mardone az onhoro az jak zindagii xus ʙahramand soxtaem, tu ʙa onho manigar. In ʙaroi on ast, ki imtihonason kunem. Rizqi Parvardigorat ʙehtaru pojdortar ast
20|132|Kasoni xudro ʙa namoz farmon deh va xud dar on kor ʙosaʙr ʙos. Az tu ruzi namexohem. Mo ʙa tu ruzi medihem. Va oqiʙati nek az oni parhezgoron ast
20|133|Va guftand: «Caro mu'cizae az Parvardigoras ʙaroi mo nameovarad?» Ojo dalelhoi ravsane, ki dar saxifahoi pesin omada, ʙa onho narasidaast
20|134|Agar pes az omadani Pajomʙare azoʙason mekardem, meguftand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, caro rasule ʙar mo nafiristodi to pes az on ki ʙa xorivu rasvoi aftem, az ojoti tu pajravi kunem?»
20|135|Bigu: «Hama muntazirand, sumo niz muntazir ʙimoned. Ba zudi xohed donist, onho, ki ʙa rohi rost meravand va onho, ki hidojat joftaand, ci kasone hastand»
21|1|Ruzi hisoʙi mardum nazdik sud va onon hamcunon ʙa ƣaflat rujgardonand
21|2|Az sui Parvardigorason ʙarojason har pande tozae omad, onro sunidand va sargarmi ʙozica ʙudand
21|3|Dilhojason ƣofil sudaast. Va on sitamgaron sar dar gusi jakdigar nihodandu pinhoni guftand: «Ojo in mard jak insone monandi sumo nest? Ojo ʙo on ki ʙa casmn xud meʙined, hamcunon az pai codu meraved?»
21|4|Guft: «Parvardigori man az har suxane dar osmonu zamin ogoh ast va U sunavovu donost»
21|5|Guftand: «Na Xoʙhoi pareson ast jo duruƣest, ki meʙofad jo soirest. Pas ʙaroi mo az on guna, ki ʙa pajomʙaroni pesin doda suda ʙud, mu'cizae ʙijovarad»
21|6|Pes az onho mardumi dehaero, ki halok kardem, imon najovarda ʙudand. Ojo inho imon meovarand
21|7|Mo pes az tu ʙa pajramʙari faqat mardonero, ki ʙa onho vahj mekardem firistodem va agar xud namedoned, az ahli kitoʙ ʙipursed

21|13|Meguzered! Bo nozu israt ʙa xonahoi xud ʙoz garded to pursida saved
21|14|Guftand; «Voj ʙar mo, mo sitamkor ʙudaem!»

21|18|Balki haqro ʙar sari ʙotil mezanem, to onro dar ham kuʙad va ʙotil noʙudsavanda ast. Va voj ʙar sumo az on ci ʙa Xudo sifat medihed

22|1|Ej mardum, az Parvardigoraton ʙitarsed, ki zilzilai qijomat hodisai ʙuzurgest
22|2|On ruz, ki ʙuʙinedas, har sirdihande sirxoraasro az jod ʙiʙarad va har homilae ʙori xudro, ʙar zamin guzorad va mardumro cun maston ʙini, hol on ki mast nestand, ʙalki azoʙi Xudo saxt ast
22|3|Ba'ze az mardum ʙe hec donise dar ʙorai Xudo ʙahs mekunand va ʙa dar sajtoni sarkase pajravi mekunand
22|4|Bar sajton cunin muqarrar suda, ki har kasro, ki dustas ʙidorad, gumroh kunad va ʙa azoʙi otasi suzonas kasonad
22|5|Ej mardum, agar az ruzi qijomat dar suʙha hasted, Mo sumoro az xok va sipas az nutfa, on goh az laxtai xune va sipas az poraguste goh tamom ofarida, goh notamom ʙijofaridaem, to qudrati xudro ʙarojaton oskor kunem. Va to zamone mu'ajjan har ciro xohem, dar rahmxho nigah medorem. On goh sumoro, ki kudake hasted, ʙerun meovarem, to ʙa haddi zurmandii xud rased. Ba'ze az sumo memirandva ʙa'ze ʙa solxurdagi ʙurda mesavand, to on goh ki har ci omuxtaand, faromus kunand. Va tu zaminro xuskida meʙini. Cun ʙoron ʙar on ʙifiris- tem, dar cunʙis ojad va nas'u namo kunad va az har guna gijohi ʙoravnaq ʙirujonad
22|6|Va inho dalel ʙar on ast, ki Xudo haq ast, murdagonro zinda mesozad va ʙar har kore tavonost
22|7|Va niz qijomat xohad omad, sake dar on nest. Va Xudo hamai kasonero, ki dar gurho hastand, zinda mekunad
22|8|Az mardum kasest, ki ʙe hec donise va hec rohnamoi va hec kitoʙi ravsaniʙaxse dar ʙorai Xudo ʙahs mekunad
22|9|Gardanro ʙa takaʙʙur ʙa jak su mepeconad, to mardumro az rohi Xudo gumroh sozad. Nasiʙi u dar dunjo xorist va dar ruzi qijomat azoʙi otasro ʙa u mecasonem
22|10|In cazoi korhoest, ki pes az in kardai va Xudo ʙa ʙandagonas sitam namekunad
22|11|Va az mijoni mardum kasest, ki Xudoro ʙo suʙha meparastad. Agar xajre ʙa u rasad, dilas ʙa on orom girad va agar ozmoise pes ojad, ruj ʙartoʙad. Dar dunjovu oxirat zijon ʙinad va on zijone oskor ast
22|12|Ƣajri Xudo kasero mexonad, ki na zijone ʙa u merasonad va na naf'e va in gumrohiest ʙeoxir
22|13|Kasero mexonad, ki zijonas nazdiktar az naf'i ust. Ci ʙad dustdorest va ci ʙad hamsuhʙat
22|14|Xudo kasonero, ki imon ovarda va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙa ʙihisthoe, ki dar on nahrho corist, doxil mesozad va Xudo har ci xohad, hamon mekunad
22|15|Kase, ki mepindorad, ki Xudo dar dunjovu oxirat jorias naxohad kard, xudasro ʙo resmone ʙa saqf ʙijovezad to xudro xafa kunad va ʙingarad, ki ojo in hila xasmasro az mijon xohad ʙurd
22|16|Ba in tarz Qur'onro nozil kardem ʙo ojote ravsangar. Va Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, hidojat mekunad
22|17|Xudo mijoni onon, ki imon ovardaand va onon, ki dini jahud jo soʙion jo nasoro jo macus ixtijor kardaand va onon, ki musrik sudaand, dar ruzi qijomat hukm mekunad. Zero U ʙar dar kore sohid ast
22|18|Ojo nadidai, ki har kas dar osmonhovu har kas, ki dar zamin ast va oftoʙu moh va sitoragonu kuhho va daraxtonu cunʙandagon va ʙisjore az mardum Xudoro sacda mekunand? Va ʙar ʙisjore azoʙ muqarrar suda va har kiro Xudo xor sozad, hec kas giromias namedorad. Zero Xudo har ci ʙixohad, hamon mekunad. (Sacda)
22|19|In du guruh dar ʙorai Parvardigorason ʙa xusumat ʙarxostaand. Baroi onon, ki kofirand, comahoe az otas ʙuridaand va az ʙolo ʙar sarason oʙi cuson merezand

22|23|Xudo kasonero, ki imon ovarda va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙa ʙihisthoe, ki dar on nahrho corist, doxil mesozad. Dar on co ʙo dastʙandhoe az tillovu marvorid orosta savand va liʙosason az harir ast
22|24|Onho ʙa on suxani pok va ʙa rohi Xudovandi sutudani rohnamoi sudaand
22|25|Onhoe, ki kofir sudand va mardumro az rohi Xudo va mascidulharom, ki ʙaroi mardumi ci muqimu ci ƣariʙ jakson ast, ʙozmedorand va niz har kiro dar on co qasdi kacravi jo sitamkori dosta ʙosad, azoʙi dardovar mecasonem
22|26|Va makoni xonaro ʙaroi Iʙrohim oskor kardem va guftem: «Hec cizro sariki Man masoz va xonai Maro ʙaroi tavofkunandagon va ʙa namoz istodagon va roke'onu socidon pokiza ʙidor»
22|27|Va mardumro ʙa hac da'vat kun to pijoda jo savor ʙar suturoni loƣar az rohhoi dur nazdi tu ʙijojand
22|28|To naf'hoero, ki az oni onhost, ʙuʙinand va nomi Xudoro dar ruzhoe mu'ajjan ʙa hangomi zaʙhi corpojone, ki Xudo rizqi onho soxta, jod kunand. Pas az onho ʙixuredu ʙenavojoni faqirro niz ta'om dihed

22|31|Rujovardagon ʙa Xudo ʙosed va sirknajovardagon ʙa U; va har kas, ki ʙa Xudo sirk ovarad, cun on kasest, ki az osmon furu aftad va murƣ uro ʙiraʙojad jo ʙodas ʙa makone dur andozad

22|35|onon, ki cun nomi Xudo ʙurda savad, dar dil ʙitarsand va ʙa on hangom, ki ʙa onho musiʙate rasad, soʙirand va namozguzoronand va az on ci ruziason dodaem, sadaqa mekunand
22|36|Suturoni qurʙoniro ʙaroi sumo az siorhoi Xudo qaror dodem. Sumoro dar on xajrest. 22|37|Gustu xuni in suturon ʙa Xudo namerasad. On ci ʙa U merasad, parhezgorii sumost. Hamcunin onhoro romi sumo soxt to Xudoro ʙa sukronai on, ki hidojataton kardaast, ʙa ʙuzurgi jod kuned. Va nekukoronro xusxaʙar deh

22|40|Onhoe, ki ʙa nohaq az dijorason ronda sudaand, faqat in ʙud, ki meguftand; «Parvardigori mo Xudoi jaktost?» Va agar Xudo ʙa'zero ʙa vasilai ʙa'ze digar daf' nakarda ʙud, dajrhovu kalisoho va kunisthovu mascidhoe, ki nomi Xudo ʙa farovoni dar on ʙurda mesavad, vajron megardid. 22|46|Ojo dar zamin sajr namekunand, to sohiʙi dilhoe gardand, ki ʙa on aql kunand va gushoe, ki ʙo on ʙisnavand? Zero casmho nestand, ki kur mesavand, ʙalki dilhoe, ki dar sinaho coj dorand, kur savand

22|73|Ej mardum, misole ova; rda sud. Bad-on gus dihed. Kasone, ki onhoro ʙa coi Olloh ʙa xudoi mexoned, agar hama gird ojand, magasero naxohand ofarid va agar magase cize az onho ʙiraʙojad, ʙozsitondanasro natavonand. Toliʙu matluʙ har du notavonand

23|101|Cun dar sur damida savad, hec xesovande mijo- nason namonad va hec az xoli jakdigar napursand

24|1|Suraest, ki onro nozil kardaem va vociʙas soxtaem va dar on ojote ravsan firistodaem, ʙosad, ki pand gired

24|3|Mardi zinokor ƣajri zani zinokor jo musrikro namegirad va zani zinokorro ƣajri mardi zinokor jo musrik namegirad. Va in ʙar mu'minon harom sudast
24|4|Kasonero, ki zanoni pokro ʙa zino mutahham mekunand va cahor sohid nameovarand, hastod zarʙa ʙizaned va az on pas hargiz sohidiasonro napazired, ki mardume fosiqand

24|11|Kasone, ki on duruƣi ʙuzurgro soxtaand, guruhe az sumojand. Mapindored, ki sumoro dar on sarre ʙuvad. Na, xajri sumo dar on ʙuvad. Har marde az onho ʙa on andoza gunoh, ki kardaast, ʙa cazo rasad va az mijoni onho, on ki ʙestarini in ʙuhtonro ʙa uhda dorad ʙa azoʙe ʙuzurg giriftor meojad

24|19|Baroi kasone, ki dust dorand, dar ʙorai mu'minon tuhmati zino pahn savad, dar dunjovu oxirat azoʙe dardovar muhajjost. Xudo medonad, va sumo namedoned
24|20|Halok mesuded, agar fazlu rahmate, ki Xudo ʙa sumo dodaast, nameʙud. Va agar Xudo mehruʙonu ʙaxsojanda nameʙud
24|21|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, poj ʙa coi poi sajton maguzored. Va har ki poj ʙa coi poi sajton guzorad, ʙidonad, ki u ʙa fahsovu munkar (korhoi ʙad) farmon medihad. Va agar fazlu rahmate ki Xudo ʙar sumo arzoni dostaast, nameʙud, hec jak az sumo hargiz rui poki namedid. Vale Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, pokiza mesozad. Va Xudo sunavovu donost
24|22|Tavongaron va onon, ki kusoise dar kori onhost, naʙojad savgand ʙixurand, ki ʙa xesovandonu miskinon va muhociron dar rohi Xudo cize nadihand. Bojad ʙiʙaxsandu ʙiʙaxsojand. Ojo namexohed, ki Xudo sumoro ʙiʙaxsojad? Va Xudost ʙaxsojandai mehruʙon
24|23|Kasone, ki ʙar zanoni pokdoman va ʙexaʙar az zino va mu'min tuhmati zino mezanand, dar dunjovu oxirat la'nat sudaand va ʙarojason azoʙest ʙuzurg

24|31|Va ʙa zanoni mu'min ʙigu, ki casmoni xud ʙipusand va sarmgohi xud nigoh dorand va zinathoi xudro cuz on miqdor, ki pajdost, oskor nakunand va miqna'ahoi (rujmolhoi) xudro to gireʙon ʙipusand va zinathoi xudro oskor nakunand, ƣajri ʙa savhari xud jo padari xud jo padari savhari xud jo pisari xud jo pisari savhari xud jo ʙarodari xud jo pisari ʙarodari xud jo pisari xohari xud jo zanoni hamdini xud, jo ʙandagoni xud jo mardoni xidmatguzori xud, ki raƣʙat ʙa zan nadorand, jo kudakone, ki az sarmgohi zanon ʙexaʙarand. Va niz cunon poj ʙar zamin nazanand to on zinat, ki piihon kardaand, donista savad. Ej mu'minon, hamagon ʙa dargohi Xudo tavʙa kuned, sojad nacot joʙed
24|32|Bezanonatonro va ƣulomu kanizoni xudro, ki soista ʙosand, hamsar dihed. Agar ʙenavo ʙosand, Xudo ʙa karami xud tavongarason xohad soxt, ki Xudo kusoisdihanda va donost
24|33|Onon, ki tavonoii zanosui nadorand, ʙojad pokDomani pesa kunand, to Xudo az karami xud tavongarason gardonad. Va az ʙandagonaton onon, ki xohoni ʙozxaridani xudand, agar dar onho xajre jofted, ʙozxaridanasonro ʙipazired. Va az on mol, ki Xudo ʙa sumo arzoni dostaast, ʙa onon ʙidihed. Va kanizoni xudro agar xohand, ki parhezgor ʙosand, ʙa xotiri sarvati dunjavi ʙa zino macʙur nakuned. Har kas, ki ononro ʙa zino vodorad, Xudo ʙaroi on kanizon, ki ʙa macʙuri ʙa on kor vodor gastaand, ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
24|34|Ba tahqiq ʙaroi sumo ojote ravsan va dostonhoe az kasone, ki pes az sumo ʙudaand, va niz pandhoe ʙaroi parhezgoron nozil kardem
24|35|Xudo nuri osmonhovu zamin ast. Misoli nuri U cun caroƣdonest, ki dar on caroƣe ʙosad, on caroƣ daruni sisae va on sisa cun sitorae duraxsanda. Az ravƣani daraxti purʙarakati zajtun, ki na sarqi astu na ƣarʙi afruxta ʙosad. Ravƣanas ravsani ʙaxsad, harcand otas ʙa on narasida ʙosad. Nur ʙar ʙoloi nur. 24|37|Mardone, ki hec ticorat va xaridu furuxte az jodi Xudo va namoz guzoridanu zakot dodaj ʙozason nadorad, az ruze, ki dilhovu didagon digargun mesavand, metarsand

24|39|Amalhoi kofiron cun saroʙest (mavci ƣarmi) dar ʙijoʙone. Tasna oʙas pindorad va cun ʙa on nazdik savad, hec najoʙad va Xudoro nazdi xud joʙad, pas cazoi uro ʙa tamom ʙidihad. Va Xudo zud ʙa hisoʙho merasad
24|40|Jo monandi torikihoest dar darjoe cuqur, ki mavcas pusonad va ʙar ʙoloi on mavce digar va ʙar ʙolojas aʙrest tira, torikihoe ʙar ʙoloi jakdigar, on tavr, ki agar dasti xud ʙe? run orad onro natavonad did. Va on, ki Xudo rohasro ʙa hec nure ravsan nakarda ʙosad, hec nure ʙar rohi xud najoʙad
24|41|Ojo nadidai, ki har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast va niz murƣone, ki dar parvozand, tasʙehgui Xudo hastand? Hama namozu tasʙehi Uro medonand. Va Xudo ʙa har kore, ki mokunand, oƣoh ast
24|42|Az oni Xudost farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin va ʙozgasti hamagon nazdi Ust
24|43|Ojo nadidai, ki Xudo aʙrhoero ʙa ohistagi meronad, on goh, onhoro ʙa ham mepajvandad va aʙre ʙuzurg padid meovarad va ʙoronro ʙini, ki dar on cost, tagarg (ƶola) mefiristad va har kiro xohad, ʙo on mezanad va az har ki mexohad, ʙozas medorad. 24|44|Xudo saʙu ruzro megardonad. Xiradmandonro dar in iʙratest
24|45|Va Xudo har cunʙandaero az oʙ ʙijofarid Ba'ze az onho ʙar sikam meravand va ʙa'ze ʙar du po meravand va ʙa'ze ʙar cahor po meravand. Xudo har ci ʙixohad, meofarinad. Zero Xudo ʙar har kore tavonost
24|46|Ba tazdik ojote ravsangar nozil kardem va Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, ʙa rohi rost hidojat mekunad
24|47|Va megujand: «Ba Xudovu pajomʙaras imon ovardaem va ito'at mekunem». Pae az on guruhe az onho ʙozmegardand. Va inho imon najovardaand

24|54|Bigu: «Ba Xudo ito'at kuned va ʙa pajomʙar ito'at kuned. Pas agar rujgardon saved, ʙar pajomʙar ast on ci ʙa u taklif kardaand va ʙar sumost on ci ʙar sumo taklif kardaand. Va agar ʙa u ito'at kuned, hidojat joʙed. Va ʙar uhdai pajomʙar ƣajri taʙliƣi oskor hec nest»
24|55|Xudo ʙa kasone az sumo, ki imon ovardaand va korhoe soista kardaand, va'da dod, ki dar rui zamin conisini digaronason kunad, hamcunon, ki mardumero, ki pes az onho ʙudand, conisini digaron kard, Va dinasonro, ki xud ʙarojason pisandida ast, ustuvor sozad. Va vahsatasonro ʙa tinci ivaz kunad. Maro meparastand va hec cizero ʙo Man sarik namekunand. Va onho, ki az in pas nosukri kunand, nofarmonand
24|56|Va namoz ʙiguzored ra zakot ʙidihed va ʙa pajomʙar ito'at kuned, ʙosad, ki ʙar sumo rahmat ovarand
24|57|Mapindor, ki kofiron metavonand dar in sarzamin ʙa coe ʙigurezand. Cojgohason cahannam ast va ci ʙad sarancomest
24|58|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙojad ƣulomoni sumo va onho, ki hanuz ʙa haddi ʙuluƣ narasidaand, dar se hangom az sumo ʙaroi doxil sudan ʙa xona ruxsat talaʙand: pes az namozi suʙh va hangomi zuhr, ki liʙos az tan ʙerun mekuned va ʙa'd az namozi xuftan. In se vaqt vaqti xilvati sumost. Dar ƣajri on se hangom sumo va onho gunohe nakardaed, agar ʙar jakdigar ʙigzared. Xudo ojotro incunin ʙaroi sumo ʙajon mekunad. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
24|59|Va cun atfoli sumo ʙa haddi ʙuluƣ rasidand, ʙojad monandi kasone, ki zikrason guzast, ruxsat talaʙand. Xudo ojotro incunin ʙaroi sumo ʙajon mekunad. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
24|60|Pirazanon, ki digar umedi suj kardanason nest, ʙe on, ki zinathoi xudro oskor kunand, agar codari xud ʙinihand, gunohe nakardaand. Va xuddori kardan ʙarojason ʙehtar ast va Xudo sunavovu donost
24|61|Bar noʙino harace (gunohe) nest va ʙar lang gunohe nest va ʙar ʙemor gunohe nest. Va ʙar sumo gunohe nest, agar az xonai xud jo xonai padaraton jo xonai modaraton jo xonai ʙarodaraton jo xonai xoharaton jo xonai amakaton jo xonai ammaaton jo xonai doijaton (taƣojaton) jo xonai xolaaton jo xonae, ki kalidhoi on nazdi sumost, jo xonai dustaton cize ʙixured. Va gunohe ʙar sumo nest, agar ʙo ham ʙixured jo cudo-cudo. Va cun ʙa xonae doxil saved, ʙar jakdigar salom kuned. in salomest muʙorak va pokiza az coniʙi Xudo. Xudo ojotro ʙaroi sumo incunin ʙajon mekunad, sojad, ki aql kuned
24|62|Mu'minon kasone hastand, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon ovardaand va cun ʙo pajomʙar dar kore jakcoja ʙosand, to az u ruxsat natalaʙidaand, naʙojad ʙiravand. Onho, ki az tu ruxsat metalaʙand, kasone hastand, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon ovardaand. Pas hangome ki az tu ʙaroi ʙa'ze az korhojason ruxsat xostand, ʙar har jak az onon, ki xohi, ruxsat ʙideh va ʙarojason az Xudo ʙaxsois ʙixoh ki Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
24|63|Oncunon ki jakdigarro sado mekuned, pajomʙarro sado nakuned. Xudo medonad ci kasone az sumo dar panohi digare xudro pinhon mesozand va ohistaohista ʙerun meravand. Onon, ki az farmoni U sarpeci mekunand, ʙojad ʙitarsand, ki maʙodo ʙa onho fitnae jo azoʙe dardovar ʙirasad
24|64|Az oni Xudost har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast. Medonad, ki sumo ʙar ci kored. Va on ruz, ki ʙa U ʙozgardonda savand, ononro az korhoe, ki kardaand, ogoh sozad. Va Xudo ʙar har cize donost
25|1|Buzurg astu ʙuzurgvor on kas, ki in furqonro ʙar ʙandai Xud nozil kard, to cahonijonro ʙimdihandae ʙosad
25|2|On kas, ki az oni Ust farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin va farzande nagiriftaast va Uro sarike dar farmonravoi nest va har cizro ʙijofaridaast va onro ʙa miqdor ofaridaast
25|3|Ƣajri U xudojone digar giriftand, ki hec ciz nameofarinand, va xud maxluqand. Na moliki zijoni xud hastand va na naf'i xud va moliki margu zindagi va qijomat nestand
25|4|Va kofiron guftand, ki in cuz duruƣe, ki xud ʙoftaast va guruhe digar uro ʙar on jori dodaand, hec nest. Haqqo, on ci megujand, sitamu ʙotil ast

25|8|Caro az osmon gance ʙarojas afkanda nasavad? Caro uro ʙoƣe nest, ki az on ʙixurad?» Va sitamkoron guftand: «Sumo ʙa mardi codusudae pajravi mekuned!»

25|18|Gujand: «Poki Tu! Moro sazovor naʙudaast, ki cuz tu kasero ʙa jori girem. Tu xud onho va padaronasonro ʙarxurdor soxti, cunon ki jodi Turo faromus kardand va mardume sudand ʙa halokat aftoda
25|19|Inho on ciro megufted, duruƣ xondand va aknun natavoned azoʙero az xud dur sozed jo xudro jori dihed. Va har kas az sumo, ki sitam kunad, azoʙe ʙuzurgas mecasonem
25|20|Pes az tu pajomʙarone firistodaem, ki ta'om mexurdand va dar ʙozorho roh meraftand. Va sumoro vasilai ozmoisi jakdigar qaror dodem. Ojo saʙr tavoned kard? Va Parvardigori tu ʙinost

26|86|va padaramro ʙijomurz, ki az gumrohon ast
26|87|va dar ruzi qijomat maro rasvo masoz
26|88|ruze, ki na mol naf' medihad va na farzandon
26|89|ƣajri on kas, ki ʙo qalʙe pokiza az sirk ʙa nazdi Xudo ʙijojad!»
26|90|Va ʙihistro ʙaroi parhezgoron nazdik orand
26|91|Va cahannamro dar nazari kofiron oskor kunand
26|92|Ba onho gujand: Cizhoe, ki ʙa coi Xudoi jakto meparastided, kucojand
26|93|Ojo joriaton mekunand, jo xud jori mecujand?»
26|94|Onho va kofironro sarmagun dar cahannam andozand
26|95|va hamai laskari Iʙlisro
26|96|Va dar hole, ki dar cahannam ʙo jakdigar husumat mekunandu, megujand
26|97|«Ba Xudo savgand, ki mo dar gumrohii oskor ʙudem
26|98|on goh ki sumoro ʙo Parvardigori cahonijon ʙaroʙar medonistem
26|99|Va moro ʙadkoron gumroh soxtand
26|100|va aknun moro safe'one (xaloskunandahoe) nest
26|101|va moro dusti mehruʙone nest
26|102|Kos ʙori digar ʙa dunjo ʙozgardem, to az mu'minon gardem»
26|103|Dar in iʙratest va ʙestarinason imon najovardand
26|104|Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
26|105|Qavmi Nuh pajomʙaronro duruƣ ʙarozardand
26|106|On goh ki ʙarodarason Nuh ʙa onho guft: «Ojo nametarsed
26|107|Man ʙaroi sumo pajomʙare rostgu hastam
26|108|Az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned

26|110|Pas az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned!»
26|111|Guftand: «Ojo ʙa tu imon ʙijovarem va hol on ki kamʙaƣalon pajravi tu hastand?»
26|112|Guft: «Donisi man ʙa korhoe, ki mekunand, namerasad
26|113|Agar mefahmed, hisoʙas tanho ʙo Parvardigori man ast
26|114|Va man mu'minonro dur namekunam
26|115|Bimdihandae oskor hastam»
26|116|Guftand: «Ej Nuh agar ʙas nakuni, sangsor mesavi»
26|117|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, qavmi man maro duruƣ meʙarorand
26|118|Mijoni manu onho rohe ʙarkusoj va marovu mu'minoni hamrohi maro nacot ʙideh»
26|119|U va hamrohonasro dar on kistii pur nacot dodem
26|120|Va ʙoqiro ƣark, kardem

26|123|Qavmi Od pajomʙaronro takziʙ kardand (duruƣ ʙarovardand)
26|124|On goh, ki ʙarodarason Hud guft: «Ojo nametarsed
26|125|Man ʙaroi sumo pajomʙare rostgu hastam

26|127|Man az sumo dar ʙaroʙari hidojati xud muzde nametalaʙam. Muzdi man tanho ʙar uhdai Parvardigori cahonijon ast
26|128|Ojo ʙar sari har ʙalandi ʙa ʙehudagi ʙinoe ʙaland mesozed
26|129|Va ʙad-in pindor, ki hamesa zindaed, qasrxoe ʙino mekuned
26|130|Va har goh intiqom gired, cun ʙerahmon intiqom megired
26|131|Pas az Xudo ʙitarsed va az man ito'at kuned

26|133|Va ʙa sumo corpojonu farzandon ato kardaast
26|134|va ʙoƣhovu casmasoron
26|135|Man az azoʙi ruze ʙuzurg ʙar sumo ʙimnokam»
26|136|Guftand: «Barjuj mo jakson ast, ki moro pand dihi jo pand nadihi
26|137|Inho cuz hamon duruƣu najrangi pesinijon nest
26|138|Va mo azoʙ naxohem sud»
26|139|Pas duruƣas ʙarovardand va Mo ononro halok kardem. Alʙatta dar in iʙratest va ʙestarinason imon najovardand
26|140|Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
26|141|Qavmi Samud pajomʙaronro duruƣ ʙarovardand
26|142|On goh ki ʙarodarason Soleh guft: «Ojo nametarsed
26|143|Man ʙaroi sumo pajomʙare rostgu hastam
26|144|Az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned
26|145|Man az sumo dar ʙaroʙari hidojati xud muzde nametalaʙam. Muzdi man tanho ʙar uhdai Parvardigori cahonijon ast
26|146|Ojo pindored, ki sumoro dar in ne'matho emin raho mekunand
26|147|Dar ʙoƣhovu casmasorho
26|148|Va kistzorhovu nahlho (xurmozorho) ʙo on sukufahoi narmu latif
26|149|Va sodmon dar kuhho xonahoe metarosed
26|150|Pas az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned
26|151|Va farmoni in isrofkoronro qaʙul nakuned
26|152|Inho, ki dar zamin fasod mekunand va isloh namekunand»
26|153|Guftand: «Ƣajri in nest, ki turo codu kardaand
26|154|Tu niz ʙasare monandi mo hasti. Agar rost megui, nisonae ʙijovar»
26|155|Guft: «In modasuturi man ast. Jak ruz oʙ xurdan haqqi u ʙosad va jak ruz haqqi sumo
26|156|Ba on oseʙe narasoned, ki azoʙi ruze ʙuzurg sumoro furu megirad»
26|157|Onro kustand va pusajmon sudand
26|158|Pas azoʙ onhoro furu girift., Alʙatta dar in iʙratest va ʙestarinason imon najovardand
26|159|Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
26|160|Qavmi Lut pajomʙaronro duruƣ ʙarovardand
26|161|On goh, ki ʙarodarason Lut guft: «Ojo nametarsed
26|162|Mam ʙaroi sumo pajomʙare rostgu hastam
26|163|Az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned
26|164|Man az sumo dar ʙaroʙari hidojati xud muzde nametalaʙam. Muzdi man tanho ʙar uxdai Parvardigori cahonijon ast
26|165|Caro az mijoni mardumi cahon ʙo mardon meomezed
26|166|Va hamsaronero, ki Parvardigoraton ʙarojaton ofaridaast, tark megued? Na, sumo mardume tacovuzkor hasted!»
26|167|Guftand: «Ej Lut, agar ʙas nakuni, az sahr ʙerunat mekunem»
26|168|Guft: «Man ʙo kori sumo dusmanam
26|169|Ej Parvardigori man, maro va kasonamro az oqiʙati amale, ki mekunand, nacot ʙaxs!»
26|170|U va hamai kasonasro nacot dodem
26|171|ƣajri pirazane, ki xost ʙimonad
26|172|Sipas digaronro halok kardem
26|173|ʙar onho ʙorone ʙoronidem va ci ʙad ʙud ʙoroni tahdidsudagon
26|174|Alʙatta dar in iʙratest va ʙestarinason imon najovardand
26|175|Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
26|176|Mardumi Ajka pajomʙaronro duruƣ ʙarovardand
26|177|On goh ki Su'ajʙ ʙa onho guft: «Ojo az Xudo nametarsed
26|178|Man ʙaroi sumo pajomʙare rostgu hastam
26|179|Az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned
26|180|Man az sumo dar ʙaroʙari hidojati xud muzde nametalaʙam. Muzdi man tanho ʙar uhdai Parvardigori cahonijon ast
26|181|Pajmonaro (zarfi cenkuniro) tamom ʙipardozed va kamfurusi makuned
26|182|Va ʙo tarozui durust vazn kuned
26|183|Ba mardum kam madihed va ʙeʙokona dar zamin fasod makuned
26|184|Az on kas, ki sumo va ofaridagoni pes az sumoro ofaridaast, ʙitarsed»
26|185|Guftand: «Ƣajri in nest, ki turo codu kardaand
26|186|Tu niz insone monandi mo hasti va mepindorem, ki duruƣ megui
26|187|Agar rost megui, porae az osmonro ʙar sari mo andoz»
26|188|Guft: «Parvardigori man ʙa koro, ki mekuned, donotar ast»
26|189|Pas duruƣas ʙarovardand va dar on ruzi aʙri azoʙ ononro furu girifg. Va on azoʙi ruze ʙuzurg ʙud
26|190|Alʙatta dar in iʙratest va ʙestarinason imon najovardand
26|191|Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
26|192|Va in kitoʙ nozilsuda az coniʙi Parvardigori cahonijon ast
26|193|Onro ruhulamin nozil kardaast
26|194|ʙar dili tu, to az ʙimdihandagon ʙosi
26|195|ʙa zaʙoni araʙii ravsan
26|196|Va on dar navistahoi pesinijon niz hast
26|197|Ojo in nisona ʙar onho ʙasanda nest, ki ulamoi ʙani-Isroil az on ogohand
26|198|Agar onro ʙar jake az acamon (ƣajri araʙho) nozil karda ʙudem
26|199|va ʙarojason onro mexond, ʙa on imon nameovardand
26|200|Ba in tarz Qur'onro dar dilhoi gunahkoron roh dodem
26|201|Ba on imon nameovarand to azoʙi dardovarro ʙuʙinand
26|202|Va on azoʙ nogahon va ʙexaʙar ʙar onon furud meojad
26|203|Megujand: «Ojo moro muhlate xohand dod?»
26|204|Ojo ʙa azoʙi mo mesitoʙand
26|205|Didi, ki harcand solho ʙahramandason soxtem
26|206|ʙoz ham azoʙe, ki ʙa onho va'da suda ʙud, ʙar sarason omad
26|207|On ʙahramandiho ʙa holason naf' nakard
26|208|Mo hec dehaero halok nakardem, cuz on, ki ʙarojason ʙimdihandagone ʙudand
26|209|to pandason dihand. Zero mo sitamkor nestem
26|210|Va in Qur'onro sajtonho nozil nakardaand
26|211|Onon na loiqi in korand va na tavoni on dorand
26|212|Sajtonhoro az sunidani vahj dur dostaand
26|213|Pas ʙo Xudoi jakto xudoi digarero maxon, to maʙod dar sumori azoʙsavandagon daroi
26|214|Xesovandoni nazdikatro ʙitarson
26|215|Dar ʙaroʙari har jak az mu'minon, ki ʙa tu pajravi mekunad, xoksoru narm ʙos
26|216|Va agar ʙar tu nofarmoni kardand, ʙigu: «Man az korhoi sumo ʙezoram!»
26|217|Va ʙar Xudoi piruzmandu mehruʙon tavakkal kun
26|218|On, ki turo meʙinad, on goh, ki ʙarmexezi
26|219|va namoz xondanatro ʙo digar namozguzoron meʙinad
26|220|Alʙatta Ust sunavoi dono
26|221|Ojo sumoro ogoh kunam, ki sajtonho ʙa nazdi kiho meojand
26|222|Bar har duruƣgui gunahkor meojand
26|223|Gus medihand va ʙestarinason duruƣgujonand
26|224|Va gumrohon az pai soiron meravand
26|225|Ojo nadidai, ki soiron dar har vodie sargastaand
26|226|Va cizho megujand, ki xud amal namekunand
26|227|Ƣajri onho, ki imon ovardand va korhoi soista kardand va Xudoro farovon jod kardand va cun mavridi sitam voqe' sudand, intiqom giriftand. Va sitamkoron ʙa zudi xohand donist, ki ʙa ci makone ʙozmegardand
27|1|To, sin. In ast ojoti Qur'on va kitoʙi ravsangar
27|2|Rahnamun va xusxaʙarest ʙaroi mu'minon
27|3|onon, ki namoz meguzorand va zakot medihand va ʙa ruzi qijomat jaqin dorand
27|4|Amalhoi onhoero, ki ʙa oxirat imon nadorand, dar dar nazarason ʙijorostem. Az in ruj sargasta mondaand
27|5|Onho hamon kasonand, ki azoʙi saxt az oni onhost va dar oxirat zijonkortarand
27|6|Tu kase hasti, ki Qur'on az coniʙi Xudoi hakimu dono ʙa tu nozil mesavad
27|7|Muso ʙa xonavodai xud guft: «Man az dur otase didam, ʙa zudi, ki az on ʙarojaton xaʙare ʙijovaram jo porai otase. Sojad garm saved»
27|8|Cun ʙa otas rasid, sadojas dodand, ki ʙarakat doda suda on, ki daruni otas ast va on, ki dar kanori on ast. Va pok ast Xudoi jakto, on Parvardigori cahonijon
27|9|«Ej Muso, Man Xudoi ƣoliʙu hakim hastam
27|10|Asojatro ʙijafkan!»; Cun didas, ki monandi more mecunʙad, gurezon ʙozgast va ʙa aqiʙ nanigarist. «Ej Muso, matars. Pajomʙaron naʙojad, ki dar nazdi man ʙitarsand
27|11|ƣajri kase, ki gunohe karda ʙosad va pas az ʙadkori nekukor savad. Zero Man ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙonam
27|12|Dastatro dar gireʙon ʙiʙar, to ʙe hec oseʙe safed ʙerun ojad. Bo nuh nisona nazdi Fir'avn va qavmas ʙirav, ki mardume fosiqand»
27|13|Cun nisonahoi ravsani Moro didand, guftand: «In codue oskor ast!»
27|14|Bo on, ki dar dil ʙa on jaqin ovarda ʙudand, vale az rui sitamu ʙartaricui inkoras kardand. Pas ʙingar, ki oqiʙati taʙahkoron ci guna ʙuvad
27|15|Mo ʙa Dovudu Sulajmon donis dodem. Guftand: «Sukr Xudoro ast, ki moro ʙar ʙisjore az ʙandagoni mu'mini xud ʙartari dod!»
27|16|Va Sulajmon vorisi Dovud sud va guft: «Ej mardum, ʙa mo zaʙoni murƣon omuxtand va az har ne'mate ato kardand. Va in inojatest oskor!»
27|17|Sipohijoni Sulajmon az cinnu odami va parranda gird omadand va onho ʙa saf meraftand
27|18|To ʙa vodii murcagon rasidand. Murcae guft: «Ej murcagon, ʙa lonahoi xud daroed, to Sulajmonu laskarijonas sumoro ʙexaʙar pomol nakunand»
27|19|Sulajmon az suxani u laʙxand zadu guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro tavfiq deh to sukri ne'mati turo, ki ʙar man va padaru modari man arzoni dostai, ʙa coj ovaram va korhoi soistae kunam, ki tu xusnud savi va maro ʙa rahmati xud dar sumori ʙandagoni soistaat darovar!»
27|20|Dar mijoni murƣon custucu kard va guft: «Caro hudhudro nameʙinam. Ojo az ƣoiʙsudagon ast
27|21|Ba saxttarin tarze azoʙas mekunam jo sarasro meʙuram, agar ʙaroi man dalele ravsan naorad»
27|22|Der kardanas ʙa daroz nakasid. Bijomadu guft «Ba cize dast joftaam, ki tu dast najofta ʙudi va az Saʙo ʙarojat xaʙare durust ovardaam
27|23|Zanero joftam, ki ʙar onho podsohi mekunad. Az har ne'mate ʙarxurdor ast va taxte ʙuzurg dorad
27|24|Didam, ki xud va mardumas ʙa coi Xudoi jakto oftoʙro sacda mekunand. Va sajton amalhojasonro dar nazarason ʙijorostaast va az rohi Xudo gumrohason kardaast, cunon ki rui hidojat naxohand did
27|25|Caro Xudoero, ki nihoni osmonhovu zaminro oskor mekunad va har ciro pinhon medored jo oskor mesozed, medonad, sacda nakunand
27|26|Xudoi jakto, ki hec xudoe ƣajri U nest. Parvardigori arsi azim». (Sacda)
27|27|Guft: «Aknun ʙingarem, ki rost guftai jo dar sumori duruƣgujoni
27|28|In nomai maro ʙiʙar va ʙar onho afkan, sipas ʙa jak su sav va ʙingar, ki ci cavoʙ medihand»
27|29|Zan guft: «Ej ʙuzurgon, nomae giromi ʙa sui man partofta sud
27|30|Noma az Sulajmon ast va in ast: «Ba nomi Xudoi ʙaxsojandai mehruʙon»
27|31|«Bar man ʙartari macued va ʙa taslim nazdi man ʙijoed»
27|32|Zan guft: «Ej ʙuzurgon, dar kori man ra'j ʙidihed, ki to sumo hozir naʙosed, man hec korero hal natavonam kard»
27|33|Guftand: Mo qudratmandon va sohiʙoni cangi saxt hastem. Korho ʙa dasti tust. Bingar, ki ci farmon medihi»
27|34|Zan guft: «Podsohon cun ʙa dehae darojand, vajronas mekunand va azizonasro xor mesozand. Ore, cunin kunand
27|35|Man hadjae nazdason mefiristam va menigaram, ki qosidon ci cavoʙ meovarand»
27|36|Cun qosid nazdi Sulajmon omad, Sulajmon guft: «Ojo mexohed ʙa mol maro jori kuned? On ci Xudo ʙa man doda, az on ci ʙa sumo doda ʙehtar ast. Na, sumo ʙa hadjai xud sodmon hasted
27|37|Aknun ʙa nazdason ʙozgard. Laskare ʙar sarason mekasem, ki hargiz toqati onro nadosta ʙosand. Va ʙa xorivu zori az on co ʙerunason mekunem»
27|38|Guft: «Ej ʙuzurgon, kadom jak az sumo taxti uro, pes az on, ki ʙa taslim nazdi man ojad, ʙarojam meovared?»
27|39|Ifrite az mijoni cinho guft: «Man qaʙl az on, ki az cojat ʙarxezi, onro nazdi tu hozir mekunam, ki man ʙar in kor ham tavonojamu ham ʙovarinok»
27|40|Va on kas, ki az ilmi kitoʙ ʙahrae dost, guft: «Man, pes az on, ki casm ʙar ham zani, onro nazdi tu meovaram». Cun onro nazdi xud did, guft: «In ʙaxsisi Parvardigori man ast, to maro ʙijozmojad, ki sukrguzoram jo kofiri ne'mat. Pas har ki sukr gujad, ʙaroi xud guftaast va har ki nosukri kunad, Parvardigori man ʙenijozu karim ast»
27|41|Guft: «Taxtasro digargun kuned, ʙuʙinem onro ʙozmesinosad jo az onhost, ki ʙoznatavonand sinoxt»
27|42|Cun omad, guftandas: «Ojo taxti tu cunin ʙud?» Guft: «Gujo hamon ast. Va mo pes az in ogoh suda ʙudem va taslim ʙudaem»
27|43|Va uro az har ci ʙa coi Xudoi jakto meparastid, ʙozdost. Zero u dar zumrai kofiron ʙud
27|44|Guftandas: «Ba sahni qasr daroj!» Cun ʙididas, pindost, havzi pur az oʙ ast. Doman az soqhojas ʙargirift. Sulajmon guft: «In sahnest sof az sisa». Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, man ʙar xud sitam kardaam va inak ʙo Sulajmon dar ʙaroʙari Parvardigori cahonijon taslim sudam»
27|45|Va ʙa qavmi Samud ʙarodarason Solehro firistodem, ki: Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparasted. Nogahon du guruh sudand va ʙo jakdigar ʙa xusumat ʙarxostand
27|46|Guft: «Ej qavmi man, caro pes az neki ʙar ʙadi mesitoʙed? Caro az Xudo ʙaxsois namexohed? Sojad ʙar sumo rahmat ovarad»
27|47|Guftand: «Mo turo va joronatro ʙa foli ʙad giriftaem». Guft: «Foli ʙadaton nazdi Xudost. Inak mardume fireʙxurda hasted!»
27|48|Dar sahr nuh mardi nosoleh ʙudand, ki dar on sarzamin fasod mekardand, na isloh
27|49|Guftand; «Ba Xudo savgand xured, ki u va kasonas ro saʙona mekusem. Va cun kase ʙa talaʙi xunas ʙarxezad, ʙiguem: «Mo ʙa hangomn halokati kasoni u on co naʙudaem va mo rostguftorem»
27|50|Va ƣofil ʙudand, ki agar onho hilae andesidaand, Mo niz hilae andesidaem
27|51|Bingar, ki oqiʙati makrason ci sud: Mo onho va qavmasonro ʙa tamomi halok kardem
27|52|On xonahoi onhost, ki ʙa cazoi zulme, ki mekardand, xoli aftodaast. Dar on donojonro iʙratest
27|53|Onhoero, ki imon ovarda ʙudand va parhezgor ʙudand, nacot dodem
27|54|Va Lutro ʙa jod or. On goh ki ʙa qavmi xud guft: «Korhoi zist mekuned, dar hole, ki xud ʙa zistii on ogohed
27|55|Caro az rui sahvat ʙa coi zanon ʙa mardon sahvat meroned? Sumo mardume nodon hasted!»
27|56|Cavoʙi qavmi u in ʙud, ki guftand: «Xonadoni Lutro az dehi xud ʙerun kuned. Onon da'voi poki mekunand» (Porai)
27|57|U va kasonas, ƣajri zanasro, nacot dodem. Cunon xostem, ki on zan az ʙozmondagon ʙosad
27|58|Borone ʙar onho ʙoronidem va ʙoroni tahdidsudagon ci ʙad ʙoronest
27|59|Bigu; «Sukr Ollohro va salom ʙar ʙandagoni intixoʙkardai U. Ojo Olloh ʙehtar ast jo on cizho, ki sariki U qaror medihand
27|60|Jo on kase, ki osmonhovu zaminro ofarid va az osmon ʙarojaton oʙ firistod va ʙo on ʙustonhoe xusmanzar rujonidem, ki sumoro tavoni rujonidani daraxte az on nest. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Na, onho mardume hastand az haq qacrav
27|61|Jo on ki zaminro oromgoh soxt va dar on rudho pajdo kard, kuhho va mijoni du dare mone'e qaror dod, Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Na, ʙestarinason namedonand
27|62|Jo on ki darmondaro cun ʙixonadas, posux medihad va ranc az u dur mekunad va sumoro dar zamin conisini pesinijon mesozad. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Ci andak pand megired
27|63|Jo on ki sumoro dar torikihoi ʙijoʙonu darjo roh menamojad va on ki pes az ʙoroni rahmatas ʙodhoro ʙa muƶda mefiristad. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Olloh ʙolotar ast az har ci sariki U mesozand
27|64|Jo on ki maxluqotro meofarinad, sipas onhoro ʙozmegardonad va on, ki az osmonu zamin ʙa sumo ruzi medihad. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Bigu; Agar rost megued: daleli xud ʙijovared!»
27|65|Bigu: «Hec kas dar osmonhovu zamin ƣajʙro namedonad, magar Olloh. Va niz namedonand ci vaqt zinda mesavand!»
27|66|Dar ʙoʙi oxirat ʙa jaqin rasidand? Na! Hamcunon dar sak hastand, ʙalki mardume noʙinojand
27|67|Kofiron guftand: «Ci guna agar movu padaronamon xok sudem, moro az qaʙr ʙerun meovarand
27|68|Ba mo va padaronamon ham pes az in cunin va'dae doda ʙudand. Inho cize ƣajri afsonahoi pesinijon nest!»
27|69|Bigu: «Dar zamin sajr kuned va ʙingared, ki pojoni kori gunahkoron ci guna ʙudaast!»
27|70|Barojason anduhgin maʙos va az hilae, ki meandesand, tangdil masav
27|71|Megujand: «Agar rost megued, on va'dai qijomat ci vaqt xohad ʙud?»
27|72|Bigu: «Sojad ʙa'ze az on ci ʙa sitoʙ metalaʙed, nazdiki sumo ʙosad»
27|73|Va Parvardigori tu fazli xudro ʙar mardum ato mekunad, vale ʙestarinason sukr namegujand
27|74|Va Parvardigori tu medonad, ki ci cizro dar dil nihon kardaand va ci cizro oskor mesozand
27|75|Va dar osmonhovu zamin hec cizi maxfi nest, ki on dar kitoʙi muʙin naomada ʙosad
27|76|In Qur'on ʙisjore az cizhoero, ki ʙani-Isroil dar on ixtilof dorand, ʙarojason hikojat mekunad
27|77|Va ʙaroi mu'mimon hidojatu rahmat ast
27|78|Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ʙa ra'ji xud mijonason hukm xohad kard, ki U ƣoliʙu donost
27|79|Pas ʙa Xudo tavakkal kun, ki tu hamroh ʙo haqiqate ravsan hasti
27|80|Tu nametavoni murdagokro sunavo sozi va ovozi xudro ʙa gusi karone, ki az tu ruj megardonand. Birasoni
27|81|Tu nametavoni kuronro az gumrohijason roh namoi. Ovozi xudro tanho ʙa gusi kasone tavoni rasond, ki ʙa ojoti Mo imon ovardaand va musalmon hastand
27|82|Cun farmoni qijomat muqarrar gardad, ʙarojason cunʙandae az zamin ʙerun meovarem, ki ʙo onon suxan ʙigujad, ki in mardum ʙa ojoti Mo jaqin nameovardand
27|83|Ruze, ki az har millate guruhero az onon, ki ojoti Moro duruƣ meʙarovardand, cam' meovarem va ononro ʙa saf ʙironand
27|84|to cun ʙa mahsar ʙirasand, gujad: «Ojo sumo ojoti Maro duruƣ meʙarovarded va hol on, ki donisi sumo ʙa on ihota najofta ʙud? On ci kore ʙud, ki mekarded?»
27|85|Ba cazoi sitame, ki mekardand, hukmi azoʙ ʙar onho muqarrar savad, ʙe on, ki hec suxane ʙigujand
27|86|Ojo nameʙinand, ki saʙro padid ovardem, to dar on ʙijoromand va ruzro ravsani ʙaxsidem. Alʙatta dar in ʙaroi mu'minon iʙrathost
27|87|Ruze, ki dar sur damida savad va hamai kasone, ki dar osmonhovu zamin hastand, ƣajri on kas ki Xudo ʙixohad, ʙitarsand va hama xoru zalil ʙa sui U ravon savand
27|88|Va kuhhoro ʙini, pindori, ki ʙeconand, hol on, ki ʙa sur'ati aʙr meravand. Kori Xudovand, ast, ki har cizero ʙa kamol xalq kardaast. Alʙatta U ʙa har ci mekuned, ogoh ast
27|89|Har kas, ki kori neke kunad, ʙehtar az onro mukofot girad va nekukoron az vahsati on ruz dar amon ʙosand
27|90|Va ononro, ki korhoi ʙad mekunand, sarnagun dar otas andozand, ojo cuz muvofiqi korhoe, ki kardaed, cazo joʙed
27|91|Ba man farmon suda, ki Parvardigori in sahrro ʙiparastam. Sahre, ki Xudovande, ki hama ciz az oni Ust, hurmatas nihoda va amr sudaam, ki az musalmonon ʙosam
27|92|Va Qur'onro tilovat kunam. Pas har ki hidojat joft, ʙa naf'i xud hidojat joftaast va har ki gumroh sud, ʙigu: «Man ʙimdihandae hastam»
27|93|Va ʙigu: «Sukr Xudorost. Ojoti xudro ʙa sumo nison medihad, to onhoro ʙisinosed. Va Parvardigori tu az hec kore, ki mekuned, ʙexaʙar nest»
28|1|To, sin, mim
28|2|In ast ojathoi in kitoʙi ravsangar
28|3|Baroi onho, ki imon meovarand, dostoni rostini Muso va Fir'avnro ʙar tu mexonem
28|4|Fir'avn dar on sarzamin ʙartari cust va mardumasro firqa-firqa soxt. Firqaero xor medost va pisaronasonro mekust va zanonasonro zinda meguzost, ki u az fasodkoron ʙud
28|5|Va Mo ʙar on hastem, ki ʙar mustaz'afoni (za'ifoni) rui zamin ne'mat dihem va ononro pesvojon sozem va vorison gardonem
28|6|Va onhoro dar on sarzamin oʙruvu qudrat ʙaxsidem va ʙa Fir'avnu Homon va laskarijonason cizero, ki az on metarsidand, nison dihem
28|7|Va ʙa modari Muso vahj kardem, ki siras ʙideh va agar ʙar u ʙimnok sudi uro ʙa darjo ʙijandoz va matars va ƣamgin masav, uro ʙa tu ʙozmegardonem va dar sumori pajomʙaronas meovarem
28|8|Xonadoni Fir'avn uro joftand, to dusmanonason va saʙaʙi anduhason gardad, Fir'avn va Homon va laskarijonason xato mekardand
28|9|Zani Fir'avn guft: «In saʙaʙi sodmonii manu tust. Uro nakused, sojad ʙa mo naf'e ʙirasonad, jo uro ʙa farzandi girem». Va namedonistand, ki ci mekunand
28|10|Dili modari Muso tang sud. Va agar dilasro qavi nakarda ʙudem, to az mu'minon ʙosad, nazdik ʙud, ki on sirro fos sozad
28|11|Va ʙa xohari u guft: «Az pai u ʙirav». Va zan ʙe on ki onho fahmand, az dur dar u menigarist
28|12|Pistoni hamai dojagonro az pes ʙar u harom karda ʙudem. On zan guft: «Ojo mexohed sumoro ʙa xonavodae rohnamoi kunam, ki uro ʙarojaton nigoh dorand va nekxohas ʙosand?»
28|13|Pas uro nazdi modaras ʙargardonidem, to casmoni on zan ravsan gardad va ƣamgin naʙosad va ʙidonad, ki va'dai Xudo haq ast, vale ʙestarinason namedonand
28|14|Cun ʙa haddi ʙuluƣ rasid va ʙoquvvat sud, uro hikmatu donis dodem va nekukoronro cunii mukofot medihem
28|15|Bexaʙar az mardumi sahr ʙa sahr doxil sud. Du tanro did, ki ʙo ham cang mekunand. In jak az pajravonas ʙud va on jak az dusmanonas. On ki az pajravonas ʙud, ʙar ziddi on digar, ki az dusmanonas ʙud, az u jori xost. Muso muste ʙar u zad va uro kust. Guft: «In kori sajton ʙud. U ʙa oskoro dusmane gumrohkunanda ast»
28|16|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, man ʙa xud sitam kardam. Maro ʙiʙaxsoj». Va Xudojas ʙiʙaxsid. Zero ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
28|17|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, ʙa sukri ne'mate, ki ʙar man ato kardi, hargiz pustiʙoni gunahkoron naxoham sud!»
28|18|Digar ruz dar sahr tarson va casm ʙar rohi hodisa megardid. Marde, ki diruz az u madad xosta ʙud, ʙoz ham az u madad xost. Muso ʙa u guft: «Tu ʙa oskoro gumroh hasti!»
28|19|Cun xost mardero, ki dusmani har dui onho ʙud, ʙizanad, guft: «Ej Muso, ojo mexohi hamcunon ki diruz jakero kusti, maro niz ʙikusi? Tu mexohi, ki dar in sarzamin zolime ʙosi va namexohi, ki az muslihon ʙosi»
28|20|Marde az durdasti sahr davon omadu guft: «Ej Muso, sardoroni sahr dar ʙorai tu masvarat mekunand to ʙikusandat. Berun ʙirav. Man xajrxohi tu hastam!»
28|21|Tarsonu nigaron az sahr ʙerun sud. Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro az sitamkoron nacot deh!»
28|22|Cun ʙa coniʙi Madjan ravon sud, guft: «Sojad Parvardigori man maro ʙa rohi rost rahʙari kunad»
28|23|Cun ʙa oʙi Madjan rasid, guruhe az mardumro did, ki corpojoni xudro oʙ medihand va pusti sarason du zanro did, ki gusfandoni xudro ʙozmeronand, Guft: «Sumo ci mekuned?» Guftand: «Mo oʙ namedihem, to on goh, ki cuponon ʙozgardand, ki padari mo pire ʙuzurgvor ast»
28|24|Gusfandonro oʙ dod. Sipas ʙa soja ʙozgastu guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, man ʙa on ne'mate, ki ʙarojam mefiristi, muhtocam»
28|25|Jake az on du zan, ki ʙa ozarm (sarm) roh meraft, nazdi u omad va guft: «Padaram turo mexonad, to muzdi oʙ dodanatro ʙidihad». Cun nazdi u omad va sarguzasti xud ʙiguft, guft: «Matars, ki tu az mardumi zolim nacot joftai»
28|26|Jake az on du guft: «Ej padar, uro mardikor gir, ki agar cunin kuni, ʙehtarin mardi nerumandi ʙovarinokest, ki mardikor kardai»
28|27|Guft: «Mexoham jake az in du duxtaramro zani tu kunam, ʙa sarti on, ki hast sol mardikori man ʙosi. Va agar dah solro purra kuni, xud xidmatest va man namexoham, ki turo ʙa masaqqat afkanam. Insoolloh, maro az solehon xohj joft»
28|28|Guft: «In ast pajmon mijoni manu tu. Har jak az du muddatro, ki tamom kunam, ʙar man sitame, naxohad raft va Xudo ʙar on ci meguem, vakil ast»
28|29|Cun Muso muddatro tamom kard va ʙo zanas ravon sud, az sui Tur otase did. Ba kasoni xud guft: «In co isted, Otase didam. Sojad az on xaʙare jo porai otase ʙijovaram, to garm saved»
28|30|Cun nazdi otas omad, az kanorai rosti vodi dar on sarzamini muʙorak az on daraxt sado doda sud, ki ej Muso, man Xudoi jakto, Parvardigori cahonijonam
28|31|Asojatro ʙiparto! Cun didas, ki monandi more mecunʙad, gurezon ʙozgast va ʙa aqiʙ nanigarist. «Ej Muso, pes oju matars. Tu dar amon hasti
28|32|Dasti xud ʙa gireʙon ʙiʙar to ʙerun ojad safed ʙe hec oseʙe. Va to az vahsat ʙijoromi, dasti xud dar ʙaƣal kun. In du az coniʙi Parvardigorat huccathoi tu ʙaroi Fir'avn va atrofijoni ust, ki onon mardume nofarmonand»
28|33|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, jake az onhoro kustaam va metarsam maro ʙikusand
28|34|Va ʙarodaram Horun ʙa zaʙon az man fasehtar ast. Uro ʙa madadi man ʙifirist, to maro tasdiq kunad, ki ʙimi on doram, ki duruƣgujam sumorand»
28|35|Guft: «Turo ʙo ʙarodarat qavidast xohem kard va ʙarojaton huccate qaror medihem. Ba saʙaʙi nisonahoe, ki sumoro dodaem, ʙa sumo dast naxohand joft. Sumo va pajravonaton ƣoliʙ xohed ʙud»
28|36|Cun Muso ojoti ravsani Moro nazdason ovard, guftand; «In coduest soxta, mo az nijogonamon cunin cizhoe nasunidaem»
28|37|Va Muso guft: «Parvardigori man ʙa on kase, ki az coniʙi U ʙa hidojat omadaast va oqiʙati pisandida dar on dunjo az oni ust, ogohtar ast. Zero sitamkoron rastagor (nacotjofta) namesavand!»
28|38|Fir'avn guft: «Ej camoat, man ʙaroi sumo xudoe ƣajri xud namesinosam. Ej Homon, ʙaroi man ocur (xist) ʙipaz va torame (gunʙade) ʙaland ʙisoz, sojad xudoi Musoro ʙuʙinam, ki duruƣgujas pindoram»
28|39|U va laskarhojas ʙa nohaq dar zamin sarkasi kardand va pindostand, ki ʙa nazdi mo ʙozgardonida namesavand
28|40|Pas u va laskarhojasro giriftem va ʙa darjo partoftem. Bingar, ki oqiʙati kori sitamkoron ci guna ʙud
28|41|Va ononro az on guna pesvojone soxtem, ki mardumro ʙa otas da'vat mekunand va dar ruzi qijomat kase joriason nakunad
28|42|Dar in dunjo az pajason la'nat ravona soxtem va dar ruzi qijomat az zistrujonand
28|43|Pas az on, ki mardumi ruzgori pesinro halok soxtem, ʙa Muso kitoʙ dodem, to mardumro iʙratu hidojat va rahmat ʙosad. Sojad pand girand
28|44|On goh ki ʙa Muso farmoni amri pajƣamʙariro vahj kardem, tu na dar coniʙi ƣarʙii Tur ʙudi va na az hoziron
28|45|Vale Mo az on pas naslhoero ʙijofaridem, ki umrason ʙa daroz kasid. Va tu dar mijoni mardumi Madjan muqim naʙudi, ki ojoti Moro ʙar onho ʙixoni. Vale Mo ʙudem, ki pajomʙarone mefiristodem
28|46|Tu dar kanori Tur naʙudi, on goh ki Musoro nido kardem. Vale in rahmatest az coniʙi Parvardigorat to mardumero, ki pes az tu ʙimdihandae nadostand, ʙim dihj. Bosad, ki pandpazir savand
28|47|To cun ʙa saʙaʙi amalhoe, ki kardaand, musiʙate ʙa onho rasad, nagujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, caro pajomʙare ʙar mo nafiristodi, to az ojoti Tu pajravi kunem va az mu'minon ʙosem?»
28|48|Cun pajomʙari rostguj az coniʙi Mo ʙar onon firistoda sud, guftand: «Caro on ci ʙa Muso doda suda, ʙa u doda nasuda?» Ojo inho pes az in ʙa on ci ʙa Muso doda suda ʙud, kofir nasuda ʙudand? Va guftand, ki in har du, du codust monandi ham va mo ʙa hec jak imon nameovarem
28|49|Bigu: «Agar rost megued, az coniʙi Xudovand kitoʙe ʙijovared, ki az in du ʙehtar roh ʙinamojad, to man ham az on pajravi kunam!»
28|50|Pas agar icoʙatat nakardand, ʙidon, ki az pai havoi nafsi xud meravand va kist gumrohtar az on kas, ki ʙe on, ki rohnamoi az Xudo xohad, az pai havoi nafsi xud ravad? Zero Xudo mardumi zolimro hidojat namekunad
28|51|Barojason suxan dar suxan pajvastem, ʙosad, ki pandpazir gardand
28|52|Kasone, ki pes az in kitoʙ kitoʙason doda ʙudem, ʙa on imon meovarand
28|53|Va cun ʙar onon tilovat sud, guftand: «Ba on imon ovardem, Haqqest az coniʙi Parvardigori mo va mo pes az on taslim ʙudaem»
28|54|Inon ʙa saʙaʙi saʙre, ki kardaand, du ʙor podos doda savand. Inon ʙadiro ʙa neki dur mekunand va niz az on ci ruzijason dodaem, sadaqa mekunand
28|55|Va cun suxani ʙehudae ʙisnavand, az on rujgardoni kunand va gujand: «Kirdorhoi mo az oni mo va kirdorhoi sumo az oni sumo. Ba salomat ʙimoned. Mo xostori cohilon nestem!»
28|56|Tu har kasro, ki ʙixohi, hidojat namekuni. Xudost, ki har kiro ʙixohad, hidojat mekunad va U hidojatjoftagonro ʙehtar mesinosad
28|57|Guftand: «Agar az dini tu pajravi kunem, moro az sarzaminamon ʙarmekanand». Ojo onhoro dar harame amn coj na dodaem, ki hama guna mevaho dar on faroham mesavad va in rizqest az coniʙi Mo? Vale ʙestarinason namedonand
28|58|Ci ʙaso mardumi dehaero halok soxtem, ki az zindagii xud ducori sarmasti suda ʙudand va in xonahoi onhost, ki ʙa'd az onho andak zamone kas dar onho sukno (maskan) girift va Mo vorisi onho ʙudem
28|59|Parvardigori tu mardumi dehahoro halok nakard, to on goh, ki az xudason pajomʙare ʙar onho firistod va u ojoti Moro ʙar onho ʙixond. Va mo dehahoro noʙud kardaem, ʙa saʙaʙi on, ki mardumas sitamkor ʙudaand
28|60|Cizhoe, ki ʙa sumo doda sudaast, mato'est va oroisi in zindagii dunjavist. Hol on ki on ci nazdi Xudost, ʙehtaru mondanitar ast. Caro aqlatonro kor namefarmoed
28|61|Ojo on kas, ki uro va'dahoi nek dodaem va on va'dahoro xohad did, monandi kasest, ki uro az mato'i incahoni ʙahramand kardaem va dar ruzi qijomat ham az hozir karda sudagon ast
28|62|Va ruze, ki ononro nido medihad va megujad: «Sarikonero, ki ʙaroi Man mepindostaed, kucojand?»
28|63|Onon, ki hukm dar ʙoraason tahqiq suda megujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, inho kasone, hastand, ki mo gumrohason kardem. Az on ru gumrohason kardem, ki xud gumroh ʙudem. Az onho ʙezori mecuem va ʙa tu megaravem. Inho moro nameparastidaand»
28|64|Va gufta savad: «Aknun ʙutonatonro farjod kuned». Farjod mekunand, vale ʙa onho cavoʙ namedihand. Va cun, azoʙro ʙuʙinand, orzu kunand, ki kos az hidojatjoftagon meʙudand
28|65|Va ruze, ki Xudo nidojason kunad va gujad: «Pajomʙaronro ci guna qaʙul karded?»
28|66|Dar in ruz xaʙarho ʙar onon pusida savad va az jakdigar niz natavonand pursid
28|67|Ammo on kas, ki tavʙa karda va imon ovarda va amali soleh ʙa coj ovarda, sojad, ki az nacotjoftagon ʙosad
28|68|Parvardigori tu har ciro, ki ʙixohad, meofarinad va meixtijorad. Vale onhoro tavoni ixtijor nest. Pok ast Xudo va az har ci ʙarojas sarik mesozand va ʙartar ast
28|69|Va Parvardigori tu har ciro, ki dar dil pinhon dostaand, jo oskor kardaand, medonad
28|70|Ust Xudoi jakto. Hec xudoe ƣajri U nest. Sano (sukr) xosi Ust, ci dar in cahon va ci dar cahoni digar. Va farmon farmoni Ust. Va hamagon ʙa U ʙozgardonda mesaved
28|71|Bigu: «Ci tasavvur mekuned, agar Olloh saʙatonro to ruzi qijomat tuloni sozad? Ƣajri U kadom xudost, ki sumoro ravsani medihad? Magar namesunaved?»
28|72|Bigu: «Ci tasavvur mekuned, agar Olloh ruzatonro to ruzi qijomat tuloni sozad? Ƣajri U kadom xudost, ki sumoro saʙ medihad, ki dar on ʙijosoed? Magar nameʙined
28|73|Va az rahmati U on ki ʙaroi sumo saʙu ruzro padid ovard, to dar on jak ʙijosoed va dar in jak ʙa talaʙi ruzi ʙarxezed, ʙosad, ki sukr gued»
28|74|Va ruze, ki Xudo nidojason kunad va gujad: «Sarikone, ki ʙaroi Man tasavvur mekarded, kucojand
28|75|Va az har millate sohide ʙijovarem va guem: «Daleli xud ʙijovared. On goh ʙidonand, ki haq az oni Olloh ast va on ʙuton, ki ʙa duruƣ xudo mexondand noʙud savand»
28|76|Qorun az qavmi Muso ʙud, ki ʙar onho afzuni cust. Va ʙa u cunon ganchoe dodem, ki ʙardostani kalidhojas ʙar guruhe az mardumi nerumand dusvor menamud. On goh, ki qavmas ʙa u guftand: «Sarmast maʙos, zero Xudo sarmastonro dust nadorad
28|77|Dar on ci Xudojat ato kardaast, cahoni oxiratro ʙicuj va nasiʙi xudro az dunjo faromus makun. Va hamcunon ki Xudo ʙa tu neki karda, neki kun va dar zamin az pai fasod marav, ki Xudo fasodkunandagonro dust nadorad!»
28|78|Guft: «On ci ʙa man doda suda, ʙa saʙaʙi donisi man ʙudaast». Ojo nadonistaast, ki Xudo pes az u naslhoero halok karda, ki quvvatason az u afzuntar va sumorason ʙestar ʙudaast? Va in gunahkoronro az gunohason namepursand
28|79|Orosta ʙa zevarhoi xud ʙa mijoni mardumas omad. Onon, ki xostori zindagii dunjavi ʙudand, guftand: «Ej kos, on ci ʙa Qorun doda suda, moro niz meʙud, ki u sohiʙi nasiʙi ʙuzurg ast»
28|80|Ammo donisjoftagon guftand: «Voj ʙar sumo. Baroi onho, ki imon meovarand va korhoi soista mekunand, savoʙi Xudo ʙehtar ast. Va ʙa in savoʙ soʙiron rasand»
28|81|Pas u va xonaasro dar zamin furu ʙurdem va dar ʙaroʙari Xudo hec guruhe nadost, ki jorias kunad va xud jori kardani xudro nametavonist
28|82|Ruzi digar on kason, ki diruz orzu mekardand, ki ʙa coi u meʙudand, meguftand: «Acaʙo, ki Xudo ruzii har kasro, ki xohad farovon kunad jo tang sozad. Agar Xudo ʙa mo niz ne'mati farovon doda ʙud, moro niz dar zamin furu meʙurd. Nameʙini, ki kofiron nacot namejoʙand?»
28|83|In cahoni oxiratro az oni kasone soxtaem, ki dar in cahon na xohoni takaʙʙuri hastand va na xohoni fasod. Va sarancomi nek az oni parhezgoron ast
28|84|Har kas, ki kori neke ʙa coj orad, ʙehtar az on muzd joʙad va har ki gunohe kunad, pas onho, ki gunoh kardaand, ʙa andozai amalason cazo doda savand
28|85|On kas, ki Qur'onro ʙar tu farz kardaast, turo ʙa va'dagohat ʙozmegardonad. Bigu: «Parvardigori man ʙehtar medonad, ki ci kase ʙar rohi rost ast va ci kase dar gumrohii oskor ast»
28|86|Agar rahmati Parvardigorat naʙud, umedi onro nadosti, ki in kitoʙ ʙar tu doda savad. Pas naʙojad pustiʙoni kofiron ʙosi
28|87|Pas az on, ki ojathoi Xudo ʙar tu nozil sud, turo az on ʙeroh nakunand. Mardumro ʙa sui Parvardigorat ʙixon va az musrikon maʙos
28|88|Bo Xudoi jakto xudoi digarero maxon. Hec xudoe ƣajrn U nest. Har cize noʙud sudani ast ƣajri zoti U. Farmon, farmoni Ust va hama ʙa nazdi u ʙozgardonida saved
29|1|Alif, lom, mim
29|2|Ojo mardum mepindorand, ki «Imon ovardaem». megujandu, ʙe imtihonu sancis guzosta mesavand
29|3|Alʙatta mardumero, ki pes az onho ʙudand, ozmudem, to Xudo kasonero, ki rost guftaand, ma'lum dorad va duruƣgujonro cudo kunad
29|4|Ojo onhoe, ki sodirkunandai gunoh mesavand, pindostaand, ki az Mo megurezand? Ci ʙad hukm mekunand
29|5|Har kas, ki ʙa didori Xudo u med medorad, ʙidonad, ki va'dai Xudo omadanist va U sunavovu donost
29|6|Har ki cihod kunad, ʙa naf'i xud kardaast, zero Xudo az hamai cahonijon ʙeehtijoc ast
29|7|Gunohoni ononro, ki imon ovardand va korhoi soista kardand, nest mekunem va ʙehtar az on ci amal kardaand, mukofotason medihem
29|8|Ba odami suporis kardem, ki ʙa padaru modari xud neki kunad. Va agar on du ʙikusand, ki tu cizero, ki ʙa on ogoh nesti, sariki Man qaror dihi, ito'atason makun. Bozgasti hamai sumo ʙa sui Man ast va sumoro ʙa korhoe, ki mekardaed, ogoh mekunam
29|9|Kasonero, ki imon ovardand va amalhoi soista kardand, dar guruhi solehon darovardem
29|10|Ba'ze az mardum megujand: «Ba Xudo imon ovardaem. Va cun dar rohi Xudo ozore ʙuʙinand, on ozorro cun azoʙi Xudo ʙa sumor meovarand. Va cun az sui Parvardigori tu madade rasad, megujand: «Mo niz ʙo sumo ʙudem». Ojo Xudo ʙa on ci dar dilhoi mardumi cahon meguzarad, ogohtar nest
29|11|Alʙatta, Xudo medonad, ki mu'minon ci kasonand va munofiqon ci kason
29|12|Kofiron ʙa mu'minon guftand: «Ba rohi mo ʙijoed, ʙori gunohaton ʙar gardani mo. Hol on ki inho ʙori gunohi kasero ʙar gardan naxohand girift va duruƣ megujand
29|13|Balki ʙori gunohi xud va ʙorhoe ʙo ʙori xud ʙar gardan xohand guzost va dar ruzi qijomat ʙa saʙaʙi duruƣhoe, ki ʙar ham meʙoftaand, ʙozxost xohand sud
29|14|Mo Nuhro ʙar mardumas ʙa pajomʙari firistodem. U hazor solu pancoh sol kam dar mijoni onon ʙizist. Va cun mardume zolim ʙudand, tufonason furu girift
29|15|U va kasonero, ki dar kisti ʙudand, nacot dodem va on tufonro nisoni iʙrate ʙaroi cahonijon gardonidem
29|16|Va niz Iʙrohimro ʙa pajomʙari firistodem, on goh ki ʙa mardumas guft: «Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparasted va az U ʙitarsed. In ʙarojaton ʙehtar ast, agar mardume dono ʙosed
29|17|Sumo ƣajri Xudoi jakto ʙutonero meparasted va duruƣhoi ʙuzurg mepardozed. Onhoe, ki ƣajri Xudoi jakto meparasted, nametavonand sumoro ruzi dihand. Az Xudoi jakto ruzi ʙicued va Uro iʙodat kuned va sukr gued, zero ʙa sui U ʙozgardonida mesaved»
29|18|Agar sumo takziʙ mekuned (duruƣ meʙarored), mardumone ham, ki pes az sumo ʙudand, takziʙ mekardand. Va ʙar uhdai pajomʙar ƣajri taʙliƣe ravsangar cizi digare nest
29|19|Ojo nameʙinand, ki Xudo ci guna maxluqro meofarinad va pas az nesti ʙozas megardonad? In kor ʙar Xudo oson ast
29|20|Bigu: «Dar zamin sajr kuned va ʙingared, ki ci guna Xudo mavcudotro ofarida. Sipas ofarinisi oxirinro padid meovarad. Zero Xudovand ʙar har cize tavonost
29|21|Har kiro ʙixohad, azoʙ mekunad va ʙar har ki xohad, rahmat meovard va ham ʙa nazdi U ʙozgardonida mesaved
29|22|Sumo nametavoned az Xudo ʙigurezed, na dar zamin va na dar osmon va sumoro ƣajri U hec korsozu jovare nest!»
29|23|Va onon, ki ʙa ojoti Xudo va didori U imon nadorand, az rahmati man noumedand va onhoro azoʙe dardovar ast
29|24|Cavoʙi qavmi u in ʙud, ki guftand: «Uro ʙikusad jo ʙisuzoned». Va Xudojas az otas nacot dod. Va dar in ʙaroi mu'minon iʙrathost
29|25|Guft: «Sumo ʙutonero ʙa coi Xudoi jakto ʙa xudoi giriftaed to dar in zindagonii dunjo mijonaton dusti ʙosad, vale dar ruzi qijomat munkiri jakdigar mesaved va jakdigarro la'nat mekuned va cojaton dar otas ast va hec jovare nadored
29|26|Lut ʙa U imon ovard va guft: «Man ʙa sui Parvardigoram muhocirat (tarki vatan) mekunam, zero U piruzmandu hakim ast!»
29|27|Va Ishoqu Ja'quʙro ʙa u ʙaxsidem va dar farzandoni u pajomʙarivu kitoʙ nihodem. Va muzdasonro dar dunjo dodem va u dar oxirat az solehon ast
29|28|Va Lutro pajomʙari dodem. Ba qavmi xud guft: «Sumo kore zistro pesa kardaed, ki hec jak az mardumi cahon pes az sumo cunin namekardaast
29|29|Ojo ʙo mardon meomezed va rohzani mekuned va dar maxfili xud korhoi nopisand mekuned?» Cavoʙi qavmas in ʙud, ki guftand: «Agar rost megui, azoʙi Xudoro ʙar sari mo ʙijovar!»
29|30|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro ʙar mardumi taʙaxkor (rasodkor) nusrat deh!»
29|31|Cun firistodagoni Mo Iʙrohimro muƶda ovardand, guftand: «Mo mardumi in deharo halok xohem kard, ki mardume zolim hastand»
29|32|Guft: «Lut dar on cost». Guftand: «Mo ʙehtar medonem, ci kase dar on cost. U va xonadonasro, ƣajri zanasro, ki dar hamon co xohad mond, nacot medihem»
29|33|Cun firistodagoni Mo nazdi Lut omadand, ƣamgin sud va dar ƣami korason ʙimond. Guftand: «Matars va ƣamgii maʙos, tuvu xonadonatro, ƣajri zanatro, ki dar hamon co xohad mond, nacot medihem
29|34|Mo ʙa mardumi in deha ʙa saʙaʙi fisqe, ki mekunand, az osmon azoʙ nozil mekunem»
29|35|Alʙatta az on deha ʙaroi xiradmandon iʙrate ravsan ʙar coj guzostem
29|36|Va ʙarodarason Su'ajʙro ʙa Madjan firistodem. Guft: «Ej qavmi man, Xudoro ʙiparasted va ʙa ruzi qijomat umedvor ʙosed va dar zamin ʙa taʙahkori makused
29|37|Pas takziʙas kardand (duruƣas ʙarovardand) da zilzila ononro furu girift va dar xonahoi xud ʙar coj murdand
29|38|Va Odu Samudro halok kardem. Va in az maskanhojason ʙarojaton oskor ast. Sajton korhojasonro dar nazarason ʙijorost va ononro az roh ʙozdost. Va hol on ki mardume sohiʙi aqlu xus ʙudand
29|39|Va niz Qorunu Fir'avn va Homonro, ki Muso ʙo dalelhoi ravsani xud nazdi onho omad. Onho dar zamin sarkasi mekardand, vale natavonistand az Xudo ʙigurezand
29|40|Hamaro ʙa gunohason furu giriftem: ʙar ʙa'ze ʙodhoi regʙor firistodem, ʙa'zero farjodi saxt furu girift, ʙa'zero dar zamin furu ʙurdem, ʙa'zero ƣarq soxtem. Va Xudo ʙa onho sitam namekard, onho xud ʙa xudason sitam karda ʙudand
29|41|Misoli onon, ki ƣajri Xudoro avlijo giriftand, misli ankaʙut (tortanak) ast, ki xonae ʙisoxt. Va kos medonistand, alʙatta susttarin xonaho xonai ankaʙut ast
29|42|Xudoj jakto medrnad, ki ci cizhoro ʙa coi U ʙa xudoi mexonand va Ust ƣoliʙu hakim
29|43|In misolhoro ʙaroi mardum meorem va onro faqat donojon darmejoʙand
29|44|Xudo osmonhovu zaminro ʙa rosti ʙijofarid va dar in iʙratest ʙaroi mu'minon
29|45|Har ciro az in kitoʙ ʙar tu vahj sudaast, tilovat kun. Va namoz ʙigzor, ki namoz odamiro az fahsovu munkar ʙozmedorad va zikri Xudo ʙuzurgtar ast va Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekuned, ogoh ast
29|46|Bo ahli kitoʙ ʙa nekutarin tarze ʙahs kuned. Magar ʙo onho, ki sitam pesa kardand. Va ʙigued: «Ba on ci ʙar mo nozil suda va on ci ʙar sumo nozil sudaast, imon ovardem. Va Xudoi movu Xudoi sumo jakest va mo dar ʙaroʙari U gardan nihodaem»
29|47|Hamcunon in kitoʙro ʙar tu nozil kardem va ahli kitoʙ ʙa on imon meovarand va az inho niz kasone ʙa on imon meovarand va ƣajri kofiron kase ojoti Moro inkor namekunad
29|48|Tu pes az Qur'on hec kitoʙero namexondi va ʙa dasti xud kitoʙe namenavisti. Agar cunon ʙud, ahli ʙotil ʙa sak aftoda ʙudand
29|49|Balki Qur'on ojotest ravsan, ki dar sinai ahli donis coj dorad. Va ojoti Moro sitamkoron inkor mekunand
29|50|Va guftand: «Caro az coniʙi Parvardigoras ojote ʙar u nozil namesavad?» Bigu: «Ojot dar nazdi Xudost va man ʙimdihandae oskor hastam»
29|51|Ojo onhoro kifoja nest, ki ʙar tu kitoʙ firistodaem va ʙar onho xonda mesavad. Dar in kitoʙ ʙaroi mu'minon rahmatu pand ast
29|52|Bigu: «Xudo ʙa guvohi mijoni manu sumo kofist. On ciro, ki dar osmonhovu zamin ast, medonad. Kasone, ki ʙa ʙotil garavidand va ʙa Xudo kofir sudand, zijonkoronand»
29|53|Az tu ʙa sitoʙ azoʙro metalaʙand. Agar onro zamone mu'ajjan naʙud, ʙar onho meomad. Va nogahon va ʙe on, ki xaʙar savand, ʙar onho furud xohad omad
29|54|Az tu ʙa sitoʙ azoʙro metalaʙand, hol on ki cahannam ʙar kofiron ihota dorad
29|55|Ruze, ki azoʙ az ʙoloi saru zeri poj onhoro dar ʙar girad va Xudo ʙigujad: «Ba xotiri amalhoe, ki mekarded, inak azoʙro ʙicased!»
29|56|Ej ʙandagoni man, ki ʙa man imon ovardaed, zamini man vase' ast, pas tanho Maro ʙiparasted
29|57|Har kase casandai ta'mi marg ast. Va ʙa sui Mo ʙozgardonida saved
29|58|Kasonero, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, dar ƣurfahoi ʙihist coj dihem. Az zeri on cujhoi oʙ ravon ast. Dar on co covidona ʙimonand. Amalkunandagonro ci neku muzdest
29|59|onho, ki saʙr varzidand va ʙar Parvardigorason tavakkal mekunand
29|60|Ci ʙisjor cunʙandagone, ki tavoni tahsili ruzii xud nadorand va Xudo onhoro va sumoro ruzi medihad. Va U sunavovu donost
29|61|Agar az onho ʙipursi: «Ci kase osmonhovu zaminro ofarida va oftoʙu mohro rom kardaast?» Xohand guft: «Xudoi jakto». Pas az ci saʙaʙ aqida digargun mekunand
29|62|Xudo ruzii har jak az ʙandagonasro, ki ʙixohad, farovon mekunad jo ʙar u tang megirad. Zero Xudo ʙa hama ciz donost
29|63|Agar az onho ʙipursi: «Ci kase az osmon ʙoron firistod va zamin murdaro ʙa on zinda kard?» Xohand guft: «Xudo jakto». Bigu; «Sukr Xudorost!» Vale ʙestarinason darnamejoʙand
29|64|Zindagonii in dunjo lahvu la'aʙ (ʙozi) ast. Agar ʙidonand, caxoni oxirat cahoni zindagonist
29|65|Cun ʙa kisti nisastand, Xudoro ʙo ixlos ilticovu iʙodat kunand va cun nacotason dod va ʙa xuski ovard, sirk ovarand
29|66|to ne'matero, ki ʙa onon ato karda ʙudem, kufron kunand va ʙarxurdor savand. Ba zudi xohand donist
29|67|Ojo nadonistaand, ki haramro coi amni mardum qaror dodem, hol on ki mardum dar atrofason ʙa asorat girifta mesavand? Ojo ʙa ʙotil imon meovarand va ne'mati Xudoro kufron mekunand
29|68|Pas kist sitamkortar az on, ki ʙar Xudo duruƣ meʙandad jo ʙa hangome ki haq ʙa sui u ojad, takziʙas mekunad (duruƣ mesumorad)? Ojo dar cahannam cojgohe ʙaroi kofiron nest
29|69|Kasonero, ki dar rohi Mo cihod kunand, ʙa rohhoi xud hidojatason mekunem va Xudo ʙo nekukoron ast
30|1|Alif, lom, mim
30|2|Rumijon maƣluʙ sudand
30|3|dar nazdiki in sarzamin va pas az maƣluʙ sudan ʙori digar ƣoliʙ xohand sud
30|4|dar muddati cand sol. Farmon, farmoni Xudost, ci pes az piruzi va ci ʙa'd az on. Va dar on ruz mu'minon sodmon mesavand
30|5|ʙa jorii Xudo. Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, jori mekunad, zero ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
30|6|Xudo va'da dodaast, ʙa va'dai xud xilof nakunad, vale ʙestari mardum namedonand
30|7|Onon ʙa zohiri zindagii dunjo ogohand va az oxirat ʙexaʙarand
30|8|Ojo ʙo xud nameandesand, ki Xudo osmonhovu zaminro va har ci dar mijoni onhost, ʙa haq va to muddate mahdud, ofaridaast? Va ʙisjore az mardum ʙa didori Parvardigorason imon nadorand
30|9|Ojo dar zamin namegardand, to ʙingarand, ki ci guna ʙudaast oqiʙati kasone, ki pes az onho zistaand? Kasone, ki tavonason ʙestar ʙudaast va zaminro ʙa sudgor zadan zeru ru karda va ʙestar az inho oʙodas soxta ʙudand va pajomʙarone ʙo mu'cizaho ʙar onho firistoda suda ʙud. Xudo ʙa onho zulm namekard, onon xud ʙa xudason zulm mekardand
30|10|Sipas oqiʙati on kason, ki korhoi ʙad kardand, noguvortar ʙud. Zero inho ojoti Xudoro duruƣ ʙarovardand va onhoro ʙa masxara giriftand
30|11|Xudo mavcudotro meofarinad, on goh digar ʙora ʙozmegardonad, on goh hama ʙa sui U ʙozgardonda mesaved
30|12|Ruze, ki qijomat ʙarpo savad, gunohkoron hajratzada ʙimonand
30|13|Onhoro az mijoni ʙutonason safe'one (nacotdihandae) nest. Va digar ʙa ʙutoni xud ʙovar nadorand
30|14|Va cun qijomat ʙarpo savad, dar on ruz az jakdigar cudo savand (mu'minon az kofiron)
30|15|Ammo onho, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, dar cannat ʙa sodmoni ʙarxurdorand
30|16|Va ammo onhoe, ki kofir sudaand va ojoti Moro duruƣ meʙarorand va didori oxiratro duruƣ mepindorand, hamaro dar azoʙ hozir orand
30|17|Xudoro ʙisitoed, ʙa on hangom ki ʙa saʙ darmeoed va ʙa on hangom ki ʙa suʙh darmeoed
30|18|Sukr Urost dar osmonhovu zamin, ʙa hangomi saʙ va ʙa hangome ki ʙa nimruz merased
30|19|Zindaro az murda ʙerun orad va murdaro az zinda. Va zaminro pas az murdanas zinda mesozad va sumo niz incunin az gurho ʙerun mesaved
30|20|Az nisonahoi qudrati Ust, ki sumoro az xok ʙijofarid to inson suded va ʙa har su parokanda gasted
30|21|Va az nisonahoi qudrati Ust, ki ʙarojaton az cinsi xudaton hamsarone ofarid, to ʙa onho oromis joʙed va mijoni sumo dustivu mehruʙoni nihod. Dar in iʙrathoest ʙaroi mardume, ki tafakkur mekunand
30|22|Va az nisonahoi qudrati Ust ofarinisi osmonhovu zamin va gunogunii zaʙonhovu ranghojaton. Dar in iʙrathoest ʙaroi donojon
30|23|Va az nisonahoi qudrati U xoʙidani sumost dar saʙ va ruz ʙa talaʙi ruzi ʙarxostani sumost. Dar in iʙrathoest ʙaroi mardume, ki mesunavand
30|24|Va az nisonahoi qudrati Ust, ki ʙarqro ʙa qasdi ʙimu umed ʙa sumo menamojonad. Va az osmon ʙoron mefiristad to zamini murdaro ʙa on zinda sozad. Dar in iʙrathoest ʙaroi kasone, ki ʙa aql darmejoʙand
30|25|Va az nisonahoi qudrati Ust, ki osmonu zamin ʙa farmoni U ʙarpoj istodaand. Sipas vaqte, ki sumoro az zamin faro mexonad, sumo az zamin ʙerun meoed
30|26|Az oni Ust har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast va hama farmonʙardori U hastand
30|27|Ust, ki mavcudotro meofarinad, sipas onhoro ʙozmegardonad. Va in kor ʙar U osontar ast. Urost sifati ʙartari dar osmonhovu zamin va Ust ƣoliʙu hakim
30|28|Baroi sumo az xudaton misole meovarad: magar ʙandagonaton dar on ci ʙa sumo ruzi dodaem, ʙo sumo sarik hastand, to dar mol ʙo sumo ʙaroʙar ʙosand va hamcunon ki sumo ozodon az jakdigar metarsed, az onho ham ʙimnok ʙosed? Ojotro ʙaroi mardume, kn aql mekunand, in tavr tafsil medihem
30|29|Ore, sitamkoron ʙe hec donise az havoi nafsi xud pajravi kardaand. Onro, ki Xudo gumroh kardaast, ci kase hidojat mekunad? Onhoro hec jovare nest
30|30|Ba jaktoparasti ruj ʙa din ovar. Fitratest, ki Xudo hamaro ʙa on fitrat ʙijofaridaast va dar ofarinisi Xudo taƣjire nest. Dini poku pojdor in ast. Vale ʙestari mardum namedonand
30|31|Ba U ʙozgarded va az U ʙitarsed va namoz ʙiguzored va az musrikon naʙosed
30|32|Az onon maʙosed, ki dini xudro pora-pora kardand va firqa-firqa sudand va har firqae ʙa har ci dost, dilxus ʙud
30|33|Cun ʙar odamijon zijone rasad, Parvardigorasonro ʙixonand va ʙa dargohi U tavʙa kunand va cun rahmati xud ʙa onho ʙicasonad, guruhero ʙini, ki ʙa Parvardigorason sirk meovarand
30|34|Pas ne'matero, ki ʙa onho dodaem, nosukri kunand, Aknun mutamatte' (ʙahramand) saved, ʙa zudi, ki xohed donist
30|35|Ojo ʙarojason dalele nozil kardem, to az cize, ki ʙo Xudo sarik mesozand, suxan gufta ʙosad
30|36|Cun ʙa mardum rahmate ʙicasonem, sodmon mesavand va cun ʙa saʙaʙi korhoe, ki kardaand, rance ʙa onho rasad, nogahon noumed megardand
30|37|Ojo nameʙinand, ki Xudo ruzii har kasro, ki ʙixohad, farovon mekunad jo uro tangruzi mesozad? Dar in iʙrathoest ʙaroi mardume, ki imon meovarand
30|38|Haqqi xesovandonu miskin va dar roh mondaro ado kun. In ʙehtar ast ʙaroi kasone, ki xusnudii Xudoro mecujand va onho nacotjoftagonand
30|39|Mole, ki ʙa riʙo medihed, to dar amvoli mardum afzun savad, nazdi Xudo hec afzun namesavad va mole, ki ʙaroi xusnudii Xudo az ʙoʙati zakot medihed, zijod savad, kasone ki cunin kunand, mukofoti muzo'af (ducand) dorand
30|40|Xudost, on ki sumoro ʙijofarid, sipas ruzi dod, sipas memironad, sipas zinda mekunad. Ojo kasone, ki sariki Xudo mesozed, hec az in korho tavonand? Pok ast U va az har ci ʙarojas sarik meovarand, ʙartar (ʙolotar) ast
30|41|Ba saʙaʙi amalhoi mardum fasod dar xuskivu darjo oskor sud, to ʙa onon cazoi ʙa'ze az korhojasonro ʙicasonad; sojad, ki ʙozgardand
30|42|Bigu: «Dar zamin ʙigarded va ʙingared, ki oqiʙati pesinijon ki ʙestarinason az musrikon ʙudand, ci guna ʙudaast»
30|43|Ba dini poki pojdor ruj ʙijovar, pes az on ki ruze faro rasad, ki az amri Xudo ʙozgastanas naʙosad. Dar on ruz mardum du guruh savand
30|44|kasone, ki kofir ʙosand, kufrason ʙa zijonason ʙosad va onho, ki kore soista karda ʙosand, ʙaroi xud podose (mukofoti) neku omoda kardaand
30|45|to kasonero, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, az fazli xud muzd dihad. Zero Xudo kofironro dust nadorad
30|46|Va az nisonahoi qudrati U on, ki ʙodhoi muƶdadihandaro mefiristad, to rahmati Xudro ʙa sumo ʙicasonad va to kistiho ʙa farmoni U ravon ʙosand va az fazli U ruzi ʙicued. Sojad, ki sukr gued
30|47|Va pes az tu pajomʙaronero ʙar qavmason firistodem. Onon ʙo dalelhoi ravsani xud nazdason omadand. Va Mo az kasone, ki gunoh kardand, intiqom giriftem va jori dodani mu'minon ʙar uhdai Mo ʙud
30|48|Xudost, ki ʙodhoro mefiristad, to aʙrhoro ʙarangezad va cunon ki xohad, ʙar osmon pahn kunad va onro pora-pora kunad va ʙini, ki ʙoron az daruni aʙrho ʙerun meojad. Va cun ʙoronro ʙa har ki xohad az ʙandagonas ʙirasonad, sodmon savand
30|49|agarci pes az on ki ʙoron ʙar onho ʙiʙorad, noumed ʙudaand
30|50|Pas ʙa osori rahmati Xudo ʙingar, ki ci guna zaminro pas az murdanas zinda mekunad. Cunin Xudoe zindakunandai murdagon ast va ʙar har kore tavonost
30|51|Va agar ʙode ʙifiristem, ki kistahoro zard ʙuʙinand az on pas hama kofir savand
30|52|Tu nametavoni murdagonro sunavo sozi va agar inho niz az tu ʙozgardand, ovozi xudro ʙa – gusi on karon narasoni
30|53|Tu hidojatkunandai noʙinojon az gumrohijason nesti. Tu sadojatro tanho ʙa gusi kasone merasoni, ki ʙa ojoti Mo imon ovardaand va taslim sudaand
30|54|Xudost, ki sumoro notavon ʙijofarid va pas az notavoni ʙoquvvat soxt, on goh pas az ʙoquvvati notavonivu piri ovard. Har ci ʙixohad, meofarinad va U donovu tavonost
30|55|Ruze, ki qijomat ʙarpo savad, kofiron savgand xurand, ki zijoda az soa'te dar gur naoromidaand. Ore, incunin az haq kacrav mesudand
30|56|Onon, ki donisu imon doda sudaand, gujand: Sumo muvofiqi kitoʙi Xudo to ruzi qijomat dar gur oramidaed va in ruzi qijomat ast va sumo namedonistaed»
30|57|Dar in ruz uzrxohii sitamkoron ʙa holason naf' nadihad va az onho naxohand, ki tavʙa kunand
30|58|Mo dar in Qur'on ʙaroi mardum har guna masal ovardaem. Va cun ojae ʙarojason ʙijovari, kofiron xohand guft: «Sumo ʙehudagujone ʙes nested!»
30|59|Incunin Xudo ʙar dilhoi kasone, ki az donoi ʙeʙahraand, muhr menihad
30|60|Pas saʙr kun, ki va'dai Xudo haq ast. Maʙod; onon, ki ʙa marhalai jaqin narasidaand, turo ʙesuʙotu ʙezoʙita gardonand
31|1|Alif, lom, mim
31|2|Inho ojahoi kitoʙi hikmatomez ast
31|3|Nekukoronro hidojatu rahmatest
31|4|onon, ki namoz meguzorandu zakot medihand va ʙa oxirat jaqin dorand
31|5|Inho az coniʙi Parvardigorason hidojat joftaand va inho nacotjoftagonand
31|6|Ba'ze az mardum xaridori suxanoni ʙehudaand, to ʙa nodoni mardumro az rohi Xudo gumroh kunand va Qur'onro ʙa masxara megirand. Nasiʙi inho azoʙost xorkunanda
31|7|Va cun ojoti Mo ʙar onho xonda savad, ʙo xudpisandi ruj ʙargardonand, cunon ki gui nasunidaand. Jo monandi kase, ki gushojas sangin (vaznin) suda ʙosad. Uro ʙa azoʙe dardovar muƶda deh
31|8|Nasiʙi onon, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙoƣhoi purne'mati ʙihist ast
31|9|Dar on co covidonand, va'dai Xudo rost ast. U ƣoliʙu hakim ast
31|10|Osmonhoro ʙe hec sutune, ki ʙuʙined, ʙijofarid va ʙar rui zamin kuhhoro ʙijafkand, to nalarzonadaton va az har guna cunʙandae dar on ʙiparokand. Va az osmon oʙ firistodem va dar zamin har guna gijohi nekue rujonidem
31|11|In ofarinisi Xudost. Pas ʙa Man nison dihed onho, ki ƣajri U hastand, ci ofaridaand. Balki zolimoni dar gumrohii oskore hastand
31|12|Alʙatta ʙa Luqmon hikmat dodemu guftetm: «Xudoro sukr guj, zero har ki sukr gujad, ʙa naf'i xud sukr gufta va har ki nosukri kunad, Xudo ʙenijozu (ʙeehtijoc) sitois kardanist!»
31|13|Va Luqmon ʙa pisaras guft va uro pand medod, ki ej pisaraki man, ʙa Xudo sirk majovar, zero sirk zulmest ʙuzurg
31|14|Odamiro dar ʙorai padaru modaras suporis kardem. Modaras ʙa u tomila sud va har ruz notavontar mesud va pas az du sol az siras ʙozgirift. Va suporis kardem, ki Marovu padaru modaratro sukr guj, ki ʙozgasti tu nazdi man ast
31|15|Agar on du ʙa kusis az tu ʙixohand, to cizero, ki namedoni cist, ʙo Man sarik gardoni, ito'atason nakun. Dar dunjo ʙo onho ʙa tarife pisandida zindagi kun va xud rohi kasonero, ki ʙa dargohi Man ʙozmegardand, dar pes gir. Bozgasti hamai sumo ʙa sui Man ast va Man az korhoe, ki mekardaed, ogohaton mekunam
31|16|Ej pisaraki man! «Agar amal ʙa qadri jak donai xardal dar daruni xarsange jo dar osmonho jo dar zamin, ʙosad, Xudo ʙa hisoʙas meovarad, ki U zarraʙinu ogoh ast
31|17|Ej pisaraki man! Namoz ʙiguzor va amr ʙa ma'rufu nahj az munkar kun va ʙar har ci ʙar tu rasad, saʙr kun, ki in az korhoest, ki naʙojad dar onho ʙeparvoi kard
31|18|Ba takaʙʙur az mardum ruj magardon va ʙa xudpisandi ʙar zamin roh marav, zero Xudo hec takaʙʙuri faxrfurusero dust nadorad
31|19|Dar raftorat rohi mijonaro ʙarguzin va ovozatro furud or, ja'ne ʙalandi ʙehad nakun, zero noxustarini ovozho ovozi xaron ast
31|20|Ojo nadidaed, ki Xudo har ciro, ki dar osmonhovu zamin ast, romi sumo kardaast va ne'mathoi xudro ci oskoru ci pinhon ʙa tamomi ʙar sumo ato kardaast? Va ʙa'ze az mardum ʙe hec donise jo rohnamoevu kitoʙi ravsane dar ʙorai Xudo cidol (ʙahs) mekunand
31|21|Va cun ʙa onho ʙigujand: «Ba on ci Xudo nozil kardaast, pajravi kuned», gujand: «Na! Mo az dine, ki padaroni xudro ʙar on joftaem, pajravi mekunem». Agarci sajton ʙa azoʙi otasason da'vat karda ʙosad
31|22|Har ki rui xud ʙa Xudo kunad va nekukor ʙosad, alʙatta ʙa dastgirai ustuvore cang zadaast va pojoni hamai korho ʙa sui Xudost
31|23|On kas, ki kofir sudaast, kufras turo ƣamgin nasozad. Bozgastason nazdi Most. Pas ʙa korhoe, ki kardaand, ogohason mekunem. Zero Xudo ʙa on ci dar dilho meguzarad, ogoh ast
31|24|Andake komjoʙason mesozem, sipas ʙa ʙecoragi ʙa azoʙi saxtason mekasonem
31|25|Agar az onho ʙipursi: «Ci kase osmonhovu zaminro ofaridaast?» Xohand guft: «Xudo». Bigu: «Sukr Xudoro!» Balki ʙestarason nodonand
31|26|Az oni Xudost on ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast va Xudo ʙenijozu sutudanist! (sukr guftanist)
31|27|Va agar hamai daraxtoni rui zamin qalam savand va dare murakkaʙ (rang) va haft darjoi digar ʙa madadas ʙijojad, suxanoni Xudo pojon namejoʙad. Va Xudo piruzmandu hakim ast
31|28|Ofarinisi hamai sumo va ʙoz zinda kardanaton tanho monandi zinda kardani jak tan ast Alʙatta Xudo sunavovu ʙinost
31|29|Ojo nadidai, ki Xudo az saʙ kam mekunadu ʙa ruz meafzojad va az ruz kam mekunadu ʙa saʙ meafzojad va oftoʙu mohro romi xud soxt, ki har jak to zamone mu'ajjan dar harakat ast? Va Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekuned, ogoh ast
31|30|In ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki Xudoi jakto haq ast va har ci ʙa ƣajri U mexonand, ʙotil ast va Xudost ʙalandmartaʙavu ʙuzurgvor
31|31|Ojo nadidai, ki kisti ʙa ne'mati Xudo dar darjo ravon mesavad, to Xudo ʙa'ze az ojoti qudrati xudro ʙa sumo ʙinamojonad? Dar in ʙaroi mardumi saʙrkunandai sukrguzor iʙrathost
31|32|Va cun mavchoi azim monandi aʙrho onhoro furu pusad, Xudoro az rui ixlos dar dil ʙixonand. Va cun nacotason dihad va ʙa xuski ʙarad, ʙa'ze ʙa ahdi xud vafo kunand. Va cuz ƣaddoroni (ʙevafojoni) kofiri ne'mat ojoti Moro inkor nakunand
