31|33|Ej mardum, az Parvardigoraton ʙitarsed va az ruze, ki hec padare cazoi farzandro ʙa uhda nagirad va hec farzande cazoi padarro uhdador nasavad, ʙitarsed. Va'dai Xudo haq ast. Zindagii dunjo fireʙaton nadihad va niz sajtoni fireʙkor ʙa karami Xudo fireʙaton nasozad
31|34|Xudost, ki medonad, ki qijomat ci vaqt meojad. Ust, ki ʙoron meʙoronad va az on ci dar sikamhoi zanhoi homila ast, ogoh ast. Va hec kas namedonad, ki fardo ci ciz ʙa dast xohad ovard va kase namedonad, ki dar kadom zamin xohad murd. Xudo donovu ogoh ast
32|1|Alif, Lom, Mim
32|2|Nozil sudani in kitoʙ, ki dar on hec sakke nest, az coniʙi Parvardigori cahonijon ast
32|3|Ojo megujand: «(Qur'onro) xudas ʙoftaast?» Na, suxanest ʙarhaq az coniʙi Parvardigorat, to mardumero, ki pes az tu ʙimdihandae nadostaand, tarsoni. Sojad ʙa rohi hidojat ravand
32|4|Xudost, ki osmonhovu zaminro va on ci mijoni onhost, dar sas ruz ʙijofarid va on goh ʙa ars pardoxt. Sumoro cuz U korsozu safe'e nest. Ojo pand namegired
32|5|Korro az osmon to zamin somon medihad. Sipas dar ruze, ki, miqdori on hazor sol ast, cunon ki mesumored, ʙa sui U ʙolo meraved
32|6|Ust, ki donoi nihonu oskor ast. Piruzmandu mehruʙon ast
32|7|On ki har ciro ofarid, ʙa nekutarin vach ofarid va xilqati ofaridani insonro az gil oƣoz kard
32|8|Sipas nasli uro az usorai (sirai) oʙe ʙeqadr padid ovard
32|9|On goh, a'zoi u rost kard va az ruhi xud dar on ʙidamid. Va ʙarojaton gusu casmho va dilho ofarid. Ci andak sukr megued
32|10|Va guftand: «Ojo vaqte ki dar zamin nopadid savem, ofarinisi tozae xohem joft?» Ore, onho ʙa didor ʙo Parvardigorason imon nadorand
32|11|Bigu: «Faristai marg, ki muvakkal (gumosta) ʙar sumost, sumoro memironad. Sipas ʙa sui Parvardigoraton ʙozgardonida mesaved»
32|12|Turo iʙrat ast, on goh ki gunahkoronro dar nazdi Parvardigorason sarafkanda ʙini. Gujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, didem va sunidem. Aknun moro ʙozgardon to kore soista kunem, ki inak ʙa jaqin rasidaem»
32|13|Agar mexostem, hidojati har kasro ʙa u ato mekardem, vale va'dai Man, ki cahannamro az haman cinnijonu odamijon pur mekunam, haq ast
32|14|Ba cazoi on, ki didori cunin ruzero faromus karda ʙuded, aknun ʙicased. Mo niz sumoro az jod ʙurdaem. Ba sazoi korhoe, ki mekardaed, azoʙi covidro ʙicased
32|15|Tanho kasone ʙa ojoti Mo imon ovardaand, ki cun ojoti Moro ʙisnavand, ʙa sacda ʙijaftand va Parvardigorasonro ʙa poki ʙisitojand va sarkasi nakunand (Sacda)
32|16|Az ʙistari xoʙ pahlu tihi (ʙedorxoʙi) mekunand, Parvardigorasonro ʙo ʙimu umed iltico mekunand va az on ci ʙa onho dodaem, sadaqa mekunand
32|17|Va hec kas az on mukofote az xusivu xursandi xaʙar nadorad, ki ʙa muzdi korhoi kardaas, ʙarojas pinhon karda sudaast
32|18|Ojo on kas, ki imon ovarda, mopandi kasset, ki fisq mevarzad? Na, ʙaroʙar nestand
32|19|Ammo onon, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙa cazoi neki amalhoe, ki makardaand, manzilgohe dar ʙoƣhoi ʙihist xohand joft
32|20|Va ammo fosiqon, manzilgohason otas ast. Har goh ki ʙixohand az on ʙerun ojand, ʙori digar onhoro ʙa daruni otas ʙozgardonand va ʙigujandason: «Bicased azoʙi otasero, ki duruƣas mepindosted!»
32|21|Va azoʙi dunjoro pes az on azoʙi ʙuzurgtar ʙa onho ʙicasonem, sojad, ki ʙozgardand
32|22|Kist sitamkortar az on kase, ki uro ʙa ojoti Parvardigoras pand dihand, vale ruj gardonad? Mo az gunahkoron intiqom megirem
32|23|Haqiqatan ʙa Muso kitoʙ dodem. Az didori u dar suʙha maʙos. Va onro rohnamoi ʙani-Isroil qaror dodem
32|24|Az mijoni on qavm pesvojone padid ovardem, ki cun saʙr pesa kardand va ʙa ojoti Mo jaqin dostand, ʙa farmoii Mo mardumro hidojat mekardand
32|25|Alʙatta Parvardigori tu dar ruzi qijomat dar on ci ixtilof mekardand, mijonason dovari xohad kard
32|26|Ojo on hama mardumero, ki pes az onho halok kardem va aknun inho dar xonahojason roh meravand, saʙaʙi hidojatason nasud? Dar in iʙrathost, caro namesunavand
32|27|Ojo nameʙinand, ki oʙro ʙa zamini xusku ʙegijoh ravona mesozem, to kistzorho ʙirujonem va corpojon va xudason az on ʙixurand? Caro nameʙinand
32|28|Megujand: «Agar rost megued, piruzi ci vaqt xohad ʙud?»
32|29|Bigu: «Dar ruzi piruzi, imon ovardani kofiron foidaason nadihad va muhlatason nadihad»
32|30|Pas az onho ruj gardon va muntazir ʙos, ki onho niz dar intizorand
33|1|Ej pajomʙar, az Xudo ʙitars va ʙa kofironu munofiqon ito'at makun. Zero Xudo donovu hakim ast
33|2|Ba har ci az Parvardigorat ʙa tu vahj mesavad, ito'at kun. Zero Xudo ʙa on ci mekuned, ogoh ast
33|3|Va ʙar Xudo tavakkal kun, zero Xudo korsoziro ʙasanda ast
33|4|Xudo dar daruni hec mjarde du qalʙ nanihodaast. Va zanonatonro, ki modari xud mexoned, modaraton qaror nadod va farzandxondagonatonro farzandonaton nasoxt. Inho cizhoest, ki ʙa zaʙoi megued va suxani haq az oni Xudost va Ust, ki roh menamojad
33|5|Pisarxondagonro ʙa nomi padarason ʙixoned, ki dar nazdi Xudo muvofiqi insof ast. Agar padarasonro namesinosed, ʙarodaroni dini va mavolii (dustoni) sumo ʙosand. Agar pes az in xatoe kardaed, ʙoke nest, magar on, ki ʙa qasdi dil kuned. Va Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
33|6|Pajomʙar ʙa mu'minon az xudason sazovortar ast va zanonas modaroni mu'minon hastand va dar kitoʙi Xudo xesovandoni nasaʙi az mu'minonu muhociron ʙa jakdigar sazovortarand, ƣajri on, ki ʙixohed ʙa jake az dustoni xud neki kuned. Va in hukm dar kitoʙi Xudo maktuʙ ast
33|7|Va on hangom, ki az pajomʙaron pajmon giriftem va az tuvu az Nuh va Iʙrohim va Muso va Iso ʙinni Marjam va az hamai onho pajmone saxt giriftem
33|8|to rostgujonro az sidqason ʙipursad va ʙaroi kofiron azoʙe dardovar muhajjo kardaast
33|9|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, az ne'mate, ki Xudo ʙa sumo dodaast, jod kuned, ʙa on hangom, ki laskarho ʙar sari sumo hucum kardand va Mo ʙodro va laskarhoero, ki namedided, ʙar sarason firistodem va Xudo ʙa on ci mekarded, ʙino ʙud
33|10|On goh ki az samti ʙolo va az samti poin ʙar sumo toxtand, casmho xira sud va dilho ʙa gulu rasida ʙud va ʙa Xudo gumonhoi gunogun meʙurded
33|11|Dar on co mu'minon imtihon karda sudand va saxt takon xurdand
33|12|Zero munofiqon va onhoe, ki dar dilhojason ʙemorist meguftand: «Xudo va pajomʙaras ƣajri fireʙ ʙa mo va'dae nadodaand!»
33|13|Va guruhe az onho guftand: «Ej mardumi Jasriʙ, in co coi mondanaton nest. Bozgarded». Va guruhe az onho az pajomʙar ruxsat talaʙidand. Meguftand: «Xonahoi moro hifzkunandae nest». Xonahojason ʙehifzkunanda naʙud, mexostand ʙigurezand
33|14|Va agar az atrof xonahojasonro muhosira kunand va az onho ʙixoxand, ki kofir savand, kofir xohand sud va andake ham muhlat ravo naxohand guzarond
33|15|Inho pes az in ʙo Xudo pajmon ʙasta ʙudand, ki dar cang ʙa dusman pust nakunand. Xudo az pajmoni xud ʙozxost xohad kard
33|16|Bigu: «Agar az marg jo kusta sudan ʙigureged, hargiz gurextan naf'aton nadihad. Va on goh az zindagi ƣajri andake ʙahramand naxohed sud»
33|17|Bigu: «Agar Xudo ʙarojaton qasdi ʙade dosta ʙosad jo ʙixohad ʙa sumo rahmate arzoni dorad, kist, ki sumoro az irodai U nigah dorad?» Onho ƣajri Xudo ʙaroi xud dustu madadkore naxohand joft
33|18|Xudo medonad ci kasone az sumo mardumro az cang ʙozmedorand. 'Va niz mesinosad kasonoro, ki ʙa ʙarodaroni xud megujand: «Ba nazdi mo ʙijoed». Va ƣajri andake ʙa cang nameojand
33|19|Har cizero az sumo dareƣ medorand va cui tarsu xafv ojad, ʙini, ki ʙa tu menigarand va casmonason (az tarsi i marg) davr mezanad misli kase, ki az marg ʙehus tuda ʙosad, Va cun vahsat az mijon ʙirevad, az hirsi ƣanimatho ʙo zaʙoni tezi xud ʙiranconadaton. Inho imon najovardaand. Va Xudo amalhojasonro noʙud kardaast va in kor ʙar Xudo oson ʙudaast
33|20|Mepindorand, ki laskari kofiron naraftaast. Va agar on laskarho ʙozmeomadand, orzu mekardand, ki kos dar mijoni a'roʙi ʙodijanisin meʙudand va hamesa az axʙori sumo mepursidand. Agar ham dar mijoni sumo meʙudand, ƣajri andake cang namekardand
33|21|Baroi sumo agar ʙa Xudo va ruzi qijomat umed medored va Xudoro farovon jod mekuned, dar simoi rasululloh muqtadoi (pesvoi) pisandidaest, meʙined
33|22|Va cun mu'minon on guruhhoro didand, guftand: In hamon cizest, ki Xudo va pajomʙaras ʙa mo va'da dodaand va Xudovu pajomʙaras rost guftaand». Va imon va taslimason zoid sud
33|23|Az mu'minon mardone hastand, ki ʙa pajmone, ki ʙa Xudo ʙasta ʙudand, vafo kardand. Ba'ze ʙar sari pajmoni xud con ʙoxtand va ʙa'ze casm ʙa rohand va hec pajmoni xud digargun nakardaand
33|24|To Xudo rostgujonro ʙa saʙaʙi rostii guftorason muzd dihad va munofiqonro agar xohad azoʙ kunad jo tavʙai onhoro ʙipazirad, ki Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
33|25|Xudo kofironi xasmgiriftaro ʙozpas gardonid. Inho ʙa hec ƣanimate dast najoftand. Va dar majdoni cang mu'minonro Xudo kifoja ast. Zero Xudo purtavonu ƣoliʙ ast
33|26|Az ahli kitoʙ on guruhro, ki ʙa joriason ʙarxosta ʙudand, az qal'ahojason furud ovard va dar dilhojason ʙim afkand. Guruhero kusted va guruhero ʙa asorat girifted
33|27|Xudo zaminu xonaho va molhojason va zaminhoero, ki ʙar onho poj nanihodaed, ʙa sumo meros guzost. Va Xudo ʙar har kore tavonost
33|28|Ej pajomʙar, ʙa zanonat ʙigu: «Agar xohoni zindagii dunjo va zinathoi on hasted, ʙijoed, to sumoro ʙahramand sozam va ʙa tarzi neku rahojaton kunam
33|29|va agar xohoni Xudovu pajomʙari U va saroi oxirat hasted, Xudo ʙa nekukoronaton podose (mukofote) ʙuzurg xohad dod
33|30|Ej zanoni pajomʙar, har kas az sumo kori zisti sazovori uquʙat, kunad. Xudo azoʙi uro du ʙaroʙar mekunad. Va in ʙar Xudo oson ast
33|31|Va har kas az sumo, ki ʙa farmonʙardorii Xudo va pajomʙaras davom dihad va kore soista kunad, du ʙor ʙa u mukofot dihem. Va ʙaroi u rizqe nek omoda kardaem
33|32|Ej zanoni pajomʙaar, sumo monandi digar zanon. nested, agar az Xudo' ʙitarsed. Pas ʙa narmi suxan; nagued, to on marde, ki dar qalʙi u maraze hast, ʙa tama' aftad, Va suxani pisandida ʙigued
33|33|Va dar xonahoi xud ʙimoned. Va cunon ki dar zamoni pesini cohilijat mekardand, zinathoi xudro oskor nakuned. Va namoz ʙiguzored va zakot ʙidihed va ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras ito'at kuned. Ej ahli ʙajt. Xudo mexohad, palidiro az sumo dur kunad va sumoro pok dorad
33|34|On ciro dar xonahojaton az ojoti Xudo va hikmat tilovat mesavad,. jod kuned, ki Xudo ʙorikʙinu ogoh ast!»
33|35|Xudo ʙaroi, mardoni musalmon va zanoni musalmon va mardoni mu'minu zanoni mu'min va mardoni ahli to'atu zanoni ahli to'at va mardoni rostguvu zanoni rostguj va mardoni ʙosaʙru zanoni ʙosaʙr va mardoni xudotarsu zanoni xudotars va mardoni sadaqadihandavu zanoni sadaqadihanda va mardoni ruzadoru zanoni ruzador va mardone, ki sarmgohi xud hifz mekunand va zanone, ki sarmgohi xud hifz mekunand va mardone, ki Xudoro farovon. jod mekunand va zanone ki Xudoro farovon jod mekunand, ʙaxsois va muzde ʙuzurg omoda kardaast
33|36|Hec mardi mu'minu zani mu'minro narasad ki cun Xudovu pajomʙaras dar kore hukme kardand, onhoro dar on korason ixtijor ʙosad. Har ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras nofarmoni kunad, saxt dar gumrohi aftodaast
33|37|Va tu ʙa on mard, ki Xudo. ne'matas doda ʙud va tu niz ne'matas doda ʙudi, gufti: «Zanatro ʙaroi xud nigah dor va az Xudoj ʙitars». Dar hole ki dar dili xud on ciro Xudo oskor soxt, maxfi dosta ʙudi va az mardum metarsidi, hol on ki Xudo az har kasi digar sazovorgar ʙud, ki az u ʙitarsi. Pas cun Zajd az u hocati xud ʙarorad, ʙa hamsarii tuas darovardem, to mu'minonro dar zanosui ʙo zanoni farzandxondagoni xud, agar hocati xud az u ʙarovarda ʙosand, man'e naʙosad. Va hukmi Xudovand sudanist
33|38|Bar pajomʙar dar ancom dodani on ci Xudo ʙa u muqarrar kardaast, harace (gunohe) nest, hamcunon ki Xudo ʙaroi pajomʙaroni pesin niz cunin sunnate nihoda ʙud va farmoni Xudo farmonest ʙe hec zijodavu nuqson
33|39|Kasone, ki pajomhoi Xudoro merasonand va az U metarsand va az hec kas ƣajri U nametarsand, Xudo ʙaroi hisoʙ kardani amalhojason kofist
33|40|Muhammad padari hec jak az mardoni sumo nest. U rasuli Xudo va hotami (oxirini) pajomʙaron ast. Va Xudo ʙa har cize donost
33|41|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, Xudoro farovon jod kuned
33|42|Va har ʙomdodu saʙongoh tasʙehas gued
33|43|Ust, ki Xud va faristagonas ʙar sumo duruƣ mefiristand, to sumoro az toriki ʙa ravsani ʙarad, zero Xudovand ʙa mu'minon mehruʙon ast
33|44|Ruze, ki ʙo U didor kunand, durudason in ast: «Salom!» Va Xudo ʙarojason mukofote neku omoda kardaast
33|45|Ej pajomʙar, Mo turo firistodem to sohidu muƶdadihanda va ʙimdihanda ʙosi
33|46|Va mardumro ʙa farmoni Xudo ʙa sui U da'vat kuni va caroƣe toʙnok ʙosi
33|47|Va mu'minonro xusxaʙar deh, ki az sui Xudo ʙarojason fazilate ʙuzurg omadaast
33|48|Ba kofironu munofiqon ito'at makun va ozorasonro tark kun va ʙar Xudo tavakkal kun, ki Xudo korsoziro kifoja ast
33|49|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, cun zanoni mu'minro nikoh karded, va pes az on ki ʙo onho nazdiki kuned, taloqason gufted, sumoro ʙar onho iddae nest, ki ʙipojand. Pas ononro hadja dihed va ʙa nekutarin tarz rahojason kuned
33|50|Ej pajomʙar, Mo zanonero, ki mahrasonro dodai va ononro, ki ʙa unvoni ƣanimathoi cangi, ki Xudo ʙa tu ato namudaast, molik sudai va duxtari amuho va duxtari ammaho va duxtari doiho (taƣoho) va duxtari xolahoi turo, ki ʙo tu muhocirat kardaand, ʙar tu halol kardem va niz zani mu'minero, ki xudro ʙa pajomʙar ʙaxsida ʙosad har goh pajomʙar ʙixohad uro ʙa zani girad. In hukmi maxsusi tust na digar muʹminon. Mo medonem dar ʙoram zanonason va kanizonason ci hukme kardaem, to ʙaroi tu muskilie pes najojad. Va Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
33|51|Az zanoni xud har kiro xohi ʙa navʙat muaxxar (aqiʙ) dor va har kiro xohi, ʙo xud nigah dor. Va agar az onho, ki dur dostai, jakero ʙitalaʙi, ʙar tu gunohe nest. Dar in intixoʙu ixtijor ʙojad, ki sodmon ʙosand va ƣamgin nasavagd va az on ci hamagijasonro ato menamoi, ʙojad, ki xusnud gardand va Xudo medonad, ki dar dilhoi sumo cist. Va Xudost, ki donovu ʙurdʙor ast
33|52|Ba'd az in zanon hec zane ʙar tu halol nest va niz zane ʙa coi ojaho ixtijor kardan, harcand turo az zeʙoii u xus ojad, ƣajri on ci ʙa ƣanimat ʙa dasti tu aftad. Va Xudo nazoratkunandai har cizest
33|53|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙa xonahoi pajomʙar doxil nasaved, magar sumoro ʙa xurdani ta'ome faro xonand, ʙe on ki muntazir ʙinsined, to ta'om hozir savad. Agar sumoro da'vat kunand, doxil saved, va cun ta'om xurded, parokanda garded. Na on ki ʙaroi sargarmi suxan oƣoz kuned. Alʙatta in korho pajomʙarro ozor medihad va u az sumo sarm medorad, Vale Xudo az guftani haq sarm namedorad. Va agar az zanoni pajomʙar cize xosted, az pusti parda ʙixohed. In kor ham ʙaroi dilhoi sumo va ham ʙaroi dilhoi onho pokdorandatar ast. Sumoro naʙojad, ki pajomʙari Xudoro ʙijozored va na on ki zanhojasro ʙa'd az vaj hargiz ʙa zani gired. In korho dar nazdi Xudo gunohe ʙuzurg ast
33|54|Agar cizero oskor kuned jo maxfi dored, dar har hol Xudo ʙa har cize ogoh ast
33|55|Zanonro gunohe nest, agar dar nazdi padaru pisar va ʙarodaru ʙarodarzoda va xoharzodavu zanoni hamdin va jo kanizoni xud ʙehicoʙ ʙosand. Va ʙojad az Xudo ʙitarsed, ki Xudo ʙar har cize nozir ast
33|56|Xudo va faristagonas ʙar pajomʙar salavot mefiristand. Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙar u salavot firisted va salom kuned, salome neku
33|57|Har oina (alʙatta) kasonero, ki Xudo va pajomʙarasro ozor medihand, Xudo dar dunjo va oxirat la'nat karda va ʙarojason azoʙe xorkunanda muhajjo kardaast
33|58|Va kasone, ki mardoni mu'minu zanoni mu'minro ʙe hec gunoxe, ki karda ʙosand, meozorand, tuhmatu gunohi oskorero ʙar dus mekasand
33|59|Ej pajomʙar, ʙa zanonu duxtaroni xud va zanoni mu'minon ʙigu, ki codari xudro ʙar xud pusand. In munosiʙtar ast, to sinoxta savand va mavridi ozor voqe' nagardand. Va Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
33|60|Agar munofiqon va kasone, ki dar dilhojason marazest va onho, ki dar Madina soje'a (ovoza) meparokanand, az kori xud ʙoznaistand, turo ʙar onho ƣoliʙ megardonem, to az on pas cuz andake ʙo tu dar sahr hamsoja naʙosand
33|61|Inho la'nat sudagoizpd. Har co jofta savand, ʙojad dastgir gardand va ʙa saxti kusta savand
33|62|In sunnati Xudovandist, ki dar mijoni pesinijon niz ʙud va dar sunnatn Xudo taƣjire naxohi joft
33|63|Mardum turo az qijomat mepursand, ʙigu: «Ilmi on nazdi Xudost». Va tu ci medoni, sojad qijomat nazdik ʙosad
33|64|Xudo kofironro la'nat karda va ʙarojason otase suzon muhajjo kardaast
33|65|ki dar on covidonaand va hec dustu jovare naxohand joft
33|66|Ruze, ki surathojasonro (rujhojasonro) dar otas ʙigardonand, megujand: «Ej kos, Xudoro ito'at karda ʙudem va rasulro ito'at karda ʙudem!»
33|67|Va guftand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, ʙa sarvaronu ʙuzurgoni xud ito'at kardem va onon moro gumroh kardand
33|68|Ej Parvardigori mo, azoʙasonro ducandon kun va ʙa la'nati ʙuzurge giriftorason soz!»
33|69|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, maʙosed monandi on kason, ki Musoro ozurda kardand va Xudojas az on ajʙe, ki gufta ʙudand, pokas soxt va nazdi Xudo oʙrumand ʙud
33|70|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, az Xudo ʙitarsed va suxani durust ʙigued
33|71|Xudo korhoi sumoro ʙa saloh ovarad va gunohonatonro ʙiʙaxsojad. Va har ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras ito'at kunad, ʙa komjoʙii (zafari) ʙuzurge dast joftaast
33|72|Mo in amonatro ʙar osmonhovu zamin va kuhho arza dostem, az tahammuli on ruj gardondand va az on tarsidand. Inson on amonatro ʙar dus girift, kk u sitamkoru nodon ʙud
33|73|to Xudo mardoni munofiqu zanoni munofiq va mardoni musriku zanoni musrikro azoʙ kunad va tavʙai mardoni mu'minu zanoni mu'minro ʙipazirad, ki Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
34|1|Sitois az oni Xudoest, ki har ci dar osmonhovu har ci dar zamin ast. az oni Ust. Va dar on cahon niz sitois az oni Ust va U hakimu ogoh ast
34|2|Har ciro, ki dar zamin furu savad va har ciro, ki az zamin ʙerun ojad va har ciro, ki az osmon furud ojad va har ciro, ki ʙar osmon ʙolo ravad, medonad. Va U mehruʙonu ʙaxsojanda ast
34|3|Kofiron guftand,: «Moro qijomat naxohad omad!» Bigu: «Ore, ʙa Parvardigoram — on donoi ƣajʙ savgand, ki sumoro xohad omad. Ba qadri zarrae jo kucaktar az on va jo ʙuzurgtar az on dar osmonhovu zamin az Xudo pinhon nest va hama dar kitoʙi muʙin omadaast
34|4|to kasonero, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, muzd dihad. Baroi onhost ʙaxsois va rizqi neku
34|5|Va onon, ki ʙa ojoti Mo daraftodand, to Moro ʙa notavoni orand, ʙarojason aeoʙest saxt dardovar
34|6|Onon, ki az donis ʙahramandi joftaand, medonand, ki on ci az coniʙi Parvardigorat ʙar tu nozil suda ast, haq ast va ʙa rohi Xudoi ƣoliʙu sutudani roh menamojad
34|7|Kofiron guftand: «Ojo mexohed ʙa marde dalolataton kunem, ki sumoro megujad: «On goh ki porapora saved va rez-rez, az lav ofarida xohed sud
34|8|Ojo ʙar Xudo duruƣ meʙandad, jo devona ast?» Na, onon, ki ʙa oxirat imon nadorand, dar azoʙand va saxt az roh durand
34|9|Ojo ʙa pasi ruj jo pusti sari xud az osmonhovu zamin namenigarand? Agar ʙixohem, onhoro dar zamin furu meʙarem, jo qit'ae az osmonro ʙar sarason meafkanem. Va dar in ʙaroi har ʙandae, ki ʙa Xudo ʙozmegardad, iʙratest
34|10|Dovudro az sui xud fazilate dodem, ki ej kuhho va ej parrandagon, ʙo u hamovoz saved. Va ohanro ʙarojas narm kardem
34|11|ki zirehhoi ʙaland ʙisoz va dar ʙoftani zireh andozahoro nigah dor. Va korhoi soista kuned, ki Man ʙa korhojaton ʙinoam
34|12|Va ʙodro romi Sulajmon kardem. Bomdodon jakmoha roh meraft va saʙongoh jakmoha roh. Ba casmai misro ʙarojas cori soxtem va guruhe az devho ʙa farmoni Parvardigoras ʙarojas kor mekardand va har ki az onon sar az farmoni Mo mepecid, ʙa u azoʙi otasi suzonro mecasonidem
34|13|Baroi vaj har ci mexost, az ʙinohoi ʙaland va suratho va kosahoe cun havz va deghoi mahkami ʙarcoj, mesoxtand. Ej xonadoni Dovud, ʙaroi sukr guzori kore kuned va andake az ʙandagoni Man sukrguzorand
34|14|Cun hukmi margro ʙar u rondem, hasarae az hasaroti zamin mardumro ʙar margas ogoh kard, asojasro (jak sol) xoid. Cun furu aftod, degho darjoftand, ki agar ilmi ƣajʙ medonistand, dar on azoʙi xorkunanda namemondand
34|15|Mardumi Saʙoro dar maskanhojason iʙrate ʙud: du ʙuston dostand, jake az coniʙi rost va jake az coniʙi cap. Az on ci Parvardigoraton ʙa sumo ruzi dodaast, ʙixured va sukri U ʙa coj ovared. Sahre xusu pokiza va Parvardigore ʙaxsojanda
34|16|Ruj gardondand. Mo niz seli vajrongarro ʙar onho firistodem va du ʙustonasonro ʙa du ʙuston ʙadal kardem ʙo mevae talx va suragaz va andake sidr (nomi daraxt)
34|17|Onhoro, ki nosipos ʙudand, incunin cazo dodem, Ojo Mo ƣajri nosiposonro cazo mekunem
34|18|Mijoni onon va qarijahoe (dehahoe), ki ʙarakat doda ʙudem, dehahoe oʙodon va ʙar sari roh padid ovardem. Va manzilhoi ʙaroʙar mu'ajjan kardem. «Dar on rohho ʙoamnu osoistagi saʙhovu ruzho safar kuned!»
34|19|Bar xestan sitam kardand va guftand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, manzilgohhoi moro az ham, dur gardon!» Mo niz afsonai ruzgorason gardonidem va saxt parokandaason soxtem va dar in iʙrathost ʙaroi saʙrkunandagoni sukrguzor
34|20|Sajton gumoni xudro dar ʙorai onho durust joft. Va ƣajri guruhe az mu'minon digaron az u pajravi kardand
34|21|Va sajtonro ʙar onon ƣoliʙijate naʙud, magar on ki mexostem ma'lum dorem, ki ci kasone ʙa qijomat imon dorand va ci kasone az on dar sak hastand. Va Parvardigori tu nigahʙoni har cizest
34|22|Bigu: «Bixoned kasonero, ki cuz Xudoi jakto xudo mepindored!» Moliki zarrae dar osmonhovu zamin nestand va dar ofarinisi on du sirkate nadostaand va Xudoro az mijoni onho jorigare naʙudaast
34|23|Safo'at nazdi Xudo naf' nakunad, magar dar ʙorai kase, ki U xud icozat dihad, Va cun ʙim az dilhojason ʙiravad, gujand: «Parvardigoraton ci guft?» Gujand: «Suxani haq guft. Va U ʙalandmartaʙavu ʙuzurg ast!»
34|24|Bigu: «Az osmonhovu zamin ci kase, ʙa sumo ruzi medihad?» Bigu: «Xudoi jakto». Inak movu sumo jo dar tariqi hidojat hastem jo dar gumrohii oskor». (Sacda)
34|25|Bigu: Agar mo gunohe kunem, sumoro pursis namekunand va agar sumo gunohe karded moro pursis naxohand kard»
34|26|Bigu: «Parvardigori mo movu sumoro gird meovarad, sipas mijoni mo ʙa haq dovari mekunad. Zero Ust hukmkunandavu dono!»
34|27|Bigu: «Onhoero, ki sariki Xudo pindosted, ʙa man nison ʙidihed! Hargiz, Ust Xudoi ƣoliʙu hakim!»
34|28|Turo ʙa pajomʙari firistodem, ʙar hamai mardum; muƶdadihandavu ʙimdihanda. Vale ʙestari mardum namedonand
34|29|Va megujand: «Agar rost megued, in va'da (qijomat) ci vaqt faro rasad?»
34|30|Bigu: «On ruz, ki me'ode (va'dagohi) sumost, na so'ate ta'xir kuned va na so'ate pes afted»
34|31|Va kofiron guftand: «Mo na ʙa in Qur'on imon meovarem va na ʙa kitoʙhoi pes az on!» Agar ʙuʙini on ruz, ki sitamkoronro ʙa pesgohi Parvardigorason nigoh dorand, har kas gunohi xud ʙa gardani digare andozad. Zaʙunsudagon pajravon ʙa qudratmandon (sardoron) gujand: «Agar sumo naʙuded, mo imon ovarda ʙudem»
34|32|Qudratmandon ʙa zaʙunsudagon gujand: «Ojo az on pas, ki sumoro ʙa rohi hidojat da'vat kardand, mo sumoro ʙozdostem? Na, sumo xud gunahkor ʙuded!»
34|33|Zaʙunsudagon ʙa qudratmandon gujand: «Na, sumo saʙu ruz hila mekarded, on goh ki moro farmon medoded, ki ʙa Xudoi jakto kofir savem va ʙaroi U sarikone qaror dihem!» Va cun azoʙro ʙuʙinand, dar dil pusajmoni kunand. Va Mo gulhoro ʙar gardani kofiron ʙiguzorem. Ojo na cunin ast, ki dar ʙaroʙari amalhojason cazo doda mesavand
34|34|Mo kadom ʙimdihandae ʙa dehae firistodem, tavongaroni ʙo ajsu isratas guftand: «Mo ʙa on ci sumoro ʙa on firistodaand, imon nameovarem»
34|35|Va guftand: «Molhovu avlodi mo az hama ʙestar ast va kase moro azoʙ nakunad»
34|36|Bigu: «Parvardigori man ast, ki ruzii har kasro, ki ʙixohad, farovon mekunad va ʙar har ki ʙixohad, tang megirad. Vale ʙestari mardum namedonand»
34|37|Molhovu avlodaton cize nest, ki sumoro ʙa Mo nazdik sozad. Ƣajri onhoe, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, ki muzdi inho ʙa saʙaʙi amalhojason du ʙaroʙar ast va emin dar ƣurfahoi ʙihist hastand
34|38|Onhoe, ki ʙa ojoti Mo metozand va mepindorand, ki az Mo megurezand, tu'mai azoʙand
34|39|Bigu: «Parvardigori man ast, ki ruzii har ki az ʙandagonasro, ki ʙixohad, farovon mekunad jo uro ʙa tangi meafkanad». Va agar cize sadaqa kuned, ivazasro xohad dod va U ʙehtarini ruzidihandagon ast
34|40|Ruze, ki hamaro cam' ovarad, on goh maloikaro gujad: «Ojo inho ʙudand, ki sumoro meparastidand?»
34|41|Megujand; «Tu poki. Tui valii mo, na onho. Inho cinhoro meparastidand va ʙestarin ʙa onho imon dostand»
34|42|On ruz ʙa jakdigar hec sudu zijone natavoned rasond. Va ʙa sitamkoron guem: «Bicased azoʙi otasro, ki duruƣas mepindosted!»
34|43|Cun ojoti ravsani Mo ʙar onon xonda sud, guftand: «In mardest, ki mexohad sumoro az on ci padaronaton meparastidand, ʙozdorad». Va guftand: «In ƣajri duruƣe ʙa ham ʙofta cizi digare nest!» Va kasone, ki ʙa Xudo kofir suda ʙudand, cun suxani haq ʙar onho nozil sud, guftand: «In cize ƣajri codue oskor nest!»
34|44|Pes az in kitoʙe, ki onro ʙixonand, ʙa onho nadodaem va pes az tu ʙimdihandae ʙar onho nafiristodaem
34|45|Va kasone, ki pes az onho ʙudand, pajomʙaronro takziʙ (duruƣ) kardaand va inho xud ʙa dahjaki on ci ʙa onho doda ʙudem, narasidaand va ʙo in hol pajomʙaroni Maro duruƣ ʙarovardand. Pas uquʙati Man ci saxt ʙud
34|46|Bigu: «Sumoro ʙa jak ciz pand mediham: du-du va jak-jak ʙaroi (iʙodati) Xudo ʙarxezed. Sipas ʙijandesed, to ʙidoned, ki dar jori sumo devonagie nest. Ust, ki sumoro az omadani azoʙe saxt metarsonad!»
34|47|Bigu: «Har muzde, ki az sumo talaʙidaam, az oni xudaton ʙod. Muzdi man tanho ʙar uhdai Xudost. Ust, ki ʙar har kore nozir ast!»
34|48|Bigu: «Parvardigori man ilhomʙaxsi suxani haq ast. Donoi ƣajʙhost!»
34|49|Bigu: «Haq (Qur'on) omad va ʙotil zohir namesavad va ʙoznamegardad!»
34|50|Bigu: «Agar man gumroh savam, zijonas ʙar man ast va agar ʙa rohi hidojat ravam, ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki Parvardigori man ʙa man vahj mekunad. U sunavovu nazdik ast!»
34|51|Agar ʙuʙini, on goh ki saxt ʙitarsand va xalosiason naʙosad va az makone nazdik giriftorason sozand
34|52|Gujand: «Inak ʙa rasul imon ovardem». Ammo az on coi dur ci son ʙa on dast joʙand
34|53|Pes az in ʙa U kofir suda ʙudand va ʙa gumoni xud ʙa U tuhmat mezadand
34|54|Mijoni onho va on orzu, ki dorand, cudoi aftod. Hamcunon ki ʙo digaron, ki cunin meandesidand va saxt dar suʙha ʙudand, niz cunin sud
35|1|Sitois az oni Xudovand ast, ofarinandai osmonhovu zamin, on ki faristagonro rasulon gardonid. Faristagone, ki ʙolhoe dorand, du-du va sese va cahor-cahor. Dar ofarinis har ci ʙixohad, meafzojad, zero Xudo ʙar har kore tavonost
35|2|Rahmate, ki Xudo ʙar mardum ʙikusojad, kase natavonad, ki ʙozas dorad. Va cun cizero dareƣ dorad, kas natavonad, ƣajri U, ki onro firistad. Va Ust ƣoliʙu hakim
35|3|Ej mardum, ne'matero, ki Xudo ʙar sumo ato kardaast, jod kuned. Ojo cuz Xudo ofarinandai digare hajot, ki sumoro az osmonu zamin ruzi dihad? Xudoe ƣajri U nest, pas ci guna az haq ʙerohaton mekunand
35|4|Agar turo takziʙ (duruƣ) kardaand, pajomʙaronero ham, ki pes az tu ʙudaand, takziʙ kardaand va hamai korho ʙa Xudo ʙozgardonda savad
35|5|Ej mardum va'dai Xudo haq ast. Zindagii dunjo sumoro nafireʙad va on sajtoni fireʙanda ʙa Xudo maƣruraton nagardonad
35|6|Sajton dusmani sumost. Uro dusman gired. U farmonʙaroni xudro da'vat kunad to hama az duzaxijon ʙosand
35|7|Va kofironro azoʙest saxt va ʙaroi kasone, ki imon ovardaand va kordon soista kardaand, ʙaxsois va savoʙi ʙuzurgest
35|8|Ojo on ki kirdori ʙadas dar nazaras orosta suda, cunon ki nekujas pindost, monandi kasest, ki cunin nest? Pas Xudo har kiro xohad, gumroh mekunad va har kiro xohad, hidojat mekunad. Naʙojad, ki coni tu ʙa xotiri onho ducori anduh, savad. Zero Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekunand, ogoh ast
35|9|Xudost, ki ʙodhoro firistod to aʙrhoro ʙironand. Va Mo onhoro ʙa sarzaminhoi murda meronem va zamini murdaro ʙa on zinda mekunem. Zinda gastan dar ruzi qijomat niz cunin ast
35|10|Har ki xohoni izzat ast, ʙidonad, ki izzat hamagi az oni Xudost. Suxani xusu pok ʙa sui U ʙolo meravad va kirdori nek ast, ki onro ʙolo meʙarad. Va ʙaroi onon, ki az rui makr fasodkori mekunand, azoʙest saxt va makrason niz az mijon ʙiravad
35|11|Xudo sumoro az xok va sipas az nutfa ʙijofarid. On goh cufthoi jakdigaraton qaror dod. Hec zane homilador namesavad va namezojad magar ʙa ilmi U. Va umri har solxurdae ʙa darozo kasad va az umri kase kam gardad, alʙatta hama dar kitoʙe navista sudaast. Va in korho ʙar Xudo oson ast
35|12|In du darjo jakson nestand: jake oʙas sirinu guvorost va jake suru talx. Az har du gusti toza mexured va az onho cizhoe ʙaroi oroisi tani xud ʙerun mekased. Va meʙini kistihoro, ki oʙro mesikofand, to sumo az fazli Xudo ruzi talaʙed va sojad, ki sukrguzor ʙosed
35|13|Az saʙ kam mekunadu ʙa ruz meafzojad va az ruz kam mekunadu ʙa saʙ meafzojad va oftoʙu mohro rom kard. Har jak to zamone muajjan dar harakatand, In ast Xudo — Parvardigori sumo. Farmonravoi az oni Ust. Cizhoero, ki ƣajri U ʙa xudoi mexoned, moliki pusti mijoni donai xurmoe ham nestand
35|14|Va agar onhoro ʙixoned, sadojatonro namesunavand va agar ʙisnavand, posuxaton nagujand. Va dar ruzi qijomat sirk ovardanatonro inkor kunand va kas hamonandi Xudoi ogoh xaʙardorat nasozad
35|15|Ej mardum, hamai sumo ʙa Xudo muhtoced. Ust ʙeehtijocu loiqi sitois
35|16|Agar ʙixohad, sumoro az mijon meʙarad va mardume nav meovarad
35|17|Va in kor ʙar Xudo dusvor nest
35|18|Hec kas ʙori gunohi digarero ʙar dus nakasad. Va agar garonʙore kasero ʙa ʙardostani ʙori xud farjod kunad, harcand xesovandi u ʙosad, az ʙardostani on ruj gardonad. Tu faqat kasonero metarsoni, ki az Parvardigorason nodida ʙimnokand va namoz meguzorand. Va har ki pok savad, ʙaroi xud pok suda. Va ʙozgasti hama ʙa sui Xudost
35|19|Noʙinovu ʙino ʙaroʙar nestand
35|20|va torikivu ravsani
35|21|va na sojavu harorati oftoʙ
35|22|Va zindagonu murdagon ʙaroʙar nestand. Xudo har kiro xohad, mesunavonad. Va tu nametavoni suxani xudro ʙa murdagone, ki dar gur xuftaand, ʙisnavoni
35|23|Tu cuz ʙimdihandae nesti
35|24|Mo turo ʙa haq ʙa pajƣamʙari firistodem, to muƶda dihi va ʙim dihi va hec millate nest, ki ʙa mijonason ʙimdihandae naomada ʙosad
35|25|Agar turo duruƣ ʙarorand, kasone ham, ki pes az inho ʙudaand, pajomʙaronasonro, ki ʙo mu'cizot va ʙo navistaho va kitoʙi ravsanoiʙaxs ʙa mijonason omada ʙudand, duruƣ ʙarovardaand
35|26|Sipas onhoero, ki kofir sudand, ʙa halokat giriftam. Uquʙati Man ci guna ʙud
35|27|Ojo nadidai, ki Xudo az osmon ʙoron firistod va ʙo on mevahoi gunogun rujonidem? Va az kuhho rohho padid ovardem: safed va surx va rangorang va ʙaƣojat sijoh
35|28|Hamcunin az mardum va cunʙandagon va cahorpojoni gunogun. Alʙatta az mijoni ʙandaoni Xudo tanho donismandon az U metarsand. Va Xudo ƣoliʙu ʙaxsojanda ast
35|29|Onon, ki kitoʙi Xudoro mexonand va namoz meguzorand va az on ci ʙa onho dodaem, pinhonivu oskoro sadaqa mekunand, umedvor ʙa ticorate hastand, ki hargiz zijon namekunad
35|30|Zero Xudo mukofotasonro ʙa tamomi medihad va az fazli xud cize ʙar on meafzojad. Zero ʙaxsojandavu sukrpazir ast
35|31|Har ci az on kitoʙ ʙa tu vahj kardaem, hak, ast, ki kitoʙhoi pes az xudro tasdiq mekunad va Xudo ʙar ʙandagonas ogohu ʙinost
35|32|Sipas kitoʙro ʙa kasone az ʙandagonamon, ki ʙarguzida ʙudem, ʙa meros dodem. Ba'ze ʙar xud sitam kardand va ʙa'ze rohi mijonaro ʙarguzidand va ʙa'ze ʙa farmoni Xudo dar korhoi nek pesi giriftand. Va in ast ʙaxsoise ʙuzurg
35|33|Ba ʙihisthoe, ki cojgohi covidonai onhost, doxil mesavand. Dar on co ʙa dastʙandahoi zaru marvoridason meorojand va dar on co comahoson az harir (sohi) ast
35|34|Va megujand: «Sukr Xudoro, ki anduh az mo dur kard, zero Parvardngori mo ʙaxsojandavu sukrpazir ast
35|35|On Xudoe, ki moro az fazli xud ʙa in cahoni covidon darovard, ki dar on co na rance ʙa mo merasad va na xastagi»
35|36|Va kofironro otasi cahannam ast, na ʙimironandason va na az azoʙason kam gardad. Kofironro cunin cazo medihem
35|37|Va az daruni otas farjod zanand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, moro ʙerun or, to korhoe soista kunem, ƣajr az on ci mekardem». Ojo on qadar sumoro umr nadoda ʙudem, ki pandgirandagon pand girand? Va sumoro ʙimdihanda omad. Pas ʙicased, ki gunohkoronro joridihandae nest
35|38|Xudo donoi nihoni osmonhovu zamin ast va U ʙa on ci dar dilhost, ogoh ast
35|39|Ust, ki sumoro dar rui zamin conisini pesinijon kard, pas har kas, ki kofiri kunad, kufras ʙar zijoni ust va kufri kofiron cuz ʙar dusmanii Parvardigorason ʙo onho najafzojad. Niz kufri kofiron faqat ʙa zijonason afzojad
35|40|Bigu: «On sarikonero, ki ʙa coi Xudoi jakto mexonded, dided? Ba man ʙinamoed, ki az in zamin ci cizro ofaridaand? Jo dar ofarinisi osmon ci sarikie dostaand? Ojo ʙar onho kitoʙe firistodaem, ki onro huccati xud sozand? Na, sitamkoron ʙa jakdigar ƣajri fireʙ va'dae namedihand»
35|41|Xudo osmonhovu zaminro nigah medorad, to az coj ʙeco nasavand va agar az coj ʙeco savand, hec jak az sumo, ƣajri U, nametavonad onhoro nigah dorad. Alʙatta Xudo ʙurdʙoru ʙaxsojanda ast
35|42|Ba Xudo qasamhoi saxt xurdand, ki agar ʙimdihandae ʙijojad, ʙehtar az har ummati digar hidojat joʙand. Vale cun ʙimdihandae omad, ʙadʙinijason afzud
35|43|ʙa sarkasi dar zamin va najranghoi ʙad. Va in najranghoi ʙad faqat najrangʙozonro dar ʙar girad. Ojo cuz sunnate, ki ʙar guzastagon raftaast, muntaziri cizi digare hastand? Dar sunnati Xudo hec taʙdile namejoʙi va dar sunnati Xudo hec taƣjire namejoʙi
35|44|Ojo dar zamin namegardand, to ʙuʙinand, ki oqiʙati mardume, ki pes az onho ʙudaand va nerue ʙestar dostaand, ʙa kuco kasid? Hec ciz dar osmonhovu zamin nest, ki Xudoro notavon sozad. Zero U donovu tavonost
35|45|Va agar Xudo ʙixohad, mardumro ʙa saʙaʙi korhoe, ki kardaand, ʙozxost kunad, ʙar rui zamin hec cunʙandae ʙoqi naguzorad, vale onhoro to zamone mu'ajjan muhlat medihad va cun muddatason tamom sud, ʙa amalhoi ʙandagoni xud ogoh ast

36|7|Azoʙi Xudo ʙaroi ʙestarinason vociʙ sudaast va imon nameovarand
36|8|Va mo ʙar gardanhojason to manahho tavqho (zancirho) nihodem, cunon ki sarhojason ʙa ʙolost va poin ovarda natavonand

36|12|Mo murdagonro zinda mekunem. Va har korero, ki pes az in kardaand va har asarero, ki padid ovardaand, menavisem va har cizro dar kitoʙi muʙin sumor kardaem
36|13|Dostoni mardumi on deharo ʙar onho ʙijovar, on goh ki rasulon ʙa on co omadand
36|14|Naxust du tanro ʙa nazdason firistodem va duruƣ ʙarovardand, pas ʙo savvumi quvvatason dodem va guftand: «Mo ʙa sui sumo firistoda sudaem»

36|17|Va ʙar uhdai mo ƣajri pajom rasonidani oskoro hec cizi digar nest»

36|82|Cun ʙixohad cizero ʙijofarinad, farmonas in ast, ki megujad: «Mavcud sav!» Pas mavcud mesavad

37|6|Mo osmoni dunjoro ʙa zinati sitoragon ʙijorostem

37|8|To suxani sokinoni olami ʙoloro nasnavand va az har suj ronda savand
37|9|To dur gardand va ʙaroi onhost azoʙe doim
37|10|Ƣajri on sajton, ki nogahon cize ʙiraʙojad va nogahon su'lai suzandae dunʙolas kunad
37|11|Pas, az kofiron ʙipurs, ki ojo ofarinisi onho dusvortar ast jo on ci Mo ofaridaem. Mo onhoro az gile caspanda ofaridaem
37|12|Tu dar taaccuʙ sudi va onho masxara mekunand
37|13|Va cun ʙa onho pand doda savad, pand, namepazirand
37|14|Va cun ojae ʙuʙinand, az jakdigar mexohand, to onro ʙa masxara girand
37|15|Va megujand: «In cize ƣajri codui oskor nest
37|16|ojo vaqte ki mo murdem va xoku ustuxon sudem, moro zinda mekunand
37|17|jo padaroni moro?»
37|18|Bigu: «Bale, va sumo xoru ʙecora mesaved!»
37|19|Va onon xud xohand did, ki ʙa jak farmon hamaro zinda mekunand
37|20|Megujand: «Voj ʙar mo, in hamon ruzi cazost!»
37|21|In hamon ruzi dovari ast, ki duruƣas mepindosted
37|22|Ononro, ki zulm mekardand va hamrohonasonro va onhoero, ki ʙa coi Xudoi jakto meparastidand, cam' ovared
37|23|Hamaro ʙa rohi cahannam roh nison dihed
37|24|Va nigah doredason, ʙojad ʙozxost savand
37|25|«Caro jakdigarro jori namekuned?»
37|26|Na, imruz hama taslimsavandagonand
37|27|Va on goh ruj ʙa jakdigar kunand va ʙipursand
37|28|Gujand: «Sumo ʙuded, ki az dari nekxohi ʙar mo medaromaded»
37|29|Gujand: «Na, sumo imon najovarda ʙuded
37|30|Moro ʙar sumo hec ƣoliʙijate naʙud. Sumo xud mardumone nofarmon ʙuded
37|31|Guftai Parvardigoramon ʙar mo vocid sud. Aknun ʙojad ʙicasem
37|32|Mo sumoro gumroh kardem va xud niz gumroh ʙudem»
37|33|Dar on ruz hama dar azoʙ sarikand
37|34|Mo ʙo gunahkoron cunin mekunem
37|35|Cun ʙa onon gufta mesud, ki ƣajri Xudoi jakto xudoe nest, takaʙʙur mekardand
37|36|va meguftand: «Ojo ʙa xotiri soiri devonae xudojonamonro tark guem?»
37|37|Na, on pajomʙar haqro ovard va pajomʙaroni pesinro tasdiq kard
37|38|Sumo azoʙi dardovarro xohed casid
37|39|Dar ʙaroʙari amalhojaton cazo xohed did
37|40|Ƣajri ʙandagoni muxlisi Xudo
37|41|ki onhoro rizqe mu'ajjan ast
37|42|az mevaho, va giromi dostagonand
37|43|dar ʙihisthoi purne'mat
37|44|ʙar taxthoe, ki ruʙarui hamand
37|45|Va come az casmai xusguvor mijonason ʙa gardis darojad
37|46|safed astu nusandagonasro lazzatʙaxs

37|48|Zanone faroxcasm, ki tanho ʙa savharoni xud nazar dorand, hamdami onhojand
37|49|Hamonandi tuxmi murƣhoe dur az dastras
37|50|Ru ʙa jakdigar kunand va guftugu kunand
37|51|Jake az onho gujad: «Maro hamnisine ʙud
37|52|ki meguft: «Ojo tu az onho hasti, ki tasdiq mekunand
37|53|Ojo on goh, ki murdemu xoku ustuxon sudem, cazojamon medihand?»
37|54|Gujand: «Metavoned az ʙolo ʙinigared?»
37|55|Az ʙolo ʙinigarad va uro dar mijoni otasi duzax ʙinad
37|56|Gujadas: «Ba Xudo savgand, nazdik ʙud, ki maro ʙa halokat afkani
37|57|Va agar mavhiʙati (ʙaxsisi) Parvardigoram naʙud, man niz az hozirsudagoni azoʙ meʙudam
37|58|Ojo moro marge nest
37|59|cuz on margi naxustin? Va digar azoʙamon namekunand?»
37|60|Har oina (alʙatta) in ast komjoʙii ʙuzurg
37|61|Amalkunandagon ʙojad ʙaroi cunin mukofote amal kunand
37|62|Ojo xurisro in ʙehtar jo daraxti zaqqum

37|85|Ba padaras va qavmas guft: «Ci meparasted

37|100|Ej Parvardigori man, maro farzande soleh ato kun!»
37|101|Pas uro ʙa pisare ʙurdʙor xusxaʙar dodem

37|103|Cun har du taslim sudand va uro ʙa pesoni xoʙonid

37|149|Az onho ʙipurs; «Ojo duxtaron az oni Parvardigori tu ʙosand va pisaron az oni onho?»
37|150|Ojo vaqte ki Mo maloikaro zan meofaridem, onho medidand

37|155|Ojo nameandesed

37|157|Agar rost megued, kitoʙatonro ʙijovared
37|158|Va mijoni Xudovu cinnijon xesovandi qoil sudand va cinnijon medonand, ki hozirkardasudagonand. (dar azoʙ)
37|159|Az on sifat, ki meovardand, Xudo pok ast
37|160|ƣajri ʙandagoni muxlisi Xudo
37|161|Sumo va ʙutone, ki meparasted

37|163|magar on kasro, ki rohii cahannam ʙosad
37|164|«Va har kas az mo coe mu'ajjan dorad
37|165|Alʙatta mo safzadagonem
37|166|Va alʙatta mo tasʙehgujandagonem»
37|167|Agarci meguftand
37|168|«Agar az pesinijon nazdi mo kitoʙe monda ʙud
37|169|mo az ʙandagoni muxlisi Xudo meʙudem»
37|170|Onho ʙa on kitoʙ kofir sudand va ʙa zudi, ki xohand fahmid

37|172|ki alʙatta onon jori mesavand
37|173|Va laskari Mo xud ƣoliʙand
37|174|Pas to muddate az onho ruj ʙigardon
37|175|Oqiʙatasonro ʙuʙin, onho niz xohand did
37|176|Ojo azoʙi Moro ʙa sitoʙ metalaʙand
37|177|Cun azoʙ ʙa majdonason farojad, in ʙimdodasudagon ci ʙomdodi ʙade xohand dost
37|178|Az onho to cande ruj ʙigardon
37|179|Pas oqiʙatasonro ʙuʙin, onho niz xohand did
37|180|Munazzah (pokast) ast Parvardigori tu — on Parvardigori piruzmand — az har ci ʙa vasfi U megujand
37|181|Va salom ʙar pajomʙaron
37|182|Va hamd az oni Parvardigori cahonijon ast
38|1|Sod. Savgand ʙa Qur'oni sarifi sohiʙi pand
38|2|ki kofiron hamcunon dar sarkasivu ziddijat
38|3|Ci ʙisjor mardumero, ki pes az onho ʙa halokat rasonidem. Onon farjod meʙarovardand, vale gurezgohe naʙud
38|4|Dar taaccuʙ sudand az in ki ʙimdihandae az mijoni xudason ʙarxost. Va kofiron guftand: «In codugare duruƣgust
38|5|Ojo hamai xudojonro jak xudo gardonida ast? Va in cize aciʙ ast!»
38|6|Buzurgonason ʙa roh aftodandu guftand: «Biraved va ʙar parastisi xudojoni xud pojdori kuned, ki in ast cize, ki az sumo xosta suda
38|7|Mo dar in oxirin din cunin suxane nasunidaem va in ƣajri duruƣ hec nest
38|8|Ojo az mijoki hamai mo vahj ʙar u nozil sudaast?» Balki onho az vahji Man dar suʙhaand va hanuz azoʙi Maro nacasidaand
38|9|jo on ki xazinahoi rahmati Parvardigori ƣoliʙi ʙaxsandaat dar nazdi onhost
38|10|Jo farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin va har ci mijoni on dust, az oni onhost? Pas ʙo nardʙonhoe xudro ʙa osmon kasand
38|11|On co laskarest nociz az cand guruhi sikastxurdai (ʙar ziddi pajramʙaron) cam'suda
38|12|Pes az onho qavmi Nuh va Od va Fir'avn, ki mardumro ʙa cahormex mekasid, pajomʙaronro duruƣ meʙarovardand
38|13|Va niz qavmi Samud va qavmi Lut va mardumi Ajka az on camo'atho ʙudand
38|14|Az inho kase naʙud, ki pajomʙaronro duruƣ naʙarovard va uquʙati Man vociʙ omad
38|15|Inho niz ʙonge saxtro intizori dorand, cunon ki onro digar tavaqqufe (ʙozistodane) naʙosad
38|16|Va guftand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, nomai a'moli moro pes az faro rasidani ruzi hisoʙ ʙa dasti mo ʙideh!»
38|17|Bar harci megujand, saʙr kun. Va az ʙandai Mo Dovudi qudratmand, ki hamesa ʙa dargohi Mo tavʙa mekard, jod ovar
38|18|Mo kuhhoro rom kardem va kuhho har somgohu ʙomdodon ʙo u tasʙeh mekardand
38|19|Va parrandagon ʙar u cam' meomadand. Hama farmonʙari u ʙudand
38|20|Farmonravoijasro ustuvori ʙaxsidem va uro hikmatu fasohat dar suxan ato kardem
38|21|Ojo xaʙari on xusumatkunandagonro sunidai, on goh ki az devori qasr ʙa mascid daromadand
38|22|Bar Dovud doxil sudand. Dovud az onho tarsid. Guftand: «Matars, mo du da'vogar hastem, ki jake ʙar digare sitam kardaast. Mijoni mo ʙa haq dovari kun va poj az adolat ʙerun maneh va moro ʙa roxi rost hidojat kun
38|23|In ʙarodari man ast. Uro navadu nuh mes (gusfand) ast va maro jak mes. Megujad: «Onro ham ʙa man ʙideh» va dar da'vo ʙar man ƣalaʙa joftaast»
38|24|Dovud guft: «U, ki mesi turo az tu mexohad to ʙa meshoi xud ʙijafzojad, ʙa tu sitam mekunad. Va ʙisjore az sarikon ƣajri kasone, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand — va inho niz andak hastand — ʙar jakdigar sitam mekunand». Va Dovud donist, ki uro ozmudem. Pas az Parvardigoras ʙaxsois xost va ʙa ruqu' daraftodu tavʙa kard. (Sacda)
38|25|Mo in xatojasro ʙaxsidem. Uro ʙa dargohi Mo taqarruʙ (nazdiki) ast va ʙozgaste neku
38|26|Ej Dovud, Mo turo xalifai rui zamin gardonidem. Dar mijoni mardum ʙa haq dovari kun va az pai havoi nafs marav, ki turo az rohi Xudo ʙeroh sozad. Onon, ki az rohi Xudo kacrav savand, ʙa on saʙaʙ, ki ruzi hisoʙro az jod ʙurdaand, ʙa azoʙe saxt giriftor mesavand
38|27|Mo in osmonu zamin va on ciro, ki mijoni onhost, ʙa ʙotil najofaridaem. In gumoni kasonest, ki kofir sudand. Pas voj ʙar kofiron az otas
38|28|Ojo kasonero, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, monandi fasokunandagon dar zamin qaror xohem dod? Jo parhezgoronro cun gunohkoron
38|29|Kitoʙe muʙorak ast, ki onro ʙar tu nozil kardaem, to dar ojathojas ʙijandesand va xiradmandon az on pand girand
38|30|Sulajmonro ʙa Dovud ato kardem. Ci ʙandae nekue ʙud va ruj ʙa Xudo dost
38|31|On goh ki ʙa hangomi asr asponi tezravro, ki istoda ʙudand, ʙa u nison dodand
38|32|guft: «Man dustii in asponro ʙar jodi Parvardigoram ʙigzidam, to oftoʙ dar pardai ƣuruʙ pusida sud (ja'ne namozi asr qazo sud)
38|33|on asponro nazdi man ʙozgardoned». Pas ʙa ʙuridani soqho va gardanason oƣoz kard
38|34|Mo Sulajmonro ozmudem va ʙar taxti u casadero afkandem va u ruj ʙa Xudo ovard
38|35|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro ʙiʙaxs va maro mulke ato kun, ki pas az man kase sazovori on naʙosad, ki tu ʙaxsojandai»
38|36|Pas ʙodro romi u kardem, ki ʙa narmi har co, ki mexost, ʙa farmoni u meraft
38|37|Va devonro, ki ham ʙinokor ʙudandu ham ƣavvos (sinovar)
38|38|Va guruhe digarro, ki hama ʙasta dar zanciri u ʙudand
38|39|In atoi ʙehisoʙi Most, xohi onro ʙideh va xohi nigah dor
38|40|Urost nazdi Mo taqarruʙu (nazdik sudanu) ʙozgaste neku
38|41|Va az ʙandai Mo Ajjuʙ jod kun, on goh ki Parvardigorasro nido kard, ki maro sajton ʙa rancu azoʙ afkanda ast
38|42|«Pojatro ʙar zamin ʙikuʙ: in oʙest ʙaroi sustusuj va sard ʙaroi osomidan»
38|43|Va ʙa u xonavodaas va hamcandi on az digar joronro ato kardem va in xud rahmate az Mo ʙud va ʙaroi xiradmandon andarze (pande)
38|44|«Dastae az cuʙhoi ʙorik ʙa dast gir va ʙo on (zanatro) ʙizan va savgandi xudro masikan». Uro ʙandae soʙir joftem, U, ki hamesa ruj ʙa dargohi Mo dost, ci neku ʙandae ʙud
38|45|Bandagoni Mo Iʙrohimu Ishoq va Ja'quʙ on mardoni qudratmandu ʙo ilmro jod kun
38|46|Ononro xislati pokdili ʙaxsidem, to jodi qijomat kunand
38|47|Onho dar nazdi Mo intixoʙsudagonu nekonand
38|48|Va Ismoil va Aljasa' va Zulkiflro jod kun, ki hama az nekonand
38|49|In Qur'on pandest va parhezgoronro ʙozgaste nekust
38|50|ʙixisthoi covidon, ki dari on ʙa rujason kusoda ast
38|51|Dar on co takja zadaand va har guna mevavu nusidani, ki ʙixohand, metalaʙand
38|52|Zanone hamsol az on guna, ki ƣajri sui xud ʙa kase nazar nadorand, nazdi onhojand
38|53|In ast on cizhoe, ki ʙaroi ruzi hisoʙ ʙa sumo va'da dodaand
38|54|In rizqi Most, ki pojon najoftanist
38|55|cunin ast. Va sarkasonro ʙadtarin ʙozgastxost
38|56|Ba cahannam meravand, ki ʙad cojgohest
38|57|Bojad oʙi cusonu cirk va xunoʙai duzaxijonro ʙinusand
38|58|Va azoʙhoi digar az har nav'
38|59|In guruh ʙo sumo (ej gumrohkunandaho) ʙa otas medarojand. Xusomadason maʙod, ki ʙa otas meaftand
38|60|Gujand: «Na, xusomad sumoro naʙod. Sumo in azoʙro pesopes ʙaroi mo firistoda ʙuded, ci ʙad cojgohest!»
38|61|Gujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, har kas, ki in azoʙro pesopes ʙaroi mo omoda kardaast, azoʙasro dar otas ducandon zijoda kun!»
38|62|Va gujand: «Caro mardonero, ki az asror (ʙadkoron). mesumurdem, aknun nameʙinem
38|63|Ononro ʙa masxara megiriftem. Ojo az nazarho dur mondaand?»
38|64|In ʙahsu cidoli ahli cahannam ʙo jakdigar cizest, ki ʙa haqiqat voqe' savad
38|65|Bigu: «Faqat hamin ast, ki man ʙimdihandae hastam va hec xudoe ƣajri Xudoi jaktoi kahhor nest
38|66|On piruzmandu ʙaxsojanda, Parvardigori osmonhovu zamin va har ci mijoni onhost»
38|67|Bigu: «In xaʙare ʙuzurg ast
38|68|ki sumo az on ruj megardoned
38|69|Hangome ki ʙo jakdigar cidol (ʙahs) mekardand, man xaʙare az sokinoni olami ʙolo nadostam
38|70|Tanho az on ruj ʙa man vahj mesavad, ki ʙimdihandae ravsangar hastam»
38|71|Parvardigorat ʙa faristagon guft: «Man ʙasarero az gil meofarinam
38|72|Cun tamomas kardam va dar on az ruhi xud damidam, hama sacdaas kuned!»
38|73|Hama faristagon sacda kardand
38|74|Ƣajri Iʙlis, ki sarkasi kardu az kofiron sud
38|75|Guft: «Ej Iʙlis, ci ciz turo az sacda kardan dar ʙaroʙari on ci Man ʙo du dasti xud ofaridaam, man' kard? Ojo ʙuzurgi namudi jo maqome arcmand dosti?»
38|76|Guft: «Man az u ʙehtaram. Maro az otas ofaridai va uro az gil»
38|77|Guft: «Az in co ʙerun sav, ki tu rondasudai
38|78|Va to ruzi qijomat la'nati Man ʙar tust»
38|79|Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro to ruze, ki az nav zinda savand, muhlat deh»
38|80|Guft: «Tu az muhlatjoftagoni
38|81|to on ruzi mu'ajjani ma'lum»

38|83|ƣajri onho, ki az ʙandagoni muxlisi Tu ʙosand»
38|84|Guft: «Haq ast va on ci megujam, rost ast
38|85|ki cahannamro az tuvu az hamai pajravonat pur kunam»
38|86|Bigu: «Man az sumo muzde nametalaʙam va nestam az onon, ki ʙa duruƣ cize ʙar xud meʙofand»
38|87|Va ii ƣajri pande ʙaroi mardumi cahon nest
38|88|Va tu ʙa'd az in az xaʙari on ogox xohi sud
39|1|Nozil sudani in kitoʙ az coniʙi Xudoi piruzmandi hakim ast
39|2|Mo in kitoʙro ʙa rosti ʙar tu nozil kardem (firistodem). Pas Xudoro ʙiparast va dini xud ʙaroi U xolis gardon
39|3|Ogoh ʙos, ki dini xolis az oni Xudost va onon, ki ƣajri U digarero ʙa xudoi giriftand, guftand: «Inonro az on ru meparastem, to vasilai nazdikii mo ʙa Xudoi jakto savand. Va Xudo dar on ci ixtilof mekunand, mijonason hukm xohad kard. Xudo onro, ki duruƣguvu nosipos ʙosad, hidojat namekunad
39|4|Agar Xudo mexost, ki ʙaroi xud farzande ʙargirad, az mijoni maxluqoti xud har ciro, ki mexost, intixoʙ mekard. Pok ast. Ust Xudoi jaktoi qahhor
39|5|Osmonhovu zaminro ʙa haq ʙijofarid. Saʙro ʙar ruz doxil mekunad va ruzro ʙar saʙ. Va oftoʙu mohro rom gardonid va har jak to zamone mu'ajjan dar harakatand. Ogoh ʙos, ki Ust piruzmandu omurzanda
39|6|Sumoro az jak tan ʙijofarid. Va az on jak tan zanasro ofarid. Va ʙarojaton az corpojon hast cuft ʙijofarid. Sumoro dar sikami modaraton dar cand marhala dar daruni torikihoi segona ofarinis ʙaxsid. In ast Xudoi jakto, Parvardigori sumo. Farmonravoi az oni Ust. Xudoe cuz U nest. Pas ci guna rujgardonaton mesozand
39|7|Agar nosiposi kuned, Xudo az sumo ʙehocat ast va nosiposiro (nosukriro) ʙaroi ʙandagonas namepisandad. Mepisandad, ki siposguzor ʙosed. Va hec kas ʙori gunohi digarero ʙar dus namekasad. Bozgasti hamai sumo nazdi Parvardigoraton ast. U sumoro az korhoe, ki mekardaed, ogoh mekunad, U ʙa on ci dar dilho meguzarad, ogoh ast
39|8|Cun ʙa odami dardu rance ʙirasad, ʙa Parvardigoras ruj meovarad va Uro mexonad. On goh cun ʙa u ne'mate ʙaxsad, hamai on du'ohoro, ki pes az in karda ʙud, az jod meʙarad va ʙaroi Xudo hamtojone qaror medihad, to mardumro az tariqi U gumroh kunand. Bigu: «Andake az kufrat ʙahramand sav, ki tu az duzaxijon xohi ʙud!»
39|9|Ojo on kas, ki dar hamai so'ati saʙ ʙa iʙodat pardoxta jo dar sucud ast jo dar qijom va az oxirat ʙimnok ast va ʙa rahmati Parvardigoras umedvor ast, ʙo on ki cunin nest, jakson ast? Bigu: «Ojo onhoe, ki medonand ʙo onhoe, ki namedonand, ʙaroʙarand?» Tanho xiradmandon pand megirand
39|10|Bigu: «Ej ʙandagoni Man, ki imon ovardaed, az Parvardigoraton ʙitarsed. Baroi onon, ki dar hajoti incahoni neki kardaand, podosi (cazoi) nek ast. Va zamini Xudo pahnovar ast. Muzdi soʙiron ʙehisoʙu komil ado mesavad!»
39|11|Bigu: «Man amr sudaam, ki Xudoro ʙiparastam va ʙaroi U dar din ixlos kunam
39|12|Va maro farmudaand, ki naxustini musalmonon ʙosam»
39|13|Bigu: «Agar Parvardigoramro nofarmoni kunam, az azoʙi on ruzi ʙuzurg metarsam»
39|14|Bigu: «Xudoro meparastam va ʙaroi U dar dini xud ixlos mevarzam
39|15|Biparasted har cizi digarero cuz U». Bigu: «Zijonkunandagon kasone hastand, ki dar ruzi qijomat xud va xonadonasonro az dast ʙidihand. Baxus ʙosed, ki in zijone oskor ast
39|16|Boloi sarason taʙaqoti otas ast va dar zeri pojason taʙaqoti otas». In cizest, ki Xudo ʙandagoni xudro ʙo on metarsonad. Pas, ej ʙandagoni Man, az Man ʙitarsed
39|17|Va kasonero, ki az parastisi ʙuton parhez kardaand va ʙa Xudo ruj ovardaan. d, ʙasorat (xaʙari xus) ast. Pas ʙandagoni Maro ʙasorat deh
39|18|on kasone, ki ʙa suxan gus medihand va az ʙehtarini on pajravi mekunand, onhojand kasone, ki Xudo hidojatason karda va onho xiradmandonand
39|19|Ojo kasero, ki hukmi azoʙ ʙar u ʙarovarda suda, tu metavoni uro, ki dar otas ast, ʙirahoni
39|20|Ammo ʙaroi onon, ki az Xudo metarsand, ƣurfahoest (imorathoest) ʙar ʙoloi ham soxta, ki az zerason cujʙoron ravon ast. In va'dai Xudost va Xudo va'dai xud xilof naxohad kard
39|21|Ojo nadidai, ki Xudo az osmon ʙoron firistod va onro cun casmasorhoe dar zamin ravon gardonid, on goh ʙa on kistahoi rangorang ʙirujonid, sipas hama xusk mesavand va meʙini, ki zard sudaand, on goh xurdason mesozad? Alʙatta xiradmandonro dar on pandest
39|22|Ojo kase, ki Xudo dilasro ʙar rui islom kusod va u dar partavi nuri Parvardigoras coj dorad, hamonandi kasest, ki imon nadorad? Pas voj ʙar saxtdilone, ki jodi Xudo dar dilhojason roh nadorad, ki dar gumrohii oskor hastand
39|23|Xudo ʙehtarin suxanro nozil kardaast. Kitoʙe mutasoʙeh va duto-duto, ki az tilovati on kasonero, ki az Parvardigorason metarsand, az tars tan ʙilarzad. Sipas tanu conason ʙa jodi Xudo ʙijoromad. In rohi Xudost, ki har kiro ʙixohad, ʙa on rohnamoi mekunad va har kiro Xudo gumroh kunad, uro hec rohnamoe naxohad ʙud
39|24|Ojo on kas, ki dar ruzi qijomat ʙo cehrai xud azoʙi saxti qijomatro az xud ʙozmedorad, monandi kasest ki ʙihistist? Ba sitamkoron gufta mesavad: «Ba kajfari (cazoi) korhoe, ki mekardaed, azoʙro ʙicassed!»
39|25|Pesinijonason duruƣ ʙarovardand va azoʙ az coe, ki namedonistand, ʙar sarason rasid
39|26|Xudo dar in cahon rasvojason soxt, vale agar ʙidonand, azoʙi oxirat ʙuzurgtar ast
39|27|Mo dar ni Qur'on ʙaroi mardum har guna misole ovardem, sojad pand girand
39|28|Qur'one ʙa zaʙoni araʙi ʙe hec (nuqsonu) kaci. Sojad parhezgori kunand
39|29|Xudo masale mezanad: «Mardero, ki cand tan dar u sarikand va ʙar sari u ixtilof dorand. Va marde, ki tanho az oni jake ʙosad. Ojo in du ʙo ham ʙaroʙarand? Sukru sipos Xudoro. Na, ʙestarason namedonand
39|30|Tu memiri va onho niz memirand
39|31|Sipas hama dar ruzi qijomat nazdi Parvardigoraton ʙo jakdigar husumat xohed kard
39|32|Pas kist sitamkortar az on, ki ʙar Xudo duruƣ meʙandad va suxani rostero, ki ʙar u omadaast, duruƣ meʙarorad. Ojo kofironro dar cahannam cojgohe nest
39|33|Va kase, ki suxani rost ovard va tasdiqas kard, onon parhezgoronand
39|34|Barojason har ci ʙixohand, dar nazdi Parvardigorason muhajjost. In ast podosi (mukofoti) nekukoron
39|35|to Xudo ʙadtarin amalhoero, ki kardaand, az onon noʙud kunad va ʙa ʙehtar az on ci mekardaand, mukofotason dihad
39|36|Turo ʙa kasone, ki ƣajri Xudo hastand, metarsonand. Ojo Xudo ʙaroi nigahdorii ʙandaas kofi nest? Va har kasro, ki Xudo gumroh sozad, hec rohnamoe naxohad ʙud
39|37|Har kasro, ki Xudo rohnamoi kunad, gumrohkunandae nest. Ojo Xudo ƣoliʙu intiqomgiranda nest
39|38|Agar az onho ʙipursi: «Cj kase osmonhovu zaminro ofaridaast?» Xohand guft: «Xudoi jakto». Bigu: «Pas inhoero, ki ƣajri U meparasted, ci guna meʙined? Agar Xudoi jakto ʙixohad ʙa man rance ʙirasonad, ojo inho metavonand on rancro daf' kunand? Jo agar ʙixohad ʙa man rahmate ato kunad, metavonand on rahmatro az man ʙozdorand?» Bigu; «Xudo ʙaroi man ʙas ast. Tavakkalkunandagon ʙa U tavakkal mekunand»
39|39|Bigu: «Ej qavmi man, muvofiqi imkoni xud amal kuned. Man niz amal mekunam. Va ʙa zudi xohed donist, ki
39|40|ci kase ʙa azoʙe, ki uro xor mesozad, giriftor mesavad jo azoʙi covid ʙar sari u furud meojad»
39|41|Mo in kitoʙro ʙa haq ʙaroi hidojati mardum ʙar tu nozil kardem. Pas har kas, ki hidojat joft, ʙa naf'i xudi ust va har ki gumroh sud, ʙa zijoni xud ʙa gumrohi aftoda va tu vakili onho nesti
39|42|Xudo conhoro ʙa hangomi murdanason megirad va niz coni kasonero, ki dar xoʙi xud namurdaand. Conhoero, ki hukmi marg ʙar onho ronda suda, nigah medorad va digaronro to zamone, ki mu'ajjan ast, ʙozmefiristad. Dar in iʙrathost ʙaroi onhoe, ki meandesand
39|43|Ojo ƣajri Xudo safe'one ixtijor kardand? Bigu: «Xatto agar on safe'on qudrat ʙa kore nadosta ʙosand va cizero darnajoʙand?»
39|44|Bigu: «Safo'at sarosar az oni Xudost. Az oni Ust farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin. Sipas hama ʙa nazdi U ʙozgardonda mesaved»
39|45|Cun Xudoro ʙa jaktoi jod kunand, dilhoi on kason, ki ʙa qijomat imon najovardaand, nafrat girad va cun nomi digare ƣajri U ʙurda savad, sodmon savand
39|46|Bigu: «Bor Xudoe, Tui ofarinandai osmonhovu zamin, donoi nihonu oskor, Tu mijoni ʙandagonat dar har ci dar on ixtilof (ziddijat) mekardaand, dovari xohi kard»
39|47|Agar har ci dar rui zamin ast va hamonandi on az oni sitamkoron meʙud, dar ruzi qijomat xudro ʙo on az azoʙi dardnok ʙozmexaridand. Va az Xudo ʙarojason cizhoe oskor mesud, ki hargiz hisoʙasro namekardand

39|50|In suxane ʙud, ki pesinijonason ham meguftand, vale har ci cam' ovarda ʙudand, ʙa holason naf' nakard

39|52|Ojo hanuz nadonistaand, ki Xudost, ki ruzii har kasro, ki ʙixohad afzun mesozad jo tangruzias mekunad? Va dar in xud iʙrathost ʙaroi mardume ki imon meovarand
39|53|Bigu: «Ej ʙandagoni Man, ki ʙar zijoni xud isrof kardaed, az rahmati Xudo noumed nasaved. Zero Xudo hamai gunohonro meʙaxsojad. Ust ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon
39|54|Pes az on ki azoʙ faro rasad va kase ʙa joriaton ʙarnaxezad, ʙa Parvardigoraton ruj ored va ʙa U taslim saved
39|55|Va pes az on ki ʙanogoh va ʙexaʙar azoʙ ʙar sumo furud ojad, ʙa ʙehtarin cize, ki az coniʙi Parvardigoraton nozil sudaast, pajravi kuned
39|56|to kase nagujad: «Ej hasrato ʙar man, ki dar kori Xudo kutohi kardam va az masxarakunandagon ʙudam»
39|57|Jo ʙigujad: «Agar Xudo maro hidojat mekard, man az parhezgoron meʙudam»
39|58|Jo cun azoʙro ʙuʙinad, ʙigujad: «Agar ʙori digar ʙa dunjo ʙozmegardidam, az nekukoron mesudam!»
39|59|Ore, ojoti man ʙaroi tu nozil sud va tu gardankasi kardi va az kofiron ʙudi
39|60|Dar ruzi qijomat kasonero, ki ʙa Xudo duruƣ ʙastaand, meʙini, rujason sijoh sudaast. Ojo mutakaʙʙironro dar cahannam cojgohe nest
39|61|Xudo parhezgoronro ʙa saʙaʙi rohi nacotjoʙi, ki dar pes girifta ʙudand, merahonad. Ba onho hec ʙadi narasad va az anduh dur ʙosand
39|62|Xudost, ki ofaridgori har cizest va U nigahʙoni har cize
39|63|Kalidhoi osmonhovu zamin nazdi Ust va onho, ki ʙa ojoti Xudo kofir sudaand, zijondidagon hastand
39|64|Bigu: «Ej nodonon, ojo maro farmon medihed, ki ƣajr az Xudoro ʙiparastam?»
39|65|Ba tu va pajomʙaroni pes az tu vahj sudaast, ki agar sirk ʙijovared, amalhojaton nociz gardad va xud az zijonkunandagon xohed ʙud
39|66|Balki Xudoro ʙiparast va sukrguzori U ʙos
39|67|Xudoro nasinoxtand, oncunon ki loiqi sinoxti Ust. Va dar ruzi qijomat zamin jakco dar qaʙzai Ust va osmonho dar ham pecida dar jadi qudrati U. Pok ast va ʙartar az har ci sariki U mepindorand
39|68|Va dar sur damida savad. Pas har ki dar osmonho va har ki dar zamin ast, — ƣajri onho, ki U ʙixohad, — ʙehus mesavand. Va ʙori digar dar on damida savad, nogahon az coj ʙarmexezand va menigarand
39|69|Va zamin ʙa nuri Parvardigoras ravsan savad va nomahoi a'molro ʙinihand va pajomʙaronu guvohonro ʙijovarand va dar mijoni mardum ʙa haq dovari savad va ʙar kase sitame naravad
39|70|Cazoi har kas ʙaroʙari kirdoras ʙa tamomi ado savad, dar hole ki Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekardaand, ogohtar ast
39|71|Va kofironro guruh-guruh ʙa cahannam ʙironand.
