Vale ʙar kofiron azoʙ hatmi suda ʙud
39|72|Gufta savad: «Az darhoi cahannam doxil saved, hamesa dar on co xohed ʙud». Cojgohi sarkason ci ʙad cojgohest
39|73|Va ononro, ki az Parvardigorason tarsidaand, guruh-guruh ʙa ʙihist meʙarand. Cun ʙa ʙihist ʙirasand, darhojas kusoda savad. Va darʙonhoi ʙixist gujandason: «Salom ʙar sumo, ʙihistaton xus ʙod, ʙa darun ʙijoed, hamesa dar in co xohed ʙud!»
39|74|Megujand: «Sukr Xudoero, ki har va'da, ki ʙa mo dod, rost ʙud. On zaminro ʙa meros ʙa mo dod. Va aknun dar har coi ʙihist, ki ʙixohem, makon megirem». Amalkunandagonro ci muzdi nekuest
39|75|Va faristagonro meʙini, ki girdi arsi Xudo halqa zadaand va ʙa sitoisi Parvardigorason tasʙeh megujand. Mijoni onho niz ʙa haq dovari gardad va gufta savad, ki sitois az oni Xudoest, ki Parvardigori cahonijon ast
40|1|Ho, mim
40|2|Nozil sudani in kitoʙ az coniʙi Xudoi ƣoliʙi donost
40|3|ʙaxsojandai gunoh, pazirandai tavʙa, saxtuquʙat, sohiʙi ni'am (ne'matho). Hec xudoe ƣajri U nest. Bozgasti hama ʙa sui Ust
40|4|Faqat kofiron dar ojoti Xudo cidol mekunand. Pas omadu raftason dar sahrho turo nafireʙad
40|5|Pes az onho qavmi Nuh va guruhhoe, ki ʙa'd az eson ʙudand, pajomʙarasonro takziʙ kardand. Va har ummate ohangi on kard, ki pajomʙarasro dastgir kunad va ʙa ʙotil ʙa xusumat ʙarxost, to haqro az mijon ʙardorad. Ammo Man onhoro ʙa uquʙat furu giriftam va uquʙati Man ci saxt ʙud
40|6|Ba in tarz hukmi Parvardigori tu ʙar kofiron vociʙ sud, ki ahli cahannamand
40|7|Onon, ki arsro meʙardorand va onon, ki ʙar girdi on hastand, ʙa sitoisi Parvardigorason tasʙeh, megujand va ʙa U imon dorand va az U ʙaroi mu'minon ʙaxsois mexohand: «Ej Parvardngori mo, rahmatu ilmi Tu hama cizro faro giriftaast. Pas ononro, ki tavʙa kardaand va ʙa rohi tu omadaand, ʙiʙaxs va az azoʙi cahannam nigah dor
40|8|Va ej Parvardigori mo, ononro va har ki soleh ʙosad, az padaronu hamsaron va farzandonason ʙa ʙihisthoi covidoni, ki ʙa onho va'da dodai, doxil kun, ki Tu ƣoliʙu hakimi
40|9|Ononro az azoʙho hifz kud, ki har kiro dar on ruz az azoʙho hifz kuni, ʙar u rahmat ovardai va on komjoʙii ʙuzurgest!»
40|10|Kofironro nido medihand, ki dusmanii Xudo ʙo sumo az dusmanii sumo ʙo xudaton, on goh ki ʙa imonaton da'vat mekardand va rohi kufr pes megirifted, ʙuzurgtar ast
40|11|Megujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, moro du ʙor mirondi va, du ʙor zinda soxti va mo ʙa gunohonamon iqror kardaem. Ojo ʙerun sudanro rohe hast?»
40|12|In azoʙ ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki cun Xudoro ʙa jaktoi mexondand, sumo inkor mekarded va agar ʙaroi U sarike qaror medodand, sumo ʙa on sarik imon meovarded. Pas farmon farmoni Xudoi ʙalandmartaʙai ʙuzurg ast
40|13|Ust, on ki ojoti Xudro ʙa sumo nison dod va ʙarojaton az osmon ruzi firistod. Tanho kase pand megirad, ki ruj ʙa Xudo ovarad
40|14|Pas Xudoro ʙixoned, dar hole ki tanho ʙaroi U dar din ixlos mekuned, agarci kofironro noxus ojad
40|15|Balandkunandai martaʙaho, sohiʙi ars, ki ʙar har jak az ʙandagonas, ki ʙixohad, ʙa farmoni Xud vahj mefiristad, to mardumro az ruzi qijomat ʙitarsonad
40|16|On ruz, ki hamagon oskor savand, hec ciz az onho ʙar Xudo pusida namonad. Dar on ruz farmonravoi az oni kist? Az oni Xudoi jaktoi qahhor
40|17|On ruz har kasro monandi amalas cazo medihand va ʙa kas sitame nameravad. Va Xudo zud hisoʙkunanda ast
40|18|Az ruzi qijomat ʙitarsonason. On goh ki dilho laʙrez az anduh nazdiki hancarho (guluho) rasad. Sitamkoronro dar on ruz na xesovande ʙosad va na safe'e, (pustiʙon) ki suxanasro ʙisnavand
40|19|Nazarhoi duzdidaro va har ci dilho nihon dostaand, medonad
40|20|Xudo ʙa haq dovari mekunad. Vale kasone, ki ƣajri U ʙa xudoi mexonand, hec dovari natavonand, zero Xudo mesunavad va meʙinad
40|21|Ojo dar zamin sajr namekunand, to ʙingarand, ki oqiʙati pesinijonason ci guna ʙudaast? Tavonoii onho va jodgorihoe, ki dar rui zamin padid ovarda ʙudand, az inho ʙes ʙud. Va Xudo onhoro ʙa cazoi kufrason furu girift va az qahri Xudovandason nigahdorandae naʙud
40|22|In ʙa on saʙaʙ ʙud, ki pajomʙaronason ʙo dalelhoi ravsan nazdason omadand, vale inkor kardand va Xudo ham ononro furu girift. Va Xudo nerumand ast va ʙa saxti uquʙat mekunad
40|23|Mo Musoro ʙo ojoti Xud va huccate oskor firistodem
40|24|ʙa sui Fir'avnu Homon va Qorun. Va guftand, ki u codugare duruƣgust
40|25|Cun dini haqro az coniʙi Mo ʙar onho arza dost, guftand: «Pisaroni kasonero, ki ʙa U imon ovardaand, ʙikused va zanonasonro zinda ʙiguzored!» Va hilasozii kofiron dar tariqi ʙarʙodi ʙosad
40|26|Fir'avn guft: «Biguzored, Musoro ʙikusam va u Xudoi xudro ʙa jori talaʙad, Metarsam dinatonro digargun kunad jo dar in sarzamin fasode ʙarxezonad
40|27|Muso guft: «Man ʙa Parvardigori xud va Parvardigori sumo az har xudpisande, ki ʙa ruzi xisoʙ ʙovar nadorad, panoh meʙaram!»
40|28|Va marde mu'min az xonadoni Fir'avn, ki imonasro pinhon dosta ʙud, guft: «Ojo mardero, ki megujad, ki Parvardigori man Xudoi jaktost va ʙo dalelhoi ravsan az coniʙi Parvardigoraton omadaast, mekused? Agar duruƣ megujad, gunohi duruƣas ʙar gardani xudi ust va agar rost megujad, ʙa'ze az va'dahoe, ki dodaast, ʙa sumo xohad rasid, Alʙatta Xudo hec isrofkori duruƣguero hidojat namekunad
40|29|Ej qavmi man, imruz farmonravoi az oni sumost. Bar in sarzamin ƣalaʙa dored. Vale agar azoʙi Xudo ʙar sari mo ojad, ci kase jorijamon xohad kard?» Fir'avn guft: «Sumoro ƣajri on ci xud maslihat dodaam, rohe nison nadiham va ʙa ƣajri rohi savoʙ rohnamoi nakunam»
40|30|On ki imon ovarda ʙud, guft: «Ej qavmi man, ʙar sumo az on ci ʙar sari on qavmhoi digar omadaast, ʙimnokam (metarsam)
40|31|Hamonandi qavmi Nuh va Od va Samud va kasone, ki az on pas omadand. Hol on ki Xudo ʙaroi ʙandagonas xostori zulm nest
40|32|Ej qavmi man, az on ruz, ki jakdigarro ʙa farjod ʙixoned, ʙar sumo ʙimnokam
40|33|On ruz, ki hamagi pust karda ʙozmegarded va hec kas sumoro az azoʙi Xudo nigoh namedorad. Va har kas, ki Xudo gumrohas kunad, hec rohnamoe nadorad
40|34|Jusuf pes az in ʙo daloili ravsan ʙar sumo maʙ'us (firistoda) sud va sumo az on ci ovarda ʙud, hamcunon dar sak meʙuded. Cun Jusuf ʙimurd, gufted: «Xudo pas az u digar pajomʙare naxohad firistod!» Xudo tacovuzkori sakovarandaro in guna gumroh mesozad
40|35|Kasone, ki ʙe hec hucate, ki dar dast dosta ʙosand, dar ojoti Xudo cidol mekunand. Kori onon nazdi Xudovu mu'minon saxt nopisand ast. Xudo ʙar dili har mutakaʙʙiri (xudro az digaron ʙolotar donandai) caʙʙore incunin mudr menihad
40|36|Fir'avn guft: «Ej Homon, ʙaroi man qal'ai ʙalande ʙisoz, sojad ʙa on darho dast joʙam
40|37|darhoi osmonho. Va Xudoi Musoro ʙuʙinam, zero pindoram, ki duruƣ megujad». Ba in son kirdori zisti Fir'avn dar nazaras orosta sud va u az roh ʙozmond va coracuii u ƣajri zijon hec naʙud
40|38|On marde, ki imon ovarda ʙud, guft: «Ej qavmi man, az pai man ʙijoed, to ʙa rohi savoʙ hidojataton kunam
40|39|Ej qavmi man, in zindagii dunjo ʙearzisu ta'ajjusest (xusguzaroniest). Va oxirat saroi ʙaqost (ʙoqi)
40|40|Har kas kori ʙade ʙikunad, faqat monandi amalas cazo joʙad. Va har kas az mardu zan, ki mu'min ʙosad va amali solehe ʙa coj orad, ʙa ʙihist doxil savad va ʙehisoʙ ruzias dihand
40|41|Ej qavmi man, cist, ki man sumoro ʙa nacot mexonam va sumo maro ʙa otas da'vat mekuned
40|42|Maro da'vat mekuned, ki ʙa Xudo kofir savam va cizero, ki namesinosam, sariki U qaror diham, hol on ki man sumoro ʙa Xudoi ƣoliʙi ʙaxsojanda da'vat mekunam
40|43|Besak on ci sumo maro ʙa on da'vat mekuned, tavonoi onas nest, ki dar dunjovu oxirat kasero ʙa sui xud xonad, hol on ki ʙozgasti mo ʙa sui Xudoi jaktost va tacovuzkoron dar cahannam ʙosand
40|44|Ba zudi on ciro, ki aknun megujam, ʙa jod xohed ovard. Va man kori xud ʙa Xudo havola kardam, zero U ʙandagonasro meʙinad!»
40|45|Xudo uro az oseʙi makre, ki ʙarojas andesida ʙudand, nigoh dost va on azoʙi noguvor xonadoni Fir'avnro dar mijon girift
40|46|Otas. Har suʙhu som ʙar on arza savand va ruze, ki qijomat ʙarpo savad, nido dihand ki xonadoni Fir'avnro ʙa saxttarin azoʙho darovared!»
40|47|Va on goh dar daruni otas ʙo jakdigar ʙa mucodala ʙarxezand va notavonon ʙa gardankason gujand, ki mo pajravoni sumo ʙudem, ojo metavoned andake az in otase, ki nasiʙi mo sudaast, kam kuned
40|48|Onon, ki sarkasi karda ʙudand, megujand: «Hamai mo dar otasem. Va Xudost, ki mijoni ʙandagonas dovari kardaast!»
40|49|Va onon, ki dar otasand, ʙa nigahʙononi cahannam megujand: «Az Parvardigoraton ʙixohed, to jak ruz az azoʙi mo kam kunad»
40|50|Megujand: «Ojo pajomʙaronaton ʙo dalelhoi ravsan nazdi sumo najomada ʙudand?» Megujand: «Bale». Megujand: «Pas du'o kuned». Va du'oi kofiron, ƣajri on ki ʙarʙod ravad, cize digar naxohad ʙud
40|51|Mo pajomʙaronamon va mu'minonro dar zindagii dunjo va dar ruzi qijomat, ki sohidon ʙaroi sohidi rost meistand, jori mekunem
40|52|dar ruze, ki sitamkoronro puzis (uzr) xostan naf' nadihad va nasiʙi onho la'nat ast va on saroi (makoni) ʙad
40|53|Mo ʙa Muso martaʙai hidojat dodem va on kitoʙro (tavrotro) ʙa ʙani-Isroil meros dodem
40|54|Kitoʙe, ki xud hidojat ast va ʙaroi xiradmandon andarz (pand)
40|55|Saʙr kun, ki va'dai Xudo haq ast. Baroi gunohat ʙaxsois ʙixoh va har somgohu ʙomdod ʙa sitoisi Parvardigorat tasʙeh ʙiguj
40|56|Onon, ki ʙe hec huccate, ki az osmon omada ʙosad, dar ʙorai ojoti Xudo mucodala mekunand, dar dilason ƣajri havasi ʙuzurgi nest, vale ʙa on naxohand rasid. Pas ʙa Xudo panoh ʙiʙar, ki U sunavovu ʙinost
40|57|Ofarinisi osmonu zamin az ofarinisi mardum ʙuzurgtar ast, vale ʙestari mardum namedonand
40|58|Noʙinovu ʙino ʙaroʙar nestand. Niz onhoe, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙo zistkoron jakson naʙosand. Ci andak pand megired
40|59|Qijomat meojad va dar on suʙhae nest, vale ʙestari mardum imon nameovarand
40|60|Parvardigoraton guft: «Duovu iltico kuned Maro, to sumoro icoʙat kunam. Onhoe, ki az parastisi Man sarkasi mekunand, ʙa zudi dar ajni xori ʙa cahannam darojand!»
40|61|Xudost, on ki saʙro ʙarojaton ofarid, to dar on ʙijoromed va ruzro ravsanoi ʙaxsid. Xudo fazli xud ʙa mardum arzoni medorad. Vale ʙestari mardum sukrkunanda nestand
40|62|In ast Xudoi jakto — Parvardigori sumo, ofaridgorn har cize. Xudoe ƣajri U nest. Pas ci guna az haq ʙerohaton mekunand
40|63|Hamcunin inho, ki ojoti Xudoro inkor mekunand, az imon ruj ʙarmegardonand
40|64|Xudost, ki zaminro qarorgohi sumo soxt va osmonro cun ʙinoe ʙardost. Va sumoro surat ʙaxsid va surathojatonro neku soxt. Va az cizhoi pokizavu xus ruzijaton dod. In ast Xudoi jakto — Parvardigori sumo. Bartaru ʙuzurgvor ast Xudo — on Parvardigori cahonijon
40|65|U zinda ast, Xudoe ƣajri U nest. Uro iʙodat kuned, dar hole, ki dini Uro ʙa ixlos pazirufta ʙosed, ki sitois (sukru zikri nek) az oni Xudoest, ki Parvardigori cahonijon ast
40|66|Bigu: «Maro man' kardaand, ki cizhoero, ki ʙa coi Xudo meparasted, parastis kunam, dar hole, ki az coniʙi Parvardigoram ʙaroi man daloile ravsan omadaast. Va ʙa man farmon dodaand, ki dar ʙaroʙari Parvardigori cahonijon taslim ʙosam»
40|67|Ust on Xudoe, ki sumoro az xok, sipas az nutfa, sipas az laxtai xune ʙijofaridaast. On goh sumoro, dar surati kudake ʙarovard, to ʙa sinni cavoni ʙirased va pir saved. Ba'ze az sumo pes az piri ʙimired va ʙa'ze ʙa on zamoni mu'ajjan merased va sojad ʙa aql darjoʙed
40|68|Ust, ki zinda mekunad va memironad. Va cun irodai cize kunad, megujadas: «Mavcud sav!» Pas mavcud mesavad
40|69|Ojo nadidai onhoe, ki dar ojoti Xudo kasmakas mekunand, ci guna kacrav mesavand
40|70|Kasone, ki in kitoʙro duruƣ mesumorand va on ciro, ki ʙa vasilai pajomʙaron firistodaem, takziʙ mekunand (duruƣ meʙarorand), ʙa zudi xohand donist
40|71|on goh ki tavqhoro ʙa gardanason andozand va ʙo zancirho ʙikasandason
40|72|dar oʙi cuson, sipas dar otas afruxta savand
40|73|On goh ʙa onho gufta savad: «On sarikon, ki ʙaroi Xudo megirifted, kuco hastand?»
40|74|Megujand: «Onhoro az dast dodaem, ʙalki pes az in cizero ʙa xudoi namexondaem». Xudo kofironro ʙa in tarz gumroh mekunad
40|75|In ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki ʙa nohaq dar zamin sodmoni mekarded va nozu karasma mekarded
40|76|Az darhoi cahannam doxil saved. Hamesa dar on co ʙimoned. Va cojgohi sarkason ci ʙad cojgohest
40|77|Pas saʙr kun, alʙatta, va'dai Xudo rost ast. E ʙa'ze az on cizhoro, ki ʙa onho va'da dodaem, ʙa tu nison medihem jo turo ʙimironem va onho ʙa nazdi Mo ʙozgardonida savand
40|78|Pes az tu pajomʙarone firistodaem. Dostoni ʙa'zero ʙarojat guftaem va dostoni ʙa'zero naguftaem. Va hec pajomʙarero narasad, ki ojate ʙijovarad, magar ʙa farmoni Xudo. Va cun farmoni Xudo darrasad, ʙa haq dovari gardad va onon, ki ʙar ʙotil ʙudaand, on co, zijon xohand did
40|79|Xudost, ki corpojonro ʙarojaton ofarid, to ʙar ʙa'ze savor saved va az ʙa'ze ʙixured
40|80|Va sumoro dar on manfiathost va metavoned ʙo onho ʙa hocate, ki dar nazar dored, ʙirased. Va ʙar onho va ʙar kistiho savor saved
40|81|Ojoti xudro ʙar sumo menamojonad. Pas kadom jak az ojoti Xudoro inkor mekuned
40|82|Ojo dar zamin sajr nakardaand, to ʙingarand, ki oqiʙati kasone, ki pes az onho mezistaand, ci guna ʙudaast? Mardume, ki quvvatason ʙestar va osorason dar rui zamin farovontar ʙud. Pas on cizhoe, ki ʙa dast meovardand, foida naʙaxsid
40|83|Cun pajomʙaronason ʙo dalelhoi ravsan ʙa sujason omadand, ʙa donisi xud dilxus ʙudand, to on cize, ki masxaraas mekardand, onhoro dar mijon girift
40|84|Va cun azoʙi Moro didand, guftand: «Ba Xudoi jakto imon ovardem va ʙa on cizhoe, ki sariki Xudo qaror doda ʙudem kofir sudem»
40|85|Ammo ʙa on hangom, ki azoʙi Moro didand, digar imonason ʙarojason sude naʙaxsid, In sunnati Xudost dar raftor ʙo ʙandagonas. Va kofiron dar on ruz zijon kardand
41|1|Ho, mim
41|2|Kitoʙest, ki az coniʙi On ʙaxsojandai mehruʙon nozil sudaast
41|3|Kitoʙest, ki ojahojas ʙa tafsilu fahmo ʙajon suda, Qur'onest ʙa zaʙoni araʙi ʙaroi mardume, ki medonand
41|4|Ham muƶdadihanda ast va ham ʙimdihanda. Bestarason az on e'roz kardaand (ruj gardondaand) va suxan namesunavand
41|5|Guftand: «Dilhoi mo az on ci moro ʙa on da'vat mekuni, dar parda ast va gushojamon sangin ast va mijoni movu tu hicoʙest. Tu ʙa kori xud pardoz va mo niz ʙa kori xud mepardozem»
41|6|Bigu: «Man insone hastam hamonandi sumo. Ba man vahj suda, ki xudojaton Xudoest jakto. Pas ʙa u ruj ovared va az U ʙaxsois ʙixohed. Va voj ʙar musrikon
41|7|onhoe, ki zakot namedihand va ʙa oxirat imon nadorand
41|8|Ononro, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista mekunand, podosest (mukofotest) tamomnosudani»
41|9|Bigu: «Ojo ʙa kase, ki zaminro dar du ruz ofaridaast, kofir mesaved va ʙaroi U sarikho qaror medihed? Ust Parvardigori cahonijon
41|10|Bar rui zamin kuhho padid ovard va onro purʙarakat soxt va rizqi hamaro mu'ajjan kard dar cahor ruz jakson ʙaroi hamai pursandagon
41|11|Sipas ʙa osmon pardoxt va on dude ʙud. Pas ʙa osmonu zamin guft: «Xoh jo noxoh ʙijoed». Guftand: «Farmonʙardor omadem»
41|12|On goh haft osmonro dar du ruz ofarid. Va dar har osmone korasro ʙa on vahj kard. Va osmoni dunjoro ʙa caroƣhoe ʙijorostem va hifzas kardem. In ast tadʙiri On ƣoliʙi dono»
41|13|Pas agar ruj gardonand, ʙigu: «Sumoro az ra'du ʙarqe hamonandi ra'du ʙarqe, ki ʙar Odu Samud furud omad, metarsonam
41|14|On goh ki rasuloni pes va ʙa'di onho navdason omadand va guftand, ki ƣajri Xudoi jaktoro maparasted, guftand: «Agar Parvardigori mo mexost, faristagonro az osmon mefarovard. Mo ʙa on ci sumo ʙo on firistoda sudaed, imon nameovarem»
41|15|Ammo qavmi Od ʙa nohaq dar, rui zamin gardankasi kardand va guftand: «Ci kase az mo ʙoquvvat tar ast?» Ojo namedidand, ki Xudoe, ki onhoro ofaridaast, az onho ʙo quvvattar ast, ki ojoti Moro inkor mekardand
41|16|Mo niz ʙode saxtu ƣurron dar ruzhoe sum ʙar sarason firistodem, to dar dunjo azoʙi xoriro ʙa onho ʙicasonem. Va azoʙi oxirat xorkunandatar ast va kase ʙa joriason ʙarnaxezad
41|17|Ammo qavmi Samud, hidojatason kardem. Va onho kuriro az hidojat ʙestar dust medostand, to on ki ʙa xotiri amalhoe, ki mekardand, so'iqai azoʙi xorkunanda onhoro furu girift
41|18|Va Mo kasonero, ki imon ovarda ʙudand va parhezgor ʙudand, nacot dodem
41|19|Va ruze, ki dusmanoni Xudoro gird ovarand va ʙa saf ʙironandason
41|20|cun ʙa kanori otas ojand, gusu casmho va pusthoson ʙa amalhoe, ki kardaand, ʙar ziddason sohidi dihand
41|21|Ba pusthoi xud gujand: «Caro ʙar ziddi mo sohidi doded?» Gujand: «On Xudoe, ki har cizero ʙa suxan meovarad va sumoro naxustin ʙor ʙijofarid va ʙa U ʙozgast mejoʙed, moro ʙa suxan ovardaast»
41|22|Az in ki gusu casmho va pusthojaton ʙa zijoni sumo sohidi dihand, cize nihon namedosted, ʙalki mepindosted, ki Xudo ʙar ʙisjore az korhoe, ki mekuned, ogoh nest
41|23|Va in ʙud gumone, ki ʙa Parvardigoraton dosted. Halokaton kard va dar sumori zijonkardagon daromaded
41|24|Pas agar saʙr kunand, cojgohason dar otas ast va agar ham toliʙi afv savand, kase onhoro afv nakunad
41|25|Ba ʙarojason hamdamone muqarrar kardem va onon holu ojandaro dar nazarason ʙijorostand. Va ʙar onho niz monandi pesinijonason az cinnu ins azoʙ muqarrar sud. Zero zijonkor ʙudand
41|26|Kofiron guftand: «Ba in Qur'on gus madihed va suxani ʙehuda ʙa on ʙijomezed, sojad piruz garded!»
41|27|Kofironro azoʙe saxt mecasonem va ʙadtar az on ci mekardaand, podos medihem
41|28|In ast kajfari (cazoi) dusmanoni Xudo otas. Dar daruni on xonae hamesagi dorand. In cazoi onhost, zero ojoti Moro inkor mekardand
41|29|Kofiron gujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, on du tanro az cinnu ins, ki moro gumroh kardand, ʙa mo ʙinamojon, to poj ʙar sari onho nihem, to az mo pasttar (pojontar) ravand!»
41|30|Bar onon, ki guftand: «Parvardigori mju Olloh ast» va pojdori kardaand, faristagon furud meojand, ki metarsed va ƣamgin naʙosed, sumoro ʙa ʙihiste, ki ʙa sumo va'da doda suda, xusxaʙar ast
41|31|Mo dar dunjo dustoni sumo ʙudem va niz dar oxirat dustdori sumoem. Dar ʙihist har ci dilaton ʙixohad va har ci talaʙ kuned, ʙarojaton faroham ast
41|32|Mehmonnavozist az coniʙi Xudoi ʙaxsojandai mehruʙon
41|33|Ci kasero suxan nekutar az suxani on, ki ʙa sui Xudo da'vat mekunad va korhoi soista mekunad va megujad, alʙatta, ki man az musalmononam
41|34|Xuʙivu ʙadi ʙaroʙar nestand. Hamesa ʙa nekutarin tarze cavoʙ deh, to kase, ki mijoni tuvu u dusmani ast, cun dusti mehruʙoni tu gardad
41|35|Barxurdor nasavand az in ƣajri kasone, ki ʙosaʙr ʙosand va kasone, ki az imon ʙahrae ʙuzurg dosta ʙosand
41|36|Va agar az coniʙi sajton giriftori vasvasae gardi, ʙa Xudo panoh ʙiʙar, ki U sunavovu donost
41|37|Va az nisonahoi qudrati U saʙu ruz va oftoʙu moh ast. Ba oftoʙu moh sacda makuned. Ba Xudoi jakto, ki onhoro ofaridaast, sacda kuned, agar Uro meparasted
41|38|Agar onon takaʙʙur mevarzand, onho, ki dar nazdi Parvardigori tu hastand, ʙe on ki malul sadand saʙu ruz tasʙehi U megujand (Sacda)
41|39|Va az ojoti qudrati U on, ki tu zaminro xusk meʙini. Cun oʙ ʙar on ʙifiristem, ʙa cunʙis ojad va gijoh ʙirujonad. On kas, ki onro zinda mekunad, zindakunandai murdagon ast, ki U ʙar har cize tavonost
41|40|Kasone, ki dar ojoti Mo rohi ʙotil pes megirand, ʙar Mo pusida nestand. Ojo on ki ʙa otas afkanda mesavad, ʙehtar ast jo on ki ruzi qijomat ʙe hec vahsate meojad? Harci mexohed ʙikuned, U ʙa korhojaton ʙinost
41|41|Ba cazoi xud rasand onon, ki ʙa Qur'on, ki ʙaroi hidojatason omadaast, imon nameovarand, hol on ki kitoʙe arcmand ast
41|42|Na az pesi ruj ʙotil ʙa u roh joʙad va na az pas. Nozilsuda az coniʙi Xudovande hakimu sutudanist. (loiqi sukru sipos ast)
41|43|Har ci dar ʙorai tu megujand, dar ʙorai pajomʙaroni pes az tu niz guftaand. Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ham ʙaxsojanda ast va ham sohiʙi uquʙatest dardovar
41|44|Agar Qur'onro ʙa zaʙoni Acam mefiristodem, meguftand: «Caro ojotas ʙa ravsani ʙajon nasudaast? Kitoʙe ʙa zaʙoni Acam va pajomʙare araʙ?» Bigu: «In kitoʙ ʙaroi onho, ki imon ovardand, hidojat va sifost va onho, ki imon naovardand, gushojason sangin ast va casmonason kur ast, cunonand, ki gui onhoro az coe dur sado mekunand
41|45|Musoro kitoʙ dodem, ammo dar on ixtilof kardand. Va agar on suxane, ki Parvardigorat az pes gufta ʙud, nameʙud mijonason kor ʙa pojon meomad. Va, alʙatta, hanuz ʙa saxti dar suʙhaand
41|46|Har kas, ki kore soista kunad, ʙa foidai xudi ust va har ki ʙad kunad, ʙa zijoni ust. Va Parvardigori tu ʙa ʙandagon zulm ravo namedorad
41|47|Ilm ʙa ruzi qijomat nazdi Ust. Va har mevae az ƣilofi xud ʙerun meojad va har modae homilador mesavadu mezojad, alʙatta ki U ʙa on ogoh ast. Va on ruz, ki onhoro nido dihad, ki sarikoni Man kucojand? Gujand: Ogohat kardem, ki kase az mo ʙa sirk guvohi namedihad
41|48|Va on ciro pes az in ʙa, xudoi mexondand, az dast dodand va donistand, ki rohi gureze nadorand
41|49|Odami har ci talaʙi xajr kunad, xasta namesavad, ammo cun ʙadi ʙa u ʙirasad, ʙadandesu noumed megardad
41|50|Agar pas az rance, ki ʙa u rasida, rahmate ʙa u ʙicasonem, megujad: «In haqqi man ast va napindoram, ki qijomate ʙarpo savad. Va agar ham maro nazdi Parvardigoram ʙargardonand, alʙatta, ki nazdi U holate xustar ʙosad». Pas kofironro ʙa amalhoe, ki kardaand, ogoh mekunem va ʙa onho azoʙe saxt mecasonem
41|51|Cun ʙa odami ne'mate ato kunem, rujgardon mesavad va ʙa takaʙʙur gardan ʙolo mekunad. Va agar ʙa u ʙadie ʙirasad, ʙisjor farjodu fiƣon mekunad
41|52|Bigu: «Ci meʙined?» Agar in kitoʙ az coniʙi Xudost va sumo ʙa on imon nameovared, gumrohtar az kase, ki hamcunon rohi muxolifat (ziddijat) dar pes giriftaast, kist
41|53|Ba zudi, ojoti qudrati Xudro dar atrofi olam va dar vucudi xudason ʙa onho nison xohem dod, to ʙarojason oskor savad, ki, U haq ast. Ojo in ki Parvardigori tu dar hama co hozir ast, kofi nest
41|54|Bahus (ogoh) ʙos, ki onho az didori Parvardigorason dar suʙhaand. Bahus ʙos, ki U ʙar har cize ihota dorad
42|1|Ho, mim
42|2|Ajn, sin, qof
42|3|Xudovandi ƣoliʙu hakim ʙa tu va kasone, ki pes az tu ʙudand, incunin vahj mefiristad
42|4|az oni Ust, har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast. Va Ust on ʙalandmartaʙai ʙuzurgvor
42|5|Nazdik ast, ki osmonho ʙa ʙoloi jakdigar dar ham sikanand va faristagon ʙa sitoisi Parvardigorason tasʙeh megujand va ʙaroi sokinoni zamin ʙaxsois metalaʙand. Ogoh ʙosed, ki Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
42|6|Xudo muroqiʙi (noziri) a'moli kasonest, ki ƣajri Uro ʙa dusti giriftand. Va tu vakili onho nesti
42|7|Va niz in Qur'onro ʙa zaʙoni araʙi ʙar tu vahj kardem to ummulquro va sokinoni atrofasro ʙim dihj. Hamcunin ononro az ruzi qijomat, ki dar on sakke nest, ʙitarsoni, ki guruhe dar ʙihistand va guruhe dar otasi suzon
42|8|Agar Xudo mexost, hamaro jak ummat karda ʙud. Vale U har kiro ki ʙixohad, ʙa rahmati xud darovarad va sitamkoronro hec dustu jovare nest
42|9|Ojo ƣajri Xudoro ʙa dusti giriftand? Dusti haqiqi Xudost. Va Ust, ki murdagonro zinda mekunad va Ust, ki ʙar har kore tavonost
42|10|Dar har ci ixtilof mekuned, hukmas ʙo Xudost. In Xudoi jakto Parvardigori man ast. Bar U tavakkal kardam va ʙa U ruj meovaram
42|11|Ofaridgori osmonhovu zamin ast. Baroi sumo, ham az sumo hamsarone ʙijofarid. Va niz ʙaroi corpojon cufthoe padid ovard. Vo ofarinisi hamsaron ʙar sumoraton meafzojad. Hec ciz monandi U nest va Ust, ki sunavovu ʙinost
42|12|Kalidhoi osmonhovu zamin az oni Ust. Dar ruzii har ki ʙixohad, kusois medihad jo tang megirad va U ʙa har cize donost
42|13|Baroi sumo dinu oine muqarrar kard az hamon guna, ki ʙa Nuh tavsija karda ʙud va az on ci ʙar tu vahj kardaem va ʙa Iʙrohimu Muso va Iso tavsija kardaem, ki dinro ʙarpoj nigah dored va dar on firqa-firqa masaved. Tahammuli on ci ʙa on da'vat mekuned, ʙar musrikon dusvor ast. Xudo har kiro xohad, ʙaroi pajƣamʙarii Xud intixoʙ mekunad va har kiro ʙa u ʙozgardad, ʙa Xud roh menamojad
42|14|Az rui hasadu adovat firqa-firqa sudand, az on pas, ki ʙa donis dast joftand. Va agar Parvardigori tu az pes muqarrar nakarda ʙud, ki onhoro to zamone mu'ajjan muhlat ast, ʙar onho hukmi azoʙ meraft. Va kasone, ki ʙa'd az onho vorisi kitoʙi Xudo sudaand, dar ʙorai on saxt ʙa suʙha aftodaand
42|15|Baroi on da'vat kun va cunon ki farmon joftai, pojdori kun va az pai xohishojason marav va ʙigu: «Ba kitoʙe, ki Xudo nozil kardaast, imon doram va ʙa man farmon dodaand, ki dar mijoni sumo ʙa adolat raftor kunam. Xudoi jakto Parvardigori mo va Parvardigori sumost. A'moli mo az oni mo va a'moli sumo az oni sumo. Mijonu movu sumo hec muhoccae (dusmanie) nest. Xudo moro dar jak co cam' meovarad va ʙozgast ʙa sui Ust!»
42|16|Va kasone, ki dar ʙorai Xudo cidol mekunand, pas az on ki da'vati Uro icoʙat kardaand, nazdi Parvardigorason huccatason nociz ast. Bar onhost xasmi Xudo va ʙar onhost azoʙe saxt
42|17|Xudost, ki in kitoʙi ʙarxaq va tarozuro nozil kardaast. Va tu ci medoni? Sojad qijomat nazdik ʙosad
42|18|Onon, ki ʙovaras nadorand, (omadani) onro ʙa sitoʙ metalaʙand va onon, ki imon ovardaand, az on ʙimnokand va medonand, ki haq ast. Ogoh ʙos, kasone, ki dar ʙorai qijomat cidol mekunand, saxt dar gumrohi hastand
42|19|Xudo ʙo ʙandagonas mehruʙon ast. Har kiro ʙixohad, ruzi medihad. Va U tavonovu ƣoliʙ ast
42|20|Har kas kisti oxiratro ʙixohad, ʙa kistaas meafzoem va har kas kisti dunjoro ʙixohad, ʙa u ato mekunem, vale digar dar kisti oxiratas nasiʙe nest
42|21|Ojo musrikonro ʙutonest, ki dine ʙarojason ovardaand, ki Xudo ruxsati onro nadodaast? Va agar qasdi ta'xiri (ʙa der partoftani) azoʙason naʙud, korason ʙa pojon omada ʙud va sitamkoronro azoʙest dardovar
42|22|Sitamkoronro ʙini, ki az hosili korhojason ʙimnokand. Va alʙatta, ʙa cazoi xud xohand rasid. Vale onho, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, dar ʙoƣhoi ʙihistand. Har ci ʙixohand, nazdi Parvardigorason hast. Va in fazlu ʙaxsoisti ʙuzurgest
42|23|In ast on cize, ki Xudo on guruh az ʙandagokasro, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙa on muƶda medihad. Bigu: «Bar on taʙliƣi Qur'on muzde az sumo cuz dust dostani xesovandon namexoham». Va har ki kori neke kunad, ʙa nekuijas meafzoem, zero Xudo ʙaxsojandavu sukrpazir ast
42|24|Jo megujand, ki ʙar Xudo duruƣ meʙandad. Agar Xudo ʙixohad, ʙar dili tu muhr menihad. Va Xudo ʙa kaligmoti xud ʙotilro mahv mekunad va haqro soʙit megardonad. U ʙar har ci dar dilho meguzarad, donost
42|25|Va Ust, ki tavʙai ʙandagonasro mepazirad va az gunohon afvason mekunad va har ci mekuned, medonad
42|26|Va duʹoi kasonero, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, icoʙat mekunad va az fazli xud ononro ʙisjor medihad. Va kofironro azoʙe saxt ast
42|27|Agar Xudo ruzii ʙandagonasro ʙisjor kunad, dar zamin fasod mekunand, vale ʙa miqdore, ki ʙixohad, ruzi mefiristad. Zero ʙar ʙandagoni xud ogohu ʙinost
42|28|Va Ust on Xudoe, ki ʙa'd az noumedijason ʙoron mefiristad va rahmati Xudro ʙa hama co parokanda mekunad va Ust korsozu sohiʙi hamdu sano
42|29|Va az nisonahoi qudrati U ofarinisi osmonhovu zamin va parokandani cunʙandagon dar on dust. Va har goh ʙixohad, ʙar cam' ovardanason tavonost
42|30|Agar sumoro musiʙate rasad, ʙa xotiri korhoest, ki kardaed. Va Xudo ʙisjore az gunohonro afv mekunad
42|31|Sumo natavoned dar rui zamin az U ʙigurezed va sumoro ƣajri U korsozu jovare nest
42|32|Az nisonahoi qudrati U kistihoest cun kuh ki dar darjoho ravonand
42|33|Agar ʙixohad, ʙodro nigah medorad, to kistiho ʙar rui darjo az raftan ʙozmonand. Alʙatta dar in ʙaroi saʙrkunandagoni sukrguzor iʙrathoest
42|34|Jo onhoro ʙa xotiri amalhojason ƣark mekunad va ʙisjorero niz meʙaxsojad
42|35|Va to ʙidonand, kasone, ki dar ojoti Mo cidol mekunand. Ononro hec gurezgohe nest
42|36|On ci sumoro dodaand, ʙahrai in zindagii dunjavist. Va on ci dar nazdi Xudost, ʙaroi onho, ki imon ovardaand va ʙa Parvardigorason tavakkal mekunand, ʙehtaru pojandatar ast
42|37|Va on kasone, ki az gunohoni ʙuzurg va zistiho parhez mekunand va cun dar xasm savand, xatohoro meʙaxsojand
42|38|va onon, ki da'vati Parvardigorasonro qaʙul mekunand va namoz meguzorand va korason ʙar pojai masvarat ʙo jakdigar ast va az on ci ʙa onho ruzi dodaem, sadaqa mekunand
42|39|va onon, ki cun sitame ʙa onho rasad, intiqom megirand
42|40|Cazoi har ʙadi ʙadiest monandi on. Pas kase, ki afv kunad va osti kunad, muzdas ʙo Xudost, zero U sitamkoronro dust nadorad
42|41|Bar kasone, ki pas az zulme, ki ʙar onho rafta ʙosad, intiqom megirand, malomate nest
42|42|Malomat ʙar kasonest, ki ʙa mardum zulm mekunand va ʙa nohaq dar rui zamin sarkasi mekunand. Baroi onhost azoʙe dardovar
42|43|Va on ki saʙr kunad va az xato darguzarad, in az korhoi pisandida ast
42|44|Har kasro, ki Xudo gumroh kunad, az on pas hec duste naxohad dost. Va zolimonro meʙini, ki cun azoʙro ʙingarand, megujand: «Ojo moro rohi ʙozgaste hast?»
42|45|Onhoro meʙini, ki ʙa cahannam meʙarand. Tarsonu xor az gusai casm nigohe duzdida mekunand. Kasone, ki imon ovarda ʙudand, megujand: «Inho xud va kasonasonro dar ruzi qijomat ʙarʙod dodand». Ogoh ʙos, ki sitamkoron dar azoʙi doim xohand ʙud
42|46|Ƣajri Xudo joru madadgore nadorand va har kasro, ki Xudo gumroh kunad, hec rohe ʙarojas nest
42|47|Pes az on ki ruze ʙijojad, ki az coniʙi Xudo ʙozgaste nadorad, ʙa Parvardigoraton cavoʙi qaʙul dihed. Dar on ruz na panohe xohed dost va na kase az sumo muhofizat tavonad kard
42|48|Agar ruj gardonand, turo nafiristodaem, ki nigahʙonason ʙosi. Bar tu ƣajri rasonidani pajƣom hec nest. Va Mo cun ʙa inson az rahmati Xud ʙicasonem, sodmon megardad va agar ʙa xotiri korhoe, ki kardaast, noravoi ʙa u rasad, nosiposi mekunad
42|49|Az oni Xudost farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin. Har ci ʙixohad, meofarinad. Ba har ki ʙixohad, duxtar meʙaxsad va ʙa har ki ʙixohad, pisar meʙaxsad
42|50|Va jo ham pisar dihad va ham duxtar. Va har kasro ʙixohad, aqim (nozo) megardonad, zero U donovu tavonost
42|51|Hec ʙasarero narasad, ki Xudo cuz ʙa vahj jo az on sui parda ʙo u suxan gujad. Jo faristae mefiristad to ʙa farmoni U har ci ʙixohad, ʙa u vahj kunad. U ʙalandpojavu hakim ast
42|52|Hamcunin kalomi Xudro ʙa farmoni Xud ʙa tu vahj kardem. Tu namedonisti kitoʙu imon cist. Vale Mo onro nure soxtem to har jak az ʙandagonamonro, ki ʙixohem, ʙa on hidojat kunem va tu ʙa rohi rost roh nison medihi
42|53|rohi on Xudoe, ki az oni Ust har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast. Ogoh ʙosed, ki hamai korho ʙa Xudo ʙozmegardad
43|1|Ho, mim
43|2|Savgand ʙa in kitoʙi ravsangar
43|3|Mo in kitoʙro Qur'one araʙi qaror dodem, ʙosad, ki ʙa aql darjoʙed
43|4|Va on dar ummulkitoʙ ast dar nazdi Mo: kitoʙe arcmandu hikmatomez
43|5|Ojo ʙa on saʙaʙ, ki mardume az had guzasta hasted, az sumo ruj gardonem va Qur'onro az sumo dareƣ dorem
43|6|Ba mijoni pesinijon pajomʙaroni ʙisjore firistodem
43|7|Va hec pajomʙare ʙar onho firistoda namesud, ki masxaraas nakarda ʙosand
43|8|Onhoro, ki az onho ʙoquvvattar ʙudand, halok kardem. Va dostoni pesinijon guzast
43|9|Agar az onho ʙipursi: «Ci kase osmonhovu zaminro ofaridaast?» Megujand: «Onhoro on ƣoliʙi dono ofaridaast!»
43|10|On ki zaminro ʙisoti sumo soxt va ʙarojaton rohho dar on padid ovard, ʙosad, ki hidojat saved
43|11|Va on ki az osmon oʙ firistod ʙa miqdor. Va ʙa on sarzamini murdaro zinda kardem. Sumo niz incunin az gurho ʙerun ovarda saved
43|12|va on ki hamai cufthoro ʙijofarid. Va ʙarojaton az kistiho va corpojon markaʙho soxt, ki savor saved
43|13|Va cun ʙar pusti onho qaror girifted, ne'mati Parvardigoratonro jod kuned va ʙigued: «Pok ast on kas, ki inhoro romi mo kard, vagarna moro tavoni on naʙud
43|14|Va mo ʙa sui Parvardigoramon ʙozmegardem»
43|15|Va ʙaron U az mijoni ʙandagonas farzande qoil sudand. Odami ʙa oskoro nosipos (nosukr) ast
43|16|Ojo U az mijoni maxluqonas ʙaroi Xud duxtaron ʙargirifta va pisaronro xosi sumo kardaast
43|17|Va cun ʙa jake az onho muƶdai tavalludi hamon cizero dihand, ki ʙa Xudoi rahmon nisʙat doda, rujas sijoh gardad va pur az xasm savad
43|18|Ojo on ki ʙa orois parvaris jofta (ja'ne duxtar) va dar hangomi cidol oskor namegardad, az oni Xudost
43|19|Va faristagonro, ki ʙandagoni Xudojand, zan pindostand. Ojo ʙa hangomi ofarinisason on co hozir ʙudaand? Ba zudi in sohidiasonro menavisand va az onho ʙozxost mesavad
43|20|Guftand: «Agar Xudoi rahmon mexost, mo faristagonro nameparastidem». On ci megujand, az rui nodonist va ƣajri ʙa duruƣ suxan namegujand
43|21|Ojo pes az Qur'on kitoʙe ʙarojason nozil kardaem, ki aknun ʙa on cang mezanand? (pajravi mekunand)
43|22|Na, megujand: «Padaronamonro ʙar dine joftem va mo az pai onho meravem»
43|23|Va on tavr pes az tu ʙa kadom dehae ʙimdihandae firistodem, mutana'imonas (sohiʙne'matonas) guftand: «Padaronamonro ʙar dine joftem va mo ʙa amalhoi onho iqtido (panravi) mekunem»
43|24|Guft: «Hatto agar ʙaroi sumo cize ʙijovaram, ki az on ci padaronatonro ʙar on jofta ʙuded, hidojatkunandatar ʙosad?» Guftand: «Mo ʙa dine, ki sumoro ʙa on firistodaand, ʙeimonem»
43|25|Pas az onho intiqom giriftem. Va ʙingar, ki oqiʙati duruƣʙarorandagon ci guna ʙudaast
43|26|Va Iʙrohim ʙa padaru qavmas guft: «Man az on ci sumo meparasted, ʙezoram
43|27|ƣajri on ki maro ofarida, ki U rohnamoijam xohad kard»
43|28|Va in suxanro dar farzandoni xud suxane pojanda kard, ʙosad, ki ʙa Xudo ʙozgardand
43|29|Va Man inhovu padaronasonro az zindagi ʙahramand kardam, to on goh ki haq va pajomʙare ravsangar ʙa sujason omad
43|30|Cun haq ʙar onho oskor sud, guftand: «In codust va mo ʙa on imon nameovarem»
43|31|Guftand: «Caro in Qur'on ʙar marde az ʙuzurgmardoni on du deha nozil nasudaast?»
43|32|Ojo onon rahmati Parvardigoratro taqsim mekunand? Xol on ki mo ruzii onhoro dar in zindagii dunjo mijonason taqsim mekunem. Va ʙa'zero ʙa martaʙa ʙolotar az ʙa'ze digar qaror dodaem, to ʙa'ze ʙa'zi digarro ʙa xidmat girand. Va rahmati Parvardigorat az on ci onho cam' meovarand, ʙehtar ast
43|33|Va agar na on ʙud, ki hamai mardum jak ummat namesudand, saqfhoi xonahoi kasonero, ki Xudoi rahmonro ʙovar nadorand, az nuqra mekardem va ʙar onho nardʙonhoe, menihodem, to ʙar on ʙolo ravand
43|34|Va ʙaroi xonahojason niz darhoe az nuqra mekardem va taxthoe, ki ʙar onho takja zanand
43|35|va az har guna zinat. Va hamai inho ʙahramandii nocizi dunjavist, hol on ki oxirat dar nazdi Parvardigori tu ʙaroi parhezgoron ast
43|36|Har kas, ki az jodi Xudoi rahmon ruj gardonad, sajtone ʙar u oʙasta mekunem,, ki hameosa hamrohas ʙosad
43|37|Va on sajtonho ononro az rohi Xudo ʙozmegardonand, vale pindorand, ki hidojatjoftagonand
43|38|To on goh ki nazdi Mo ojad, megujad: «Ej kos, durii manu tu (misli) durii masriqu maƣriʙ ʙud. Va tu ci hamrohi ʙade ʙudi»
43|39|Cun sitam karded, on ruz pusajmoni foida nakunad va har du dar azoʙ sarik ʙosed
43|40|Ojo tu mexohi ʙa karon suxan ʙisunavoni jo kuron va onhoero, ki dar gumrohii oskor hastand, roh nison dihi
43|41|Va agar turo ʙiʙarem, az onho intiqom megirem
43|42|Jo on azoʙero, ki ʙa onho va'da dodaem, ʙa tu nison medihem, ki Mo ʙar onho tavono hastem
43|43|Pas dar on ci ʙa tu vahj sudaast, cang ʙizan, (pajravi kun), ki tu ʙar rohi rost hasti
43|44|Va Qur'on saʙaʙi ʙalandovoza gastani tu va qavmi tust va ʙa zudi ʙozxost saved
43|45|Az pajomʙaroni Mo, ki pes az tu firistodaem, ʙipurs: «Ojo ƣajri Xudoi rahmon digarero ʙaroi parastisi onho qaror doda ʙudem?»
43|46|Va alʙatta Musoro hamroh ʙo ojoti Xud ʙar Fir'avn va raisoni qavmas firistodem va guft: «Man firistodai Parvardigori cahonijonam!»
43|47|Cun ojoti Moro ʙar onon arza dost, ʙa nogoh hama az on ʙa xanda aftodand
43|48|Va har mu'cizae, ki ʙa onho nison dodem, az mu'cizai digar azimtar ʙud. On goh hamaro ʙa azoʙ giriftor kardem, ʙosad, ki ʙozgardand
43|49|Guftand: «Ej codugar, Parvardigoratro ʙo on nomhoe, ki ʙo tu vahj kardaast, ʙarom mo ʙixon, ki mo hidojatsudagonem»
43|50|Cun azoʙro az onho ʙardostem, pajmoni xudro sikastand
43|51|Fir'avn dar mijoni mardumas nido dod, ki ej qavmi man, ojo podsohii Misru in cujʙoron, ki az zeri poi man cori hastand, az oni man nestand? Ojo nameʙined
43|52|Ojo man ʙehtaram jo in mardi xori zalil, ki durust suxan guftan natavonad
43|53|Caro dasthojasro ʙa dastʙandhoi tillo najorostaand? Va caro guruhe az faristagon hamrohas najomadaand

43|55|Cun Moro ʙa xasm ovardand, az onho intiqom giriftem va hamagonro ƣarq soxtem
43|56|Ononro dar sumori guzastagon va doston ʙaroi ojandagon kardem
43|57|Va cun dostoni pisari Marjam ovarda sud, qavmi tu ʙa sodmoni farjod zadand
43|58|va guftan, d: «Ojo xudojoni mo ʙehtarand jo U?» Va in suxanro faqat ʙaroi cidol ʙo tu guftaand, ki mardume xusumat kunandaand
43|59|U faqat ʙandae ʙud, ki Mo ne'matas ato kardem va mojai iʙrati ʙani- Isroilas gardonidem
43|60|Agar mexostem, ʙa coi sumo faristagone padid meovardem, to dar rui zamin conisini sumo gardand

43|64|Xudoi jakto Parvardigori manu Parvardigori sumost. Uro ʙiparasted. Rohi rost in ast»

45|1|Ho, mim

45|4|Va dar ofarinisi sumo va parokanda sudani cunʙandagon iʙrathost ʙaroi ahli jaqin. (imon)
45|5|Omadusudi saʙu ruz va rizqe, ki Xudo az osmon mefiristad va zamini murdaro ʙa on zinda mekunad va niz dar vazisi ʙodho iʙrathost ʙaroi oqilon
45|6|Inho ojoti Xudost, ki ʙa rosti ʙar tu tilovat mekunem. Ƣajri Xudovu ojotas ʙa kadom suxan imon meovarand
45|7|Voj ʙar har duruƣʙofi gunahkore
45|8|Ojoti Xudoro, ki ʙar u xonda mesavad, mesunavad. On goh ʙa gardankasi saxt meistad, cunon ki gui hec nasunidaast. Pas ʙa azoʙe dardovaras ʙasorat (xusxaʙar) deh

45|10|Pesi rujason cahannam ast. Va mole, ki ʙa dast ovardaand va kasone, ki ƣajri Xudoi jakto ʙa xudoi giriftaand, ʙa holason foida nakunad. Onhorost azoʙe ʙuzurg
45|11|In rahnamoiest. Va onon, ki ʙa ojoti Parvardigorason imon nameovarand, ʙarojason azoʙest va saxttarin azoʙhoi dardovar

45|13|Romi sumo soxt on ci dar osmonhost va on ci dar zamin ast. Hama az oni Ust. Dar in ʙaroi fikrkunandagon iʙrathoest
45|14|Ba kasone, ki imon ovardaand, ʙigu: «Az xatoi kasone, ki ʙa ruzhoi Xudo ʙovar nadorand, darguzared, to xud on mardumro ʙa cazoi amalhoe, ki murtakiʙ sudaand (kardaand), cazo dihad
45|15|Har kas kori soistae kunad, ʙa naf'i xudi ust va har kas murtakiʙi kori ʙade savad, ʙa zijoni ust. Sipas hama ʙa sui Parvardigoraton ʙozgardonda mesaved
45|16|Mo ʙa ʙani-Isroil kitoʙ va ilmi dovarivu pajomʙari ato kardem va az cizhoi pokizavu xus ruzijason kardem. Va ʙar cahonijon ʙartarijason (ʙehtariason) dodem
45|17|Va onhoro dar ʙorai on amr daloile ravsan dodem. Va dar on az rui hasadu kina ixtilof kardand, on goh, ki donis joftand. Xudo dar ruzi qijomat dar on ci ixtilof (ziddijat) mekardand, dovari xohad kard
45|18|Pas turo ʙa rohi din andoxtem. Bo on roh ʙirav va az pai xohisi nodonon marav

45|20|In Qur'on dalelhoi ravsani mardum va hidojatu rahmatest ʙaroi ahli jaqin
45|21|Ojo okon, ki kunandai ʙadiho mesavand, mepindorand, ki dar sumori kasone, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, qarorason medihem? Va ojo zindagivu margason jakson ast? Ci ʙad dovari mekunand
45|22|Va Xudo osmonhovu zaminro ʙa haq ʙijofarid, to har kasero ʙaroʙari kore, ki kardaast, cazo dihad va ʙa onho sitam nasavad
45|23|Ojo on kasro, ki havasasro cun xudoi xud girift va Xudo az rui ilm gumrohas kard va ʙar gusu dilas muhr nihod va ʙar didagonas parda afkand, didai? Agar Xudo hidojat nakunad, ci kase uro hidojat xohad kard? Caro pand namegired
45|24|Va guftand: «Cuz zindagii dunjavii mo hec nest. Memiremu zinda mesavem va moro ƣajri dahr halok nakunad». Ononro ʙa on donise nest va faqat dar pindore hastand
45|25|Va cun ojoti ravsani Mo ʙar onho tilovat savad, huccatason in ast, ki megujand: «Agar rost megued, padaroni moro zinda kuned»
45|26|Bigu: «Xudost, ki sumoro zinda mekunad, pas memiranad va sipas hamaro dar ruzi qijomat, — ki sake dar on nest, — cam' meovarad. Vale ʙestari mardum namedonand!»
45|27|Az oni Xudovand ast farmonravoii osmonu zamin. Va on ruz, ki qijomat ʙarpo savad, ahli ʙotil zijon xohand kard

45|29|In navistai Most, ki ʙa haq suxan megujad, zero Mo korhoero, ki mekardaed, menavistaem

46|1|Ho, mim
46|2|Nozil sudani in kitoʙ az coniʙi Xudoi ƣoliʙu hakim ast
46|3|Mo osmonhovu zamin va on ciro, ki dar mijoni on dust, ʙa hak, va to muddate mu'ajjan ofaridaem. Va kofiron az on ci onhoro metarsonand, ruj megardonand
46|4|Bigu: «Az onhoe, ki ƣajri Olloh ʙa xudoi mexoned, xaʙar dihed. Ba man nison dihed, ki az in zamin ci cizro ofaridaand? Jo dar xilqati (ofaridani) osmonho sirkatdostaand? Agar rost megued, ʙaroi man kitoʙe, ki pes az in Qur'on omada ʙosad jo agar donise az pesinijon mondaast, ʙijovared
46|5|Va kist gumrohtar az on, ki ʙa coi Olloh cizero ʙa xudoi mexonad, ki to ruzi qijomat ʙa u cavoʙ namedihad, va ʙuton az du'oi ʙutparaston ʙexaʙarand
46|6|Va cun dar qijomat mardumro cam' orand, ʙuton ʙo parastandagoni xud dusman ʙosand va az iʙodatason munkirand
46|7|Cun ojoti Mo ʙa ravsani ʙa onon xonda savad, kofiron haqiqatero, ki ʙarojason nozil sudaast, gujand: «Coduii oskor ast»
46|8|Jo megujand: «In kitoʙ duruƣest, ki xud ʙoftaast!» Bigu: «Agar man onro cun duruƣe ʙa ham ʙofta ʙosam, sumo nametavoned xasmi Xudoro az man ʙozdored. Xudo az on ta'naho, ki ʙa on mezaned, ogohtar ast. Va sohidii U mijoni manu sumo kofist. Va Ust ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon!»
46|9|Bigu: «Man az mijoni digar pajomʙaron navomada (avvalin) nestam va namedonam, ki ʙar man jo ʙar sumo ci xohad sud. Man ʙa cize ƣajri on ci ʙa man vahj mesavad, pajravi namekunam va man faqat ʙimdihandae oskor hastam»
46|10|Bigu: «Ci mekuned, agar Qur'on az coniʙi Xudo ʙosad va sumo ʙa on imon najovared? Jake az ʙani-Isroil ʙa on sohidi dod va imon ovard. Vale sumo gardankasi mekuned. Xudo mardumi sitamkorro hidojat namekunad!»
46|11|Kofiron mu'minonro guftand: «Agar dar on xajre meʙud, inho az mo pestar qaʙul namekardand». Va cun ʙa on roh najoftand, xohand guft, ki in duruƣe derina ast
46|12|Va pes az on kitoʙi Muso rohnamovu rahmat ʙud. Va in kitoʙest tasdiqkunandai on ʙa zaʙoni araʙi to sitamkoronro ʙime va nekukoronro xusxaʙare ʙosad
46|13|Alʙatta onon, ki guftand, ki Parvardigori mo Olloh ast, va sipas pojdori kardand, ʙime ʙar onho nest va anduhgin namesavand
46|14|Inho ʙa mukofoti amalhojason ahli ʙihistand va dar on co covidonaand
46|15|Odamiro ʙa neki kardan ʙo padaru modari xud suporis kardem. Modaras ʙori uro ʙa dusvori ʙardost va ʙa dusvori ʙar zamin nihod. Va muddati haml to az sir ʙozgiriftanas si moh ast to cun ʙa sinni cavoni rasad va ʙa cihilsolagi darojad, gujad: «Ej Parvardigori man, ʙa man ʙijomuz to sukri ne'mate, ki ʙar man va ʙar padaru modaram ato kardai, ʙa on coj oram. Kore soista ʙikunam, ki Tu az on xusnud savi va farzandoni maro soleh kun. Man ʙa Tu ʙozgastam va az taslimsudagonam»
46|16|Inho kasone hastand, ki korhoi nekasonro mepazirem va az gunohason darmeguzarem. Dar zumrai ahli ʙihistand. Har va'dae, ki ʙa onho doda suda, rost ast
46|17|Va on ki ʙa padaru modaras guft: «Uf ʙar sumo, ojo ʙa man va'da medihed, ki az guram ʙarxezonand va hol on ki mardume pes az man ʙudaand, ki ʙarnaxostaand? Va on du ʙa dargohi Xudo istiƣosa (dodxohi) mekunand va, gujand: «Voj ʙar tu, imon ʙijovar, ki va'dai Xudo haq ast!» Megujad: «Inho cize cuz hamon afsonai pesinijon nest!»
46|18|Dar ʙorai inho hamon suxan, ki dar ʙorai ummathoi pesin az cinnu ins gufta suda ʙud, ʙa haqiqat mepajvandad. Inho zijonkunandagonand
46|19|Va har jakro nisʙat ʙa kore, ki kardaast, daracahost, to Xudo cazoi korhojasonro ʙa tamomi ʙidihad va ʙa on on sitam namesavad
46|20|Va ruze, ki kofironro ʙar otas arza kunand: dar zindagii dunjavi az cizhoi pokiza va xus ʙahramand suded, imruz ʙa azoʙi xori cazojaton medihand. Va in ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki dar zamin ʙe hec haqqe takaʙʙuri mekarded va ʙadkori pes girifta ʙuded
46|21|Barodari qavmi Odro ʙa jod ʙijovar, ki cun qavmi xudro dar Ahqof ʙim dod — va pes az u pajomʙarone ʙudand va raftandu pas az u pajomʙarone omadand, — ki ƣajri Xudoi jaktoro naparasted, ki man az azoʙi ruze ʙuzurg ʙar sumo metarsam
46|22|Guftand: «Ojo omadai, to moro az xudojonamon rujgardon sozi? Agar rost megui, har ci ʙa mo va'da dodai, ʙijovar»
46|23|Guft: «Inro Xudo medonad va man on ciro ʙa on firistoda sudaam, ʙa sumo merasonam. Vale meʙinam, ki mardume nodon hasted»
46|24|Cun aʙre didand, ki az coniʙi rudxonahoson meojad, guftand: «In aʙre ʙoronzost». Na in hamon cizest, ki onro ʙa sitoʙ metalaʙided. Bod ast va dar on ʙod azoʙe dardovar
46|25|ʙa farmoni Parvardigoras hama cizro halok mekunad. Cunon sudand, ki aknun faqat xonahojasonro ʙini. Va Mo mucrimonro (gunahgoronro) in tavr cazo medihem
46|26|Va onho cunon tavonu qudrat doda ʙudem, ki ʙa sumo nadidaem. Barojason gusu casmu dil qaror dodem. Vale gusu casmu dilason ʙa holason hec foida nakard, zero ojoti Xudoro inkor mekardand, to on azoʙe, ki ʙa masxaraas megiriftand, onhoro furu srift
46|27|Mo hamai qarijahoero (dehahoero), ki atrofi sumo ʙudaand, halok kardaem va ojotro gunogun ʙajon kardem, sojad, ki ʙozgardand
46|28|Pas caro on xudojone, ki ƣajri Olloh ʙaroi nazdiki ʙa xudoi girifta ʙudand, jorijason nakardand, ʙalki az nazarason gum sudand? Ija ast duruƣu ʙoftahojason
46|29|Va guruhe az cinro nazdi tu ravona kardem, to Qur'onro ʙisnavand. Cun ʙa hazratas (nazdas) rasidand, guftand: «Gus andozed! Cun ʙa pojon omad, monandi ʙimdihandagone nazdi qavmi xud ʙozgastand
46|30|Guftand: «Ej qavmi mo, mo kitoʙe sunidem, ki ʙa'd az Muso nozil suda, kitoʙhoi pesinro tasdiq mekunad va ʙa haq va rohi rost roh menamojad
46|31|Ej qavmi mo, in da'vatkunanda ʙa Xudoro qaʙul kuned va ʙa u imon ʙijovared, to Xudo gunohonatonro ʙiʙaxsojad va sumoro az azoʙe dardovar dar amon dorad
46|32|Va har kase, ki ʙa in da'vatkunanda cavoʙ nagujad, nametavonad, dar rui zamin az Xudo ʙigurezad va uro ƣajri Xudo hec jovare nest va dar gumrohii oskorest!»
46|33|Ojo nameʙinand, ki Xudo jaktost, on ki osmonhovu zaminro ʙijofarid va dar ofaridani onho darnamond. U metavonad murdagonro zinda kunad. Bale, U ʙar har kore tavonost
46|34|Ruze, ki kofiron ʙa otas arza savand... Ojo in haqiqat nest? Gujand: «Bale, ʙa Parvardigoramon savgand!» Gujad: «Ba xotiri on ki kofir ʙuded, inak azoʙro ʙicased!»
46|35|Pas pojdori kun, hamcunon ki pajomʙaroni ululazm (ʙoazm) pojdori karda ʙudand, Va dar uquʙatason sitoʙ makun. On ruz, ki on va'daero, ki ʙa onho doda suda, ʙingarand, pindorand, ki cuz ʙa qadri so'ate az ruz dar gur namonda ʙudand. In rasonidani pajƣom ast. Ojo cuz nofarmonon ʙa halokat merasand
47|1|Xudo amalhoi kasonero, ki kofir sudand va mardumro az rohi Xudo ʙozdostand, ʙotil soxtaast
47|2|Xudo gunohi kasonero, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand va ʙa on ci ʙar Muhammad nozil suda, — ki on haq ast va az coniʙi Parvardigorason, — imon ovardaand, az onho dur kard va korhojasonro ʙa saloh ovard
47|3|Va in ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki kofiron ʙa ʙotil pajravi kardand va onon, ki imon ovardand, ʙa haqqe, ki az coniʙi Parvardigorason omada ʙud, pajravi kardaand. Xudo ʙaroi mardum incunin misol meorad
47|4|Cun ʙo kofiron ruʙaru suded, gardanasonro ʙizaned. Va cun onhoro saxt furu kufted, asirason kuned va saxt ʙiʙanded. On goh jo ʙa minnat ozod kumed jo ʙa fidja (ʙa ivazi pul). To on goh, ki cang ʙa pojon ojad. Va in ast hukmi Xudo. Va agar Xudo mexost, az onon intiqom megirift, vale xost to sumoro ʙa jakdigar ʙijozmojad. Va onon, ki dar rohi Xudo kusta sudaand, amalhojasonro ʙotil namekunad
47|5|Ba zudi, ki hidojatason kunad va korhojasonro ʙa saloh ovarad
47|6|Va ʙa ʙihiste, ki ʙarojason vasf kardaast, doxilason sozad
47|7|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, agar Xudoro jori kuned, sumoro jori xohad kard va pojdori xohad ʙaxsid
47|8|Halokatu surʙaxti ʙod ʙar kofiron. Xudo amalhojasonro ʙotil kardaast
47|9|Zero onon cizero, ki Xudo nozil kardaast, noxus dorand. Xudo niz amalhojasonro noʙud kard
47|10|Ojo dar zamin sajr nakardaand, to ʙingarand, ki oqiʙati kasone, ki pes az onho ʙudaand, ci guna ʙudaast? Xudo halokason kard va kofiron niz oqiʙate oncunon xohand dost
47|11|In ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki Xudo jovari 'kasonest, ki imon ovardaand. Va kofironro hec jovare nest
47|12|Xudo kasonero, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista mekunand, ʙa ʙihisthoe, ki nahrho az on porist, doxil xohad kard. Va kofiron az in cahon ʙahramand mesavand va cun corpojon mexurand va cojgohason otas ast
47|13|Ci qarijahoe (dehahoe), ki mardumas az mardumi qarijai tu, ki az on ʙerunat kardand, xele purquvvattar ʙudand, ki halokason kardem va hec jorikunandae nadostand
47|14|Ojo kase, ki az coniʙi Parvardigoras daleli ravsane dorad, monandi kasonest, ki kirdori ʙadason dar nazarason orosta suda va az pai havohoi xud meravand
47|15|Vasfi ʙihiste, ki ʙa parhezgoron va'da doda suda, in ast, ki dar on nahrhoest az oʙhoe taƣjirnopazir va nahrhoe az sire, ki ta'mas digargun namesavad va nahrhoe az saroʙ, ki osomandagon az on lazzat meʙarand va nahrhoe az asali musaffo. Va dar on co har guna meva, ki ʙixohand, hast va niz ʙaxsoisi Parvardigorason. Ojo ʙihistijon monandi kasone hastand, ki dar otasi covidonaand va ononro az oʙe cuson meosomanand, cunon ki rudahojason tika-tika mesavad
47|16|Ba'ze ʙa tu gus medihand, to on goh ki az nazdi tu ʙerun ravand, az donismandon mepursand: «In ci suxanone ʙud, ki meguft?» Xudo ʙar dilhojason muhr nihodaast va az pai havohoi xud raftaand
47|17|Onon, ki hidojat joftaand, Xudo ʙa hidojatason meafzojad va parhezgorijason ato mekunad
47|18|Ojo tanho muntaziri onand, ki ʙa nogoh qijomat faro rasad? Har oina (Alʙatta) nisonahoi qijomat oskor sudaast. Va cun faro rasad, pand giriftanasonro ci foida
47|19|Pas ʙidon, ki hec xudoe cuz Olloh nest. Az gunohi xud va az gunohi mardonu zanoni mu'min ʙaxsois ʙixoh. Xudo medonad, ki ruz ʙa kuco meraved va saʙ ʙa kuco meoromed
47|20|Kasone, ki imon ovardaand, megujand: «Caro az coniʙi Xudo surae nozil namesavad?» Cun surae az muhqamot nozil savad, ki dar oja suxan az cang rafta ʙosad, ononro, ki dar dilason maraze hast, ʙini, ki cun kase, ki ʙehusii marg ʙar u ƣoliʙ suda, ʙa tu menigarand. Pas ʙarojasoja soistatar
47|21|farmonʙardorist va suxani neku guftan. Va cun tasmim ʙa cang girifta sud, agar ʙo Xudo sadoqat kunand, ʙarojason ʙehtar ast
47|22|Ojo agar ʙa hukumat rasided, mexohed dar zamin fasod kuned va pajvandi xesovandijatonro ʙiʙured
47|23|Inhoand, ki Xudo la'natason kardaast va gushojasonro karu casmonasonro kur soxtaast
47|24|Ojo dar Qur'on nameandesand jo ʙar dilhojason quflhost
47|25|Sajton amalhoi kasonero, ki ʙa'd az oskor sudani rohi hidojat murtad sudand (az din gastand) va ʙozgastand, dar nazarason ʙijorost va orzujason daroz kard
47|26|Va in ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki ʙa on guruh, ki ojoti Xudoro noxus medostand, meguftand: «Mo dar ʙa'ze az korho farmonʙardori sumo hastem. Va Xudo az rozason ogoh ast
47|27|Ci gunaand, on goh ki faristagon onhoro memironand va ʙar ru va pusthojason mezanand
47|28|In ʙa cazoi on ast, ki ʙa on ci Xudoro ʙa xasm meovarad, pajravi mekardaand va ʙa on ci xusnudas mesoxta, ʙadʙini dostaand. Xudo niz amalhojasonro noʙud kard
47|29|Ojo onon, ki dar dilason marazest, mepindorand, ki Xudo kinaero, ki dar dil pinhon dorand, oskor naxohad kard
47|30|Agar ʙixohem, onhoro ʙa tu menamojonem va tu onhoro ʙa simojason 'jo az sevai suxanason xohi sinoxt va Xudo az amalhojaton ogoh ast
47|31|Va sumoro meozmoem, to mucohidon va soʙironatonro ma'lum dorem va xaʙarhojatonro oskor kunem
47|32|Kasone, ki imon najovardand va az rohi Xudo rujgardon sudand va ʙo on ki rohi hidojat ʙarojason oskor suda ʙud, ʙo pajomʙar muxolifat namudand, hec zijone ʙa Xudo naxohand rasonid va Xudo amalhojasonro noʙud xohad kard
47|33|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙa Xudo ito'at kuned va ʙa pajomʙar ito'at kuned va a'moli xudro ʙotil masozed
47|34|Xudo kasonero, ki kofir sudand va mardumro az rohi Xudo ʙozdostand va dar kufr murdand, hargiz naxohad ʙaxsond
47|35|Susti navarzed, to da'vat ʙa musoliha kuned. Sumo ʙartar hasted va Xudo ʙo sumost va az podoshojaton (mukofothojaton) naxohad kam kard
47|36|Zindagii incahoni faqat ʙozicavu ʙehudagist. Va agar imon ʙijovared va parhezgori kuned, Xudo mukofothojatonro xohad dod. Va az sumo molhojatonro nametalaʙad
47|37|Agar az sumo mole talaʙad va ʙardavom ham talaʙad, on goh ʙaxili mekuned va kinahoi pinhonatonro oskor mesozad
47|38|Ogoh ʙosed ki sumoro da'vat mekunand to dar rohi Xudo sadaqa kuned. Ba'ze az sumo ʙaxili mekunand, va har kas ki ʙaxili kunad, dar haqqi xud ʙaxili kardaast. Zero Xudo ʙehocat ast va sumo hocatmandoned. Va agar ruj ʙartoʙed, ʙa coi sumo mardume digar orad, ki hargiz misli sumo naʙosand
48|1|Mo ʙaroi tu piruzii namojonero hukm kardaem
48|2|To Xudo gunohi turo, on ci pes az in ʙuda va on ci pas az in ʙosad, ʙaroi tu ʙiʙaxsojad va ne'mati xudro ʙar tu komil kunad va turo ʙa rohi rost roh namojad
48|3|Va Xudo jorijat kunad, jori kardane piruzmandona
48|4|Ust, ki ʙar dilhoi mu'minon oromis firistod, to ʙar imonason pajvasta ʙijafzojad. Va az oni Xudost laskarhoi osmonhovu zamin va Xudo donovu hakim ast
48|5|Va to mardonu zanoni mu'minro ʙa ʙihisthoe doxil kunad, ki dar on nahrho corist va dar on co covidonand va gunohonasonro nest kunad. Va in dar nazdi Xudo komjoʙii ʙuzurgest
48|6|Va mardonu zanoni munofiq va mardonu zanoni musrikro, ki ʙar Xudo ʙadgumonand, 'azoʙ kunad. Bar onho ʙod musiʙati ʙad va Xudo ʙar onho xasm girift va la'natason kard va cahannamro ʙarojason omoda kardaast va cahannam cojgohi ʙadest
48|7|Az oni Xudost laskarhoi osmonhovu zamin va Xudo ƣoliʙu hakim ast
48|8|Turo guvohidihandavu muƶdadihanda va ʙimdihanda firistodaem
48|9|To ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon ʙijovared va jorijas kunedu ʙuzurgas dored va Xudoro suʙhgohu somgoh tasʙeh gued
48|10|Onon, ki ʙo tu ʙaj'at (ahd) mekunand, cuz in nest, ki ʙo Xudo ʙaj'at mekunand. Dasti Xudo ʙoloi dasthojason ast. Va har ki ʙaj'atro ʙiskanad, ʙa zijoni xud sikastaast. Va har ki ʙa on ʙaj'at, ki ʙo Xudo ʙastaast, vafo kunad, uro muzde neku dihad
48|11|Az a'roʙi ʙodijanisin onon, ki az cang qafokasi kardand, ʙa tu xohand guft: «Doroivu kasoni mo moro az cang ʙozdostand, pas ʙaroi mo ʙaxsois ʙixoh». Ba zaʙon cize megujad, ki dar dilason nest. Bigu: «Agar Xudo ʙarojaton zijone ʙixohad jo sude ʙixohad, ci kase metavonad dar ʙaroʙari Xudo onro digargun kunad?» Balki Ust, ki ʙa korhojaton ogoh ast
48|12|Jo mepindosted, ki pajomʙar va mu'minon hargiz nazdi kasonasen ʙoz naxohand gast va dil ʙa in xus karda ʙuded. Pindori ʙade dostaed va mardume sazovori halokat ʙudaed
48|13|Va har kas ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon najovardaast, ʙidonad, ki ʙaroi kofiron otase suzon omoda kardaem
48|14|Az oni Xudost farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin. Har kiro ʙixohad, meʙaxsad va har kiro ʙixohad, azoʙ mekunad va Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
48|15|Cun ʙaroi giriftani ƣanimatho ʙa roh ʙijafted, onon, ki az cang taxalluf (qafokasi) namudaand, xohand guft: «Bigzored, to mo ham az pai sumo ʙijoem! Mexohand suxani Xudoro digargun kunand. Bigu: '«Sumo hargiz az pai mo naxohed omad. Xudo az pes cunin guftaast». Sipas xohand guft: «Balki ʙar mo hasad meʙared?» Na, inho cuz andake namefahmand
48|16|Ba a'roʙi ʙodijanisin, ki az cang taxalluf namudaand, ʙigu: «Ba zudi ʙaroi cang ʙa mardume saxt nerumand da'vat karda mesaved, ki ʙo onho ʙicanged jo musalmon savand. Agar ito'at kuned, Xudojaton muzde neku xohad dod va agar, hamcunon ki pes az in sar ʙartoftaed, sar ʙartoʙed, sumoro ʙa azoʙe dardovar azoʙ mekunad»
48|17|Bar kur harace (gunohe) nest va ʙar lang xarace nest va ʙar ʙemor xarace nest. Va har ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras ito'at kunad, uro ʙa ʙihisthoe doxil mekunad, ki dar on nahrho ravon ast. Va har ki sar ʙartoʙad, ʙa azoʙe dardovaras azoʙ mekunad
48|18|Xudo az mu'minon, on hangom ki dar zeri daraxt ʙo tu ʙaj'at kardand, xusnud gast va donist, ki dar dilason ci meguzarad. Pas oromis ʙar onho nozil kard va ʙa fathe (ƣalaʙae) nazdik mukofotason dod
48|19|va ʙa ƣanimathoi ʙisjor, ki ʙa dast meovarand. Va Xudo ƣoliʙu hakim ast
48|20|Xudo ʙa sumo va'dai ƣanimathoi ʙisjor dodaast, ki ʙa dast meovared va in ƣanimatro zudtar ato kard va sumoro az oseʙi mardumon amon ʙaxsid, to ʙaroi mu'minon iʙrate ʙosad va ʙa rohi rost hidojatason kunad
48|21|Va ƣanimathoi digare, ki hanuz ʙa onho dast najoftaed. Har oina (Alʙatta) Xudo ʙa on (ʙo ilmas) ihota dorad va U ʙa har kore tavonost
48|22|Va agar kofiron ʙo sumo ʙa cang ʙarxezand, pust gardonda ʙigrezand va digar hec dustu jorigare namejoʙand
48|23|In sunnati Xudost, ki az pes cunin ʙudaast va tu dar sunnati Xudo digarguni 'naxohi joft
48|24|Ust, ki cun dar ʙatni (moʙajni) Makka ʙar onho ƣoliʙijataton dod, dasti onhoro az sumo va dasti sumoro az onho ʙozdost. Va Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekarded, ogohu ʙino ʙud
48|25|Inho hamonhojand, ki kofir sudand va sumoro az mascidulharom ʙozdostand va naguzostand, ki qurʙoni ʙa qurʙongohas ʙirasad. Agar mardoni musalmonu zanoni musalmone, ki onhoro namesinosed, dar mijoni onho naʙudand va ʙimi on naʙud, ki onhoro zeri poj kuned va nodonista gunoh sodir kuned, Xudo dasti sumoro az onho ʙoznamedost. Va Xudo har kiro ʙixohad, somili rahmati Xud gardonad. Agar az jakdigar cudo meʙudand, kofironasonro ʙa azoʙe dardovar azoʙ mekardem
48|26|On goh ki kofiron tasmim giriftand, dar dili xud ta'assuʙro, ta'assuʙi cohili, Xudo niz oromisi Xudro ʙar dili pajomʙaras va mu'minon furud ovard va ʙa taqvo lozimason kard, ki inho ʙa taqvo sazovortaru soistatar ʙudand va Xudo ʙar har cize donost
48|27|Xudo xoʙi pajomʙarasro rost ʙarovard, ki gufta ʙud: «Agar Xudo ʙixohad, emin guruhe sartarosida va guruhe muj kutoh karda ʙe hec tars ʙa mascidulharom doxil mesaved. U cizhoe medonist, ki sumo namedonisted. Va cuz on dar hamin nazdiki fathe nasiʙi sumo karda ʙud
48|28|Ust, ki pajomʙarasro ʙa hidojat va dini haq firistod, to on dinro ʙar hamai dinho ƣoliʙ gardonad. Va Xudo ʙaroi sohidi didan kofist
48|29|Muhammad — pajomʙari Xudo va kasone, ki ʙo u hastand, ʙar kofiron saxtgirand va ʙo jakdigar mehruʙon. Ononro ʙini, ki ruqu' mekunand, ʙa sacda meojand va talaʙkunandai fazlu xusnudii Xudo hastand. Nisonason asari sacdaest, ki ʙar cehrai onhost. In ast vasfason dar Tavrot va dar Incil, misli ziroate hastand, ki gijoh ʙarorad va on cavona mahkam savad va ʙar pohoi xud ʙiistad va dehqononro ʙa hajrat vodorad, to on co ki kofironro ʙa xasm ovarad. Xudo az mijoni onho kasonero, ki imon ovardaand, va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙaxsois va mukofote ʙuzurg va'da dodaast
49|1|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙar Xudovu pajomʙari U pesdasti makuned va az Xudo ʙitarsed, zero Xudo sunavovu donost
49|2|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, sadoi xudro az sadoi pajomʙar ʙalandtar nakuned va hamcunon, ki ʙo jakdigar ʙaland suxan megued, ʙo u ʙa ovozi ʙaland suxan nagued, ki amalhojaton nociz savad va sumo ogoh nasaved
49|3|Kasone, ki dar nazdi pajomʙari Xudo sadojasonro poin meovarand, hamonhojand, ki Xudo dilhojasonro ʙa takvo ozmuda ast. Onhoro ʙaxsoisu muzdi ʙisjor ast
49|4|Onhoe, ki az on sui hucraho turo nido medihand, ʙestar ʙexiradonand
49|5|Agar saʙr, mekardand, to tu xud ʙerun meomadi va nazdi onho merafti, ʙarojason ʙehtar meʙud va Xudo ʙaxsojandai mehruʙon ast
49|6|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, agar fosiqe ʙarojaton xaʙare ovard, tahqiq kuned, maʙod az rui nodoni ʙa mardume oseʙ (ranc) ʙirasoned, on goh, az kore, ki kardaed, pusajmon saved
49|7|Va ʙidoned, ki pajomʙari Xudo dar mijoni sumost. Agar dar ʙisjore az korho az sumo farmon ʙiʙarad, ʙa ranc meafted. Vale Xudo imonro mahʙuʙi sumo soxt va onro dar dilaton ʙiorost va kufru fisqu nofarmoniro dar nazaraton ʙad gardonid. Inho xud rohjoftagonand
49|8|Baxsisu ne'matest az coniʙi Xudo va Xudo donovu hakim ast
49|9|Va agar du guruh az mu'minon ʙo jakdigar ʙa cang ʙarxostand, mijonason osti andozed. Va agar jak guruh ʙar digare dast darozi kard, ʙo on ki dast darozi kardaast, ʙicanged, to ʙa farmoni Xudo ʙozgardad. Pas agar ʙozgast, mijonason sulhe odilona ʙarqaror kuned va adolat kuned, ki Xudo odilonro dust dorad
49|10|Har oina (Alʙatta) mu'minon ʙarodaronand. Mijoni ʙarodaronaton osti andozed va az Xudo ʙitarsed, sojad, ki ʙar sumo rahmat orad
49|11|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, maʙod, ki guruhe az mardon guruhi digarro masxara kunad, sojad on masxarasudagon ʙehtar az onho ʙosand. Va maʙod, ki guruhe az zanon guruhi digarro masxara kunad, sojad on masxarasudagon ʙehtar az onho ʙosand. Va az ham ajʙcuj makuned va jakdigarro ʙa laqaʙhoi zist maxoned. Bad ast unvoni fisq pas az imon ovardan. Va kasone, ki tavʙa namekunand, xud sitamkoronand
49|12|Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, az ʙisjore az gumonho ʙiparhezed. Zero ʙa'ze az gumonho dar haddi gunoh ast. Va dar korhoi pinhonii jakdigar cosusi makuned. Va az jakdigar ƣajʙat makuned. Ojo hec jak az sumo dust dorad, ki gusti ʙarodari murdai xudro ʙixurad? Pas onro noxus xohed dost. Va az Xudo ʙitarsed, zero Xudo tavʙapaziru mehruʙon ast
49|13|Ej mardum, mo sumoro az jak mardu jak zan ʙijofaridem. Va sumoro camo'atho va qaʙilaho kardem, to jakdigarro ʙisinosed. Alʙatta giromitarini sumo nazdi Xudo parhezgortarini sumost. Xudo donovu kordon ast
49|14|A'roʙi ʙodijanisin guftand: «Imon ovardem!» Bigu: «Imon najova. rdaed. Bigued, ki taslim sudaem va hanuz imon dar dilhojaton doxil nasudaast. Va agar Xudovu pajomʙarasro ito'at kuned, az savoʙi amalhoi sumo kam karda namesavad, zero Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast»
49|15|Muʹminon kasone hastand, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙari U imon ovardaand va digar sak nakardaand va ʙo molu coni xud dar rohi Xudo cihod kardaand. Inho rostgujonand
49|16|Bigu: «Ojo mexohed Xudoro az dindorii xud ogoh kuned? Hol on ki Xudo az har ci dar osmonhovu har ci dar zamin ast, ogoh ast va U ʙa har cize olim ast!»
49|17|Az in ki islom ovardaand, ʙar tu minnat mekunand. Bigu: «Ba xotiri islomaton ʙar man minnat mekuned, ʙalki Xudo ʙa on saʙaʙ, ki sumoro ʙa imon roh namudaast, ʙar sumo minnat menihad, agar rost megued!»
49|18|Alʙatta Xudo nihoni osmonhovu zaminro medonad va ʙa har kore, ki mekuned, ʙinost
50|1|Qof. Qasam ʙa in Qur'oni arcmand
50|2|Ki dar taaccuʙ sudand, az in ki az mijoni xudason ʙimdihandae sujason omad, va kofiron guftand: «In cize aciʙ ast
50|3|Ojo zamone, ki murdemu xok sudem, digar ʙor zinda mesavem? In ʙozgaste muxol (nomumkin) ast!»
50|4|Mo medonem, ki xok ci guna az (casadhoi) onho kam mekunad. Va kitoʙe, ki hama ciz dar on nigahdori suda, nazdi Most
50|5|Ore, onho suxani rostero, ki ʙar onho omada ʙud, duruƣ sumurdand. Pas dar kore surida aftodand
50|6|Ojo ʙa in osmon ʙar ʙoloi sarason nazar namekunasd, ki ci guna onro ʙino kardaem va orostaem va hec sikofe dar on nest
50|7|Va zaminro gusturdem va dar on kuhhoi ʙaland afkandem va az har guna naʙototi xusmanzar dar on rujonidem
50|8|Binise va pandest ʙaroi har ʙandae, ki ʙa Xudo ʙozgardad
50|9|Va az osmoi oʙe purʙarakat firistodem va ʙo on ʙoƣhovu donahoi daravsudani rujonidem
50|10|va naxlhoi ʙaland ʙo xusahoi ʙarham cida
50|11|to rizqi ʙaidagon ʙosad va ʙo on oʙ sarzamini murdaro zinda kardem. Baromadan az gur niz cunin ast
50|12|Pes az onho qavmi Nuh va ashoʙi Ras va Samud takziʙ karda (duruƣ ʙarovarda) ʙudand
50|13|va qavmi Odu Fir'avn va qavmi Lut
50|14|va ashoʙi Ajka va qavmi Tuʙʙa' hama pajomʙaronro duruƣ sumurdand va sazovori va'dai azoʙi Man sudand
50|15|Ojo az ofarinisi naxustin ociz suda ʙudem? Na onho dar ofarinisi toza dar sakkand
50|16|Mo odamiro ofaridaem va az vasvasahoi nafsi u ogoh hastem, zero az ragi gardanas ʙa u nazdiktarem
50|17|Hangome ki on du faristai farogiranda dar coniʙi rostu coniʙi capi u nisastaand, har cizro faro megirand
50|18|Har kalome ki megujad, alʙatta dar kanori u noziru navisandae hozir ast
50|19|Ba rosti, ki ʙehusii marg faro merasad. In ast on ci az on megurexti
50|20|Va dar sur damida mesavad, In ast, ruzi va'dahoi azoʙ
50|21|Har kase meojad va ʙo u kasest, ki meronadas va kasest, ki ʙarojas sohidi medihad
50|22|Tu az in ƣofil ʙudi. Mo parda az ʙaroʙarat ʙardostem va imruz casmonat tezʙin sudaast
50|23|Faristai (muvakkali) u gujad: «In ast on ci man omoda kardaam»
50|24|Har nosukri sarkasro ʙa cahannam ʙijandozed
50|25|on ki az ʙaxsis ʙaxili kard va tacovuzkor ʙud va sak meovard
50|26|on ki ʙo Xudoi jak to xudoi digare qaror dod. Pas ʙa azoʙi saxtas ʙipartoed
50|27|Hamnisini u gujad: «Ej Parvardigori mo, man uro ʙa sarkasi vodor nakardam, ʙalki u xud, saxt dar gumrohi ʙud»
50|28|Megujad: «Nazdi Man mucodala nakuned. Man pes az in ʙo sumo suxan az azoʙ gufta ʙudam
50|29|Va'dai Man digargun namesavad va Man ʙa ʙandagon zulm namekunam»
50|30|Ruze, ki cahannamro meguem: «Ojo pur sudai?» Megujad: «Ojo hec zijodati hast?»
50|31|Va ʙihistro ʙaroi parhezgoron nazdik ʙijovarand, to az on dur naʙosand
50|32|In hamon cizest, ki ʙa har tavʙakunasdai parhezgore va'daas doda ʙudand
50|33|Onhoero, ki dar nihon az Xudoi rahmon metarsand va ʙo dile tavʙakor omadaand
50|34|Gujand: «Dar amon az har azoʙe ʙa ʙihist doxil saved. In ruz ruzi covidonist»
50|35|Dar on co har ci ʙixohand, hast va ʙestar az on nazdi Mo hast
50|36|Pes az onho ci ʙisjor mardumero, ki ʙoquvvattar ʙudand va dar sahrho sajru custucu mekardand, ʙa halokat ovardaem. Ojo rohi gureze hast
50|37|Dar in suxan ʙaroi sohiʙdilon jo onon, ki ʙo huzur gus meandozand, andarzest (pandest)
50|38|Mo osmonhovu zamin, va on ciro mijoni onhost, dar sas ruz ofaridem va hec xastagi ʙa Mo narasid
50|39|Dar ʙaroʙari on ci megujand, pojdori kun va dar sitoisi Parvardigorat pes az ʙaromadani oftoʙ va pes az faromadani on tasʙeh guj
50|40|Va niz dar porae az saʙ va ʙa'd az har sacda uro tasʙeh guj
50|41|Va on goh ki munodi (nidokunanda, Isrofil) az makone nazdik nido medihad, gus faro dor
50|42|Ruze, ki on ovozi saxtro ʙa haq mesunavand, on ruz ruzi ʙerun sudan az gur ast
50|43|Mo zinda mekunem va memironem va ʙozgast nazdi Most
50|44|Ruze, ki zamin ʙiskofad va onho ʙa sitoʙ ʙerun ojand va in cam'ovari ʙaroi Mo oson ast
50|45|Mo ʙa on ci megujand, donotarem va tu ʙa onho zur namegui. Pas har kiro az va'dai azoʙi Man metarsad, ʙa Qur'on pand deh
51|1|Savgand ʙa ʙodhoe, ki xok parokanda mekunand
51|2|savgand, ʙa aʙrhoi garonʙor
51|3|savgand ʙa kistihoe, ki ʙa osoni ravonand
51|4|va savgand ʙa faristagone, ki taqsimkunandai korhojand
51|5|ki on ci sumoro va'da medihand, rost ast
51|6|va ruzi cazo omadanist
51|7|Va savgand ʙa osmon, ki ʙa sitoragon orosta ast
51|8|ki sumo (dar xususi pajƣamʙar) suxani gunogun megued
51|9|Az haq ʙozgardonida savad, on ki ʙozgardonidanasro xostaand
51|10|Marg ʙod ʙar on duruƣgujon
51|11|onon ki ʙa ƣaflat dar cahl furu raftaand
51|12|Mepursand: «Ruzi cazo kaj xohad ʙud?»
51|13|Ruzest, ki ʙar otas azoʙason mekunand
51|14|«Azoʙi xudro ʙicased! In ast on cize, ki ʙa sitoʙ metalaʙided!»
51|15|Parhezgoron dar ʙoƣhovu kanori casmasoron ʙosand
51|16|On ciro Xudo ʙa onho dodaast, giriftaand. Zero pes az on nekukor ʙudand
51|17|andake az saʙro mexoʙidand
51|18|va ʙa hangomi sahar istiƣfor (tavʙa) mekardand
51|19|va dar molhojason ʙaroi pursandavu mahrum xaqqe ʙud
51|20|Va dar zamin ʙaroi axli jaqin iʙrathoest
51|21|va niz dar vucudi xudaton. Ojo nameʙined
51|22|Va rizqi sumo va har ci ʙa sumo va'da suda, dar osmon ast
51|23|Pas savgand ʙa Parvardigori osmonahovu zamin, ki in suxan oncunon ki suxan megujand, haq va rost ast
51|24|Ojo dostoni mehmononi giromii Iʙrohim ʙa tu rasidaast
51|25|On goh ki nazdi u omadandu guftand: «Salom!» Guft: «Salom! Sumo mardumi nosinoxtaed!»
51|26|Dar nihon va sitoʙon nazdi kasoni xud raft va gusolai farʙehe ovard
51|27|Ta'omro ʙa nazdason guzostu guft: «Caro namexured?»
51|28|Va az onho ʙimnok sud. Guftand: «Matars!» Va uro ʙa farzande dono xusxaʙar dodand
51|29|Va zanas farjodzanon omad va ʙar ruj zadu guft: Man pirazane nozojam»
51|30|Guftand: «Parvardigori tu incunin guftaast. Va u hakimu donost!»
51|31|Guft: «Ej rasulon, ʙa ci kor omadaed?»
51|32|Guftand: «Moro ʙar mardume taʙahkor firistodaand
51|33|to tikkahoi sanghoi gili ʙar sarason ʙiʙorem
51|34|ki ʙar on sangho az coniʙi Parvardigorat ʙaroi az had, guzastaho nison guzostaand»
51|35|Pas hamai kasonero, ki imon ovarda ʙudand, ʙerun ʙurdem
51|36|Va dar on sahr ƣajri jak xona va farmonʙardoron najoftem
51|37|Va dar on sarzamin ʙaroi kasone, ki az azoʙi dardovar metarsand, nisone ʙoqi guzostem
51|38|Va iʙratest dar Muso, on goh ki uro ʙo huccate oskor nazdi Fir'avn firistodem
51|39|Va U ʙo hamai quvvaas ruj gardondu guft: «Codugarest jo devonae!»
51|40|U va laskarhojasro giriftem va ʙa darjo partoftem. Va u mustavciʙi (sazovori) malomat ʙud
51|41|Va niz iʙratest dar qavmi Od, on goh, ki ʙodi aqimro ʙar onho firistodem
51|42|Bar har cize vazid, faqat ustuxone pusidaas ʙar coj guzost
51|43|Va niz iʙratest dar qavmi Samud, on goh ki ʙa onho gufta sud: «To zamone cand ʙarxurdor saved»
51|44|Onon az farmoni Parvardigorason sar ʙozzadand va hamcunon ki menigaristand, ra'di tunde furu giriftason
51|45|Istodan natavonistand va tavoni intiqom nadostand
51|46|Va az pes qavmi Nuhro halok kardem, ki qavme nofarmon ʙudand
51|47|Va osmonro ʙa quvvat ʙarafrostem va haqqo, ki Mo tavonoem
51|48|Va zaminro gusturdem va ci neku gustarandagonem
51|49|Va az har ciz cufte ʙijofaridaem, sojad, ki iʙrat gired
51|50|Pas ʙa sui Xudovand ʙigrezed. Man sumoro az coniʙi U ʙimdihandae oskoram
51|51|Va ʙo Xudoi jakto xudoi digaroro maparasted. Man sumoro az coniʙi U ʙimdihandae oskoram
51|52|Hamcunin ʙar onhoe, ki az in pes ʙudand, har pajomʙare, ki firistoda sud, guftand: «Codugarest jo devonaest!»
51|53|Ojo ʙa in kor jakdigarro vasijat karda ʙudand? Na, xud mardume toƣi (sarkas) ʙudand
51|54|Pas az onho rujgardon sav. Kas turo malomat naxohad kard
51|55|Andarz (pand) ʙideh, ki andarz mu'minonro manfiat dorad
51|56|Cinnu insro faqat va faqat ʙaroi parastisi Xud ofaridaam
51|57|Az onho rizqe namexoham va namexoham, ki maro it'om kunand (xuronand)
51|58|Xudost ruzidihanda. Va Ust sohiʙi quvvate saxt ustuvor
51|59|In sitamkoronro az azoʙ ʙahraest monandi ʙahrae, ki joronason dostand. Pas ʙa sitoʙ cize (azoʙ) az Man naxohand
51|60|Voj ʙar kofiron, az on ruz, ki onhoro va'da dodaand
52|1|Qasam ʙa kuhi Tur
52|2|va qasam ʙa kitoʙi navistasuda
52|3|dar safhae kusoda (Qur'on)

52|17|Parhezgoron dar ʙihistho va ne'matand

52|19|Ba muzdi korhoe, ki kardaed, ʙixuredu ʙijosomed. Guvorojaton ʙod
52|20|Bar on taxthoi kanori ham cida takja mezanand. Hurijonro hamsarason megardonem
52|21|Kasone, ki xud imon ovardand va farzandonason dar imon pajravijason kardand. Farzandonasonro ʙo onho jakcoja mekunem va az muzdi amalason hec kam namekunem, ki dar kase dar garavi kori xud ast
52|22|Va pajvasta az har guna, ki ʙixohand, mevavu gust atojason mekunem
52|23|Dar on co comi maj dihand va comi maj sitonand, ki dar on na suxani ʙehuda ʙosad va na gunoh kardan
52|24|Ƣulomonason cun marvoridi pinhon dar sadaf ʙa girdason mecarxand
52|25|Pursiskunon ruj ʙa jakdigar mekunand

52|27|Pas Xudo ʙar mo minnat nihod va moro az azoʙi samum nigah dost
52|28|Mo pes az in Uro (ʙo du'ovu iltico) mexondem, ki U ehsonkunandavu mehruʙon ast!»
52|29|Pandason deh, ki tu ʙa ʙarakati ne'mati Parvardigorat na kohin (codugar) hastivu na macnun
52|30|Jo megujand: «Soirestu mo ʙaroi vaj muntaziri havodisi ruzgorem». (ki sojad ʙimirad)
52|31|Bigu: «Sumo muntazir ʙimoned, ki man niz ʙo sumo intizor mekasam»
52|32|Ojo ononro ru'johojason (xoʙhojason) ʙa in pindorho kasonida jo xud, mardume sarkas hastand
52|33|Jo megujand: «Qur'onro xud soxtaast!» Na, onho imon nameovarand
52|34|Agar rost megujand, suxane monandi on ʙijovarand
52|35|Ojo ʙe hec xoliqe ofarida sudand, jo xud xoliqi xudand
52|36|Jo osmonhovu zaminro hal kardaand? Na, ʙa jaqin narasidaand
52|37|Jo xazinahoi Parvardigorat nazdi onhost? Jo ʙar cize tasallut joftaand? (hukumat joftaand)
52|38|Jo nardʙone dorand, ki az on ʙolo meravand va gus meandozand? Pas on kase, ki gus andoxta ʙosad, huccate oskor ʙijovarad
52|39|Jo xudovandro duxtaron astu sumoro pisaron
52|40|Jo az onho muzde metalaʙi va pardoxti muzd ʙar onho dusvor ast
52|41|Jo ilmi ƣajʙ medonandu menavisand

52|43|jo onhoro xudoest ƣajri Xudoi jakto? Pok ast Xudoi jakto az har ci sarikas mesozand
52|44|Agar ʙingarand, ki qit'ae az osmon furu meaftad, megujand: «Aʙrest mutarokim (qaʙat-qaʙat cam'suda)»
52|45|Pas onhoro voguzor, to ruzero, ki dar oja ʙa halokat merasand, ʙingarand
52|46|ruze, ki makrason hec ʙa holason foidae nakunad va kas ʙa jorijason ʙarnaxezad
52|47|Baroi kasone, ki zulm mekunand, ʙoz ham azoʙest ƣajri in azoʙ, vale ʙestarinason namedonand
52|48|Dar ʙaroʙari farmoni Parvardigorat ʙosaʙr ʙos, ki tu tahti nazari Moi! Va hangome ki ʙarxosti, ʙa sitoisi Parvardigorat tasʙeh guj
52|49|Va tasʙh guj dar qisme az saʙ va ʙa hangomi nopadid sudani sitoragon
53|1|Qasam ʙa on sitora, cun pinhon sud

53|24|Ojo harci odami orzu kunad, ʙarojas hosil ast
53|25|Ham oxirat va ham dunjo az oni Xudost
53|26|Va ci ʙisjor faristagon dar osmonand, ki safo'atason hec naf' nadihad, lekin az on pas, ki Xudo ʙaroi har ki xohad, ruxsat dihad va xusnud ʙosad. (naf' kunad)
53|27|Onon, ki ʙa oxirat imon nadorand, faristagonro ʙa nomhoi zanon menomand
53|28|Inhoro ʙa on ci megujand, hec donise nest. Tanho az gumoni xud pajravi mekunand va gumon ʙaroi sinoxti haqiqat kofi nest
53|29|Pas tu niz az kase, ki az suxani Mo rujgardon mesavad va ƣajri zindagii dunjaviro namecujad, ruj gardon
53|30|Nihojati donisason hamin ast. Parvardigori tu ʙa on kase ki az rohi U gumroh mesavad jo ʙa rohi hidojat meaftad, donotar ast
53|31|Az oni Xudost har ci dar osmonhovu har ci dar zamin ast, to ʙadkoronro dar ʙaroʙari korhojason cazo dihad va nekukoronro ʙa kirdori nekason mukofot dihad
53|32|Kasone, ki az gunohoni ʙuzurgu zistiho parhez mekunand, — ƣajri on ki gunohe kucak az onho sar zanad, — ʙidonand, ki ʙaxsoisi Parvardigori tu vase' ast va U ʙa sumo on goh ki az zamin ʙijofaridaton va on goh ki dar sikami modaraton pinhon ʙuded, ogohtar ast. Xudatonro ʙegunoh nadoned. Ust, ki parhezgorro ʙehtar mesinosad
53|33|Ojo onro, ki az tu rujgardoi sud, didi

53|53|va niz Mu'tafikaro noʙud kard

54|1|Qijomat nazdik sud va moh dupora gardid
54|2|Va agar mu'cizae ʙuʙinand, ruj ʙigardodand va gujand: «"Codue ʙuzurg ast!»
54|3|Va duruƣ mepindorand va az pai havohoi xud meravand. Va har kore dar vaqti xud qaror giriftaast
54|4|Va ʙarojason xaʙarhoe omadaast, ki dar onho pandast
54|5|Hikmatest tamom. Vale ʙimdihandagon sudason nadihand

54|8|Sarhoro ʙolo girifta ʙa sui on da'vatkunanda mesitoʙad. Kofiron megujand: «In ruzi dusvorest!»

54|10|Va Parvardigorasro du'o kard: «Man maƣluʙ sudaam, intiqom ʙigir!»
